<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p159">管理员可以在 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中使用 **Export-SPOUserInfo** cmdlet 导出用户或给定网站的所有用户信息属性。请参阅 [Export-SPOUserInfo](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/export-spouserinfo)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p159">An admin can export all User information properties for a user on a given site by using the **Export-SPOUserInfo** cmdlet in SharePoint Online PowerShell. See [Export-SPOUserInfo](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/export-spouserinfo).</span></span>

##### <a name="onedrive-for-business-experience-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-421">OneDrive for Business 体验设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-421">OneDrive for Business experience settings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p160">用户的 OneDrive for Business 体验中存储的信息有助于用户查找和导航相关内容。最终用户可使用产品内功能访问大部分此类信息。管理员可以使用 [PowerShell 脚本](/powershell/scripting/overview)和 [SharePoint 客户端对象模型 (CSOM)](/sharepoint/dev/sp-add-ins/complete-basic-operations-using-sharepoint-client-library-code) 命令来导出信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p160">A user's OneDrive for Business experience stores information to help the user find and navigate content of interest to them. Most of this information can be accessed by end users using in-product features. An admin can export the information using a [PowerShell Script](/powershell/scripting/overview) and [SharePoint Client-Side Object Model (CSOM)](/sharepoint/dev/sp-add-ins/complete-basic-operations-using-sharepoint-client-library-code) commands.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-425">有关设置、存储方式和如何将其导出的详细信息，请参阅[导出 OneDrive for Business 体验设置](/sharepoint/export-odfb-lists)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-425">See [Export OneDrive for Business experience settings](/sharepoint/export-odfb-lists) for more information about the settings, how they are stored, and how to export them.</span></span>

##### <a name="onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-426">OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-426">OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online search</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p161">OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 中的应用内搜索体验存储用户的搜索查询（为期 30 天）以增加搜索结果的相关性。管理员可以使用 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中的 **Export-SPOQueryLogs** cmdlet 来导出用户的搜索查询。请参阅 [Export-SPOQueryLogs](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/export-spoquerylogs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p161">The in-app search experience in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online stores a user's search queries for 30 days to increase relevance of search results. An admin can export search queries for a user by using the **Export-SPOQueryLogs** cmdlet in SharePoint Online PowerShell. See [Export-SPOQueryLogs](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/export-spoquerylogs).</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-teams-for-education"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-430">Microsoft Teams 教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-430">Microsoft Teams for Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p162">Microsoft Teams 教育版提供了两个附加协作功能，教师和学生可以使用该功能创建和存储个人数据：作业和 OneNote 课堂笔记本。可使用内容搜索同时发现这两者之中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p162">Microsoft Teams for Education offers two additional collaboration features that teachers and students can use that creates and stores personal data: Assignments and OneNote Class Notebook. You can use Content Search to discover data in both.</span></span>

##### <a name="assignments"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-433">作业</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-433">Assignments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p163">与作业关联的学生文件存储在对应 Teams SharePoint Online 网站的文档库中。IT 管理员可使用内容搜索工具搜索与作业相关的学生文件。例如，管理员可搜索组织中的所有 SharePoint Online 网站，并在搜索查询中使用学生姓名和课堂或作业名称，以查找与 DSR 相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p163">Students files associated with an Assignment are stored in a document library in the corresponding Teams SharePoint Online site. IT admins can use the Content Search tool to search for student files that are related to assignments. For example, an admin could search all SharePoint Online sites in the organization and use the student's name and class or assignment name in the search query to find data relevant to a DSR.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p164">还有一些与作业相关的其他数据存储在课堂团队 SharePoint Online 网站中，这意味着该信息无法使用内容搜索发现。这些信息包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p164">There's other data related to Assignments that isn't stored in the class team SharePoint Online site, which means it's not discoverable with Content Search. This includes:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-439">教师在作业中分配给学生的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-439">Files that the teacher assigns to students as part of the assignment</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-440">学生成绩和教师反馈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-440">Student grades and feedback from the teacher</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-441">每个学生为作业提交的文档列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-441">The list of documents submitted for an assignment by each student</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-442">作业元数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-442">Assignment metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-443">对于这种类型的数据，IT 管理员或数据所有者（如教师）可能必须进入课堂团队中的作业才可查找与 DSR 相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-443">For this type if data, an IT admin or data owner (such as a teacher) may have to go into the Assignment in the class team to find data relevant to a DSR.</span></span>

##### <a name="onenote-class-notebook"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-444">OneNote 课堂笔记本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-444">OneNote Class Notebook</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p165">OneNote 课堂笔记本存储在课堂团队 SharePoint Online 网站中。课堂中的每个学生都有一个与教师共享的私人笔记本。还有一个可供教师在其中与学生共享文档的内容库，和一个为课堂中所有学生提供的协作空间。可使用内容搜索发现与这些功能相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p165">The OneNote Class Notebook is stored in the class team SharePoint Online site. Every student in a class has a private notebook that's shared with the teacher. There's also a content library where a teacher can share documents with students, and a collaboration space for all students in the class. Data related to these capabilities is discoverable with Content Search.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-449">下面介绍了搜索课堂笔记本的具体指南。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-449">Here's specific guidance to search for a Class Notebook.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-450">使用以下搜索条件运行内容搜索：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-450">Run a Content Search using the following search criteria:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-451">搜索所有 SharePoint Online 网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-451">Search all SharePoint Online sites</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-452">将课堂团队的名称包含在搜索关键字内；例如，“9C Biology”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-452">Include the name of the class team as a search keyword; for example, "9C Biology."</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-453">预览搜索结果，并查看对应于课堂笔记本的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-453">Preview the search results and look for the item that corresponds to the Class Notebook.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p166">选择该项，然后复制详细信息窗格中显示的文件夹路径。这是课堂笔记本的根文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p166">Select that item, and then copy the folder path that's displayed in the details pane. This is the root folder for the Class Notebook.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p167">编辑在步骤 1 中创建的搜索，将关键字查询中的课堂名称替换为课堂笔记本的文件夹路径，并在文件夹路径之前追加 **path** 网站属性，例如，**path:"<https://contosoedu.onmicrosoft.com/sites/9C> Biology/SiteAssets/9C Biology Notebook/"**。请务必包括引号和末尾斜杠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p167">Edit the search that you created in step 1 and replace the class name in the keyword query with the folder path of the Class Notebook and precede the folder path with the **path** site property; for example, **path:"<https://contosoedu.onmicrosoft.com/sites/9C> Biology/SiteAssets/9C Biology Notebook/"**. Be sure to include the quotation marks and the trailing forward slash.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-458">添加搜索条件，选择文件类型条件，使用 one 作为文件类型的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-458">Add a search condition and select the File Type condition and use one for the value of the file type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-459">这将在搜索结果中返回所有 OneNote 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-459">This returns all OneNote files in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-460">最终的关键字语法如[下](#building-search-queries-to-find-personal-data)所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-460">The resulting keyword syntax would look something like [this](#building-search-queries-to-find-personal-data):</span></span>

   ```Query
   path:"<https://contosoedu.onmicrosoft.com/sites/9C> Biology/SiteAssets/9C Biology Notebook/" AND filetype="one"
   ```

6. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-461">重新运行内容搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-461">Rerun the Content Search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-462">搜索结果应包括班级团队中 Class Notebook 的所有 OneNote 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-462">The search results should include all OneNote files for the Class Notebook from the class team.</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-to-do"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-463">微软待办</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-463">Microsoft To Do</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-464">微软待办中的任务（称为 *待办事项*，保存在 *待办事项列表* 中）在用户的 Exchange Online 邮箱中保存为“任务”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-464">Tasks (called *to-dos*, which are saved in *to-do lists*) in Microsoft To Do are saved as tasks in a user's Exchange Online mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-465">这意味着你可以使用“内容搜索”工具来搜索、访问、删除和导出待办事项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-465">That means that you can use the Content Search tool to search, access, delete, and export to-dos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-466">有关详细信息，请参阅[设置微软待办](https://support.microsoft.com/office/set-up-microsoft-to-do-490c1a8c-2333-4952-8125-841afadb9620)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-466">For more information, see [Set up Microsoft To Do](https://support.microsoft.com/office/set-up-microsoft-to-do-490c1a8c-2333-4952-8125-841afadb9620).</span></span>

#### <a name="skype-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-467">Skype for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-467">Skype for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-468">下面提供了有关如何访问、查看和导出 Skype for Business 中的个人数据的一些其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-468">Here some additional information about how to access, view, and export personal data in Skype for Business.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p171">附加到会议的文件在实际会议中保留 180 天，之后将无法访问。要访问这些文件，会议参与者可从会议请求加入会议，然后查看或下载附件。请参阅[为 Skype for Business 会议预加载附件](https://support.microsoft.com/office/preload-attachments-for-a-skype-for-business-meeting-fd3d9f9d-b448-4754-b813-02e49393f251)中的“使用会议中的附件”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p171">Files attached to a meeting are retained in the actual meeting for 180 days and then become inaccessible. These files can be accessed by meeting participants by joining the meeting from the meeting request and then viewing or downloading the attached file. See the "Use the attachments in the meeting" section in [Preload attachments for a Skype for Business meeting](https://support.microsoft.com/office/preload-attachments-for-a-skype-for-business-meeting-fd3d9f9d-b448-4754-b813-02e49393f251).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p172">Skype for Business 中的对话保留在用户邮箱的对话历史记录文件夹中。可使用内容搜索在邮箱中搜索 Skype 对话中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p172">Conversations in Skype for Business are retained in the Conversation History folder in user mailboxes. You can use Content Search to search mailboxes for data in Skype conversations.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-474">数据主体可在 Skype for Business 中导出其联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-474">A data subject can export their contacts in Skype for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-475">若要执行此操作，可在 Skype for Business 中右键选择一个联系人组，然后选择“**复制**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-475">To do this, they would right-select a contact group in Skype for Business and select **Copy**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-476">然后，可将电子邮件地址列表粘贴到文本或 Word 文档中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-476">Then they can paste the list of email addresses into a text or Word document.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p174">如果会议参与者的 Exchange Online 邮箱处于诉讼保留状态或已分配给 Office 365 保留策略，则附加到会议的文件保留在参与者邮箱中。如果文件的保留期尚未到期，可使用内容搜索在参与者邮箱中搜索这些文件。有关保留文件的详细信息，请参阅[保留附加到 Skype for Business 会议的大型文件](/skypeforbusiness/set-up-policies-in-your-organization/retaining-large-files-attached-to-a-meeting)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p174">If the Exchange Online mailbox of a meeting participant is placed on Litigation Hold or assigned to an Office 365 retention policy, files attached to a meeting are retained in the participants mailbox. You can use Content Search to search for those files in the participant's mailbox if the retention period for the file has not expired. For more information about retaining files, see [Retaining large files attached to a Skype for Business meeting](/skypeforbusiness/set-up-policies-in-your-organization/retaining-large-files-attached-to-a-meeting).</span></span>

## <a name="providing-a-copy-of-personal-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-480">提供个人数据副本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-480">Providing a copy of personal data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p175">在找到潜在响应 DSR 的个人数据后，应该由你和你的组织决定将哪些数据提供给数据主体。例如，可以为其提供实际文档副本、经过适当修订的版本或者你认为适合共享的部分的屏幕截图。对于访问请求的每个响应，需要检索包含响应数据的文档或其他项目的副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p175">After you've found personal data that is potentially responsive to a DSR, it's up to you and your organization to decide which data to provide the data subject. For example, you can provide them with a copy of the actual document, an appropriately redacted version, or a screenshot of the portions that you've deemed appropriate to share. For each of these responses to an access request, you'll have to retrieve a copy of the document or other item that contains the responsive data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-484">将副本提供给数据主体时，可能需要删除或修订有关其他数据主体和任何机密信息的个人信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-484">When providing a copy to the data subject, you may have to remove or redact personal information about other data subjects and any confidential information.</span></span>

### <a name="using-content-search-to-get-a-copy-of-personal-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-485">使用内容搜索获取个人数据副本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-485">Using Content Search to get a copy of personal data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-486">可通过两种方法使用内容搜索工具获取运行搜索后找到的文档或邮箱项目副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-486">There are two ways to use the Content Search tool to get a copy of a document or mailbox item that you've found after running a search.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p176">预览搜索结果，然后下载文档或项目副本。这是下载几个项目或文件的好方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p176">Preview the search results and then download a copy of the document or item. This is a good way to download a few items or files.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-489">导出搜索结果，然后下载搜索返回的所有项目副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-489">Export the search results and then download a copy of all items returned by the search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-490">此方法更为复杂，但却是下载大量响应 DSR 的项目的好方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-490">This method is more complex, but it's a good way to download lots of items that are responsive to the DSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-491">导出搜索结果中还包括一些实用的报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-491">Useful reports are also included with you export search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-492">可使用这些报告来获取有关每个项目的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-492">You can use these reports to get additional information about each item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-493">**Results.csv** 报告尤其有用，因为它包含大量有关导出项目的信息，如项目的提取位置（例如电子邮件的邮箱，或者位于 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 网站上的文档或列表的 URL）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-493">The **Results.csv** report is useful because it contains a lot of information about the exported items, such as the exact location of the item (for example, the mailbox for email messages or the URL for documents or lists on SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business sites).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-494">如果你需要在 DSR 调查过程中与项目所有者联系，此信息可帮助你识别该所有者的身份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-494">This information helps you identify the owner of the item, in case you need to contact them during the DSR investigation process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-495">有关导出搜索结果时包含的报告的详细信息，请参阅[导出内容搜索报告](/microsoft-365/compliance/export-a-content-search-report)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-495">For more information about the reports that are included when you export search results, see [Export a Content Search report](/microsoft-365/compliance/export-a-content-search-report).</span></span>

#### <a name="preview-and-download-items"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-496">预览和下载项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-496">Preview and download items</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-497">运行新搜索或打开现有搜索后，可审阅与搜索查询匹配的每个项目，验证其是否与正在调查的 DSR 相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-497">After you run a new search or open an existing search, you can preview each item that matched the search query to verify that it's related to the DSR you're investigating.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-498">这还包括在搜索结果中返回的 SharePoint 列表和网页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-498">This also includes SharePoint lists and web pages that are returned in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-499">你还可下载原始文件（如果必须向数据所有者提供该原始文件）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-499">You can also download the original file if you have to provide it to the data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-500">在两种情况下，都可进行屏幕截图，满足数据主体获取信息的请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-500">In both cases, you could take a screenshot to satisfy the data subject's request obtain the information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-501">某些类型的项目无法预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-501">Some types of items can't be previewed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-502">如果一个项目或文件类型不支持预览，可选择将各项目下载到本地计算机、映射的网络驱动器或其他网络位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-502">If an item or file type isn't supported for preview, you have the option to download an individual item to your local computer or to a mapped network drive or other network location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-503">仅可预览[受支持的文件类型](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-503">You can only preview [supported file types](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-504">预览和下载项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-504">To preview and download items:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-505">在安全与合规中心打开内容搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-505">Open the Content Search in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-506">如果未显示结果，请选择“**预览结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-506">If the results aren't displayed, select **Preview results**.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-507">选择一个项目进行查看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-507">select an item to view it.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-508">选择“**下载原始文件**”，将该项目下载到本地计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-508">select **Download original file** to download the item to your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-509">此外，还必须下载无法预览的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-509">You'll also have to download items that can't be previewed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-510">有关预览搜索结果的详细信息，请参阅[预览搜索结果](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-510">For more information about previewing search results, see [Preview search results](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search).</span></span>

#### <a name="export-and-download-items"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-511">导出和下载项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-511">Export and download items</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p181">还可以导出内容搜索的结果，以获取包含个人数据的电子邮件、文档、列表和网页的副本，但此方法比预览项目更复杂。请参阅下一节，了解有关[导出内容搜索结果](#export-and-download-content-using-content-search)的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p181">You can also export the results of a content search to get a copy of email messages, documents, lists, and web pages containing the personal data, though this method is more involved than previewing items. See the next section for details about [exporting the results of a Content Search](#export-and-download-content-using-content-search).</span></span>

## <a name="exporting-personal-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-514">导出个人数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-514">Exporting personal data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p182">“数据移植权限”允许数据主体请求“常用的计算机可读结构化格式”个人数据电子副本，还可请求组织将这些电子文件传输给另一数据控制者。Microsoft 通过两种方式为此权限提供支持：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p182">The "right of data portability" allows a data subject to request an electronic copy of personal data that's in a "structured, commonly used, machine-readable format", and to request that your organization transmit these electronic files to another data controller. Microsoft supports this right in two ways:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-517">提供以常用的计算机可读本机电子格式保存数据的 Office 365 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-517">Offering Office 365 applications that save data in native, machine-readable, commonly used electronic format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-518">有关 Office 文件格式的详细信息，请参阅 [Office 文件格式技术文档](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/office/cc313105(v=office.12).aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-518">For more information about Office file formats, see [Office File Formats-Technical Documents](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/office/cc313105(v=office.12).aspx).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-519">使组织能够以本机文件格式或可以轻松导入其他应用程序的格式（如 CSV、TXT 和 JSON）导出数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-519">Enabling your organization to export the data in the native file format, or a format (such as CSV, TXT, and JSON) that can be easily imported to another application.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-520">为了满足 DSR 导出请求，可以以本机文件格式导出 Office 文档，并从其他 Office 365 应用程序导出数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-520">To meet a DSR export request, you can export Office documents in their native file format and export data from other Office 365 applications.</span></span>

### <a name="export-and-download-content-using-content-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-521">使用内容搜索导出和下载内容</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-521">Export and download content using Content Search</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p184">导出内容搜索的结果时，电子邮件项目可下载为 PST 文件或单独的邮件（.msg 文件）。导出 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 网站中的文档和列表时，将导出本机文件格式的副本。例如，SharePoint 列表导出为 CSV 文件，而网页导出为 .aspx 或 html 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p184">When you export the results of a Content Search, email items can be downloaded as PST files or as individual messages (.msg files). When you export documents and lists from SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business sites, copies in the native file formats are exported. For example, SharePoint lists are exported as CSV files and Web pages are exported as .aspx or html files.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-525">使用内容搜索从某个用户的邮箱导出邮箱项目时，需要向该用户（你要导出其邮箱中的项目的用户）分配 Exchange Online 计划 2 许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-525">Exporting mailbox items from a user's mailbox using Content Search requires that the user (whose mailbox you're exporting items from) is assigned an Exchange Online Plan 2 license.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-526">导出和下载项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-526">To export and download items:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-527">在安全与合规中心打开内容搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-527">Open the Content Search in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-528">在搜索飞出页面上，选择![下载图标](../media/o365-dsr_image21.png)“**更多**”，然后选择“**导出结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-528">On the search fly out page, select ![download icon](../media/o365-dsr_image21.png) **More**, and then select **Export results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-529">你还可导出报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-529">You can also export a report.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-530">完成“**导出结果**”飞出页面上的部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-530">Complete the sections on the **Export results** fly out page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-531">请务必使用滚动条查看所有导出选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-531">Be sure to use the scroll bar to view all export options.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-532">返回安全与合规中心的内容搜索页面，并选择“**导出**”选项卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-532">Go back to the Content search page in the Security & Compliance Center, and select the **Export** tab.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-533">选择“**刷新**”更新页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-533">select **Refresh** to update the page.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-534">在“**名称**”列中，选择刚刚创建的导出作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-534">Under the **Name** column, select the export job that you created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-535">导出作业的名称为内容搜索名称追加 **\_Export**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-535">The name of the export job is the name of the content search appended with **\_Export**.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-536">在导出飞出页面上，选择“**导出密钥**”下的“**复制到剪贴板**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-536">On the export fly out page, under **Export key**, **select Copy to clipboard**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-537">在步骤 10 中，将使用此密钥下载搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-537">You'll use this key in step 10 to download the search results</span></span>
8. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-538">在飞出页面顶部，选择![下载图标](../media/o365-dsr_image21.png)“**下载结果**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-538">On the top of the fly out page, select ![download icon](../media/o365-dsr_image21.png) **Download results**.</span></span>
9. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-539">如果系统提示安装 **Microsoft Office 365 电子数据展示导出工具**，请选择“**安装**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-539">If you're prompted to install the **Microsoft Office 365 eDiscovery Export Tool**, select **Install**.</span></span>
10. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-540">在“**电子数据展示导出工具**”中，将在步骤 7 中复制的导出密钥粘贴在相应的框中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-540">In the **eDiscovery Export Tool**, paste the export key that you copied in step 7 in the appropriate box.</span></span>
11. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-541">选择“**浏览**”指定要下载搜索结果文件的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-541">select **Browse** to specify the location where you want to download the search result files.</span></span>
12. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-542">选择“**开始**”将搜索结果下载到计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-542">select **Start** to download the search results to your computer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p189">导出过程完成后，可以在本地计算机上下载文件的位置访问这些文件。内容搜索结果下载到随内容搜索命名的文件夹。来自网站的文档复制到一个名为 **SharePoint** 的子文件夹。邮箱项目复制到名为 **Exchange** 的子文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p189">When the export process is complete, you can access the files in the location on your local computer where they were downloaded. Results of a content search are downloaded to a folder named after the Content Search. Documents from sites are copied to a subfolder named **SharePoint**. Mailbox items are copied to subfolder named **Exchange**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-547">有关详细的分步说明，请参阅[从安全与合规中心导出内容搜索结果](/microsoft-365/compliance/export-search-results)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-547">For detailed step-by-step instructions, see [Export Content Search results from the Security & Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/export-search-results).</span></span>

### <a name="downloading-documents-and-lists-from-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-548">从 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 下载文档和列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-548">Downloading documents and lists from SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p190">从 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 导出数据的另一种方法是直接从 SharePoint Online 网站或 OneDrive for Business 帐户下载文档和列表。必须获得访问网站的权限，才可转到该网站并下载内容。请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p190">Another way to export data from SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business is to download documents and lists directly from a SharePoint Online site or a OneDrive for Business account. You would have to get assigned the permissions to access a site, and then go to the site and download the contents. See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-552">从 OneDrive 或 SharePoint 下载文件和文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-552">Download files and folders from OneDrive or SharePoint</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/download-files-and-folders-from-onedrive-or-sharepoint-5c7397b7-19c7-4893-84fe-d02e8fa5df05)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-553">将 SharePoint 列表导出到 Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-553">Export SharePoint lists to Excel</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/export-to-excel-from-sharepoint-bfb2ea48-6118-4fa9-abb6-cced9424e5d9)

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-554">对于某些 DSR 导出请求，你可能希望允许数据主体自行下载内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-554">For some DSR export requests, you may want to allow the data subject to download content themselves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-555">这使数据主体可以转到 SharePoint Online 网站或共享文件夹，然后选择“**同步**”以同步文档库或选定文件夹中的所有内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-555">This enables the data subject to go to a SharePoint Online site or shared folder and select **Sync** to sync all contents in the document library or selected folders.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-556">请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-556">See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-557">使用户能够通过新的 OneDrive 同步客户端同步 SharePoint 文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-557">Enable users to sync SharePoint files with the new OneDrive sync client</span></span>](/sharepoint/let-users-use-new-onedrive-sync-client)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-558">通过新的 OneDrive 同步客户端同步 SharePoint 文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-558">Sync SharePoint files with the new OneDrive sync client</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/sync-sharepoint-files-with-the-new-onedrive-sync-client-6de9ede8-5b6e-4503-80b2-6190f3354a88)

## <a name="deleting-personal-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-559">删除个人数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-559">Deleting personal data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-560">“擦除权限”可从组织的客户数据中移除个人数据，这是 GDPR 中的一项关键保护措施。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-560">The "right to erasure" by the removal of personal data from an organization's Customer Data is a key protection in the GDPR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-561">删除个人数据包括删除整个文档或文件，或删除文档或文件中的特定数据（相关操作和过程与本指南“纠正”部分所述的操作和过程相似）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-561">Removing personal data includes deleting entire documents or files or deleting specific data within a document or file (which would be an action and process like the ones described in the Rectify section in this guide).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-562">在调查或准备删除个人数据以响应 DSR 时，需要了解以下有关 Office 365 如何进行数据删除（和保留）的一些重要事项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-562">As you investigate or prepare to delete personal data in response to a DSR, here are a few important things to understand about how data deletion (and retention) works in Office 365.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-563">**软删除与硬删除：** 在诸如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 等 Office 365 服务中，存在 *软删除* 和 *硬删除* 的概念，它们在从 Microsoft 云中永久删除无法恢复之前与已删除项目的可恢复性有关（通常在一段有限时间内）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-563">**Soft delete vs. hard delete:** In Office 365 services such as Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, and OneDrive for Business there is the concept of *soft deletion* and *hard deletion*, which relates to the recoverability of a deleted item (usually for a limited period) before it's permanently removed from the Microsoft cloud with no chance of recovery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-564">在此上下文中，在硬删除项目之前一段有限的时间内，用户和/或管理员可恢复已软删除的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-564">In this context, a soft-deleted item can be recovered by a user and/or an admin for a limited amount of time before it's hard-deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-565">硬删除某个项目后，该项目将标记为永久删除，并将在相应的 Office 365 服务进行处理后立即清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-565">When an item has been hard-deleted, it's marked for permanent removal and is purged when it's processed by the corresponding Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-566">下面介绍了如何软删除和硬删除邮箱和网站中的项目（而无论是数据所有者还是管理员删除了项目）项目：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-566">Here's how soft delete and hard delete works for items in mailboxes and sites (regardless of whether the data owner or an admin deletes an item):</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-567">**邮箱：** 从“已删除邮件”文件夹删除某个项目，或通过按 **Shift + Delete** 删除某个项目时，该项目即被软删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-567">**Mailboxes:** An item is soft-deleted when it's deleted from the Deleted Items folder or when a user deletes an item by pressing **Shift + Delete**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-568">软删除项目后，该项目移动到邮箱中的“可恢复邮件”文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-568">When item is soft-deleted, it's moved to the Recoverable Items folder in the mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-569">此时，在已删除项目保留期限到期之前（在 Office 365 中，已删除项目保留策略为 14 天，但可由管理员增加到最多 30 天），用户可恢复该项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-569">At this point, the item can be recovered by the user until the deleted item retention period expires (in Office 365, the deleted item retention period is 14 days, but can be increased up to 30 days by an admin).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-570">保留期限到期后，项目被硬删除，并移动到一个隐藏文件夹（名为“*清除*”文件夹）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-570">After the retention period expires, the item is hard-deleted and moved to a hidden folder (called the *Purges* folder).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-571">该项目将在下一次处理邮箱时（每七天处理一次邮箱）从 Office 365 中永久删除（清除）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-571">The item will be permanently removed (purged) from Office 365 the next time the mailbox is processed (mailboxes are processed once every seven days).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-572">**SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 网站**：删除某个文件或文档后，该文件或文档移动到网站的回收站（也称为 *第一阶段回收站*，与 Windows 中的回收站类似）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-572">**SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business sites**: When a file or documented is deleted, it is moved to the site's Recycle Bin (also called the *first-stage Recycle Bin* (which is like the Recycle Bin in Windows).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-573">删除的项目在回收站中保留 93 天（Office 365 中网站的已删除项目保留期限）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-573">The item remains in the Recycle Bin for 93 days (the deleted item retention period for sites in Office 365).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-574">之后，该项目自动移动到网站集的的回收站（也称为 *第二阶段回收站*）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-574">After that period, the item is automatically moved to Recycle Bin for the site collection, which also called the *second-stage Recycle Bin*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-575">（请注意，具有相应权限的用户或管理员也可从第一阶段回收站中删除项目）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-575">(Note that users or admins--with the appropriate permissions--can also delete items from the first-stage Recycle Bin).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-576">此时，项目即被软删除；仍可由 SharePoint Online 中的网站集管理员或 OneDrive for Business 中的用户或管理员恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-576">At this point, the item becomes soft-deleted; it can still be recovered by a site collection administrator in SharePoint Online or by the user or admin in OneDrive for Business).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-577">项目从第二阶段回收站中删除后（无论是手动还是自动），该项目即被硬删除，用户或 IT 管理员无法再进行访问。第一阶段回收站和第二阶段回收站的保留期限都为 93 天。这意味着第二阶段回收站保留期从首次删除项目时开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-577">When an item is deleted from the second-stage Recycle Bin (either manually or automatically), it becomes hard-deleted and isn't accessible by user or an admin. The retention period is 93 days for both the first-stage and second-stage recycle bins. That means the second-stage Recycle Bin retention starts when the item is first deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-578">因此，两个回收站的总保留时间为 93 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-578">Therefore, the total maximum retention time is 93 days for both recycle bins.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-579">了解可导致项目软删除或硬删除的操作有助于在响应删除请求时，确定如何以符合 GDPR 要求的方式删除数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-579">Understanding the actions that result in an item being soft-deleted or hard-deleted will help you determine how to delete data in a way that meets GDPR requirements when responding to a deletion request.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-580">**法定保留和保留策略：** 在 Office 365 中，可对邮箱和网站实施“保留”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-580">**Legal holds and retention policies:** In Office 365, a "hold" can be place on mailboxes and sites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-581">简言之，这意味着如果邮箱或网站处于保留状态，则在项目的保留期限到期或删除保留之前，不会永久删除（硬删除）任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-581">In short, this means that nothing is permanently removed (hard-deleted) if a mailbox or site is on hold, until the retention period for an item expires or until the hold is removed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-582">在删除客户内容以响应 DSR 时，这一点非常重要：如果从处于保留状态的内容位置硬删除某个项目，不会从 Office 365 永久删除该项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-582">This is important in the context of deleting Customer Content in response to a DSR: if an item is hard-deleted from a content location that is on hold, the item is not permanently removed from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-583">这意味着 IT 管理员有可能恢复该项目。如果组织的要求和策略规定永久删除 Office 365 中的数据并使其无法恢复以响应 DSR，则必须从邮箱或网站删除保留，以便永久删除 Office 365 中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-583">That means it could conceivably be recovered by an IT admin. If your organization has a requirement or policy that data be permanently deleted and unrecoverable in Office 365 in response to DSR, then a hold would have to be removed from a mailbox or site to permanently delete data in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-584">组织针对响应 DSR 的指导原则很可能已制定了一个流程，用于确定是特定 DSR 删除请求还是法定保留优先。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-584">More than likely, your organization's guidelines for responding to DSRs have a process in place to determine whether a specific DSR deletion request or a legal hold takes precedence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-585">如果删除了保留以便删除项目，可在删除项目后重新实施保留。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-585">If a hold is removed to delete items, it can be reimplemented after the item is deleted.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-586">删除 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文档</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-586">Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-587">找到 SharePoint Online 网站或 OneDrive for Business 帐户中需要删除的文档后（按照本指南“发现”部分的指导操作），需要向数据隐私部主管或 IT 管理员分配访问网站和删除文档的必要权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-587">After you find the document on a SharePoint Online site or in a OneDrive for Business account (by following the guidance in Discover section of this guide) that needs to be deleted, a data privacy officer or IT admin would need to be assigned the necessary permissions to access the site and delete the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-588">在适当情况下，也可指示文档所有者删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-588">If appropriate, the document owner can also be instructed to delete the document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-589">下面是从网站删除文档的高级流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-589">Here's the high-level process for deleting documents from sites.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-590">转到网站并定位文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-590">Go to the site and locate the document.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p198">删除文档。从网站删除文档时，该文档发送到第一阶段回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p198">Delete the document. When you delete a document from a site, it's sent to the first-stage Recycle Bin.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p199">转到第一阶段回收站（网站回收站），并删除在上一步中删除的同一文档。文档现在发送到第二阶段回收站。**此时，文档已软删除**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p199">Go to the first-stage Recycle Bin (the site Recycle Bin) and delete the same document you deleted in the previous step. The document is sent to the second-stage Recycle Bin. **At this point, the document is soft-deleted**.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p200">转到第二阶段回收站（网站集回收站），并删除之前从第一阶段回收站中删除的同一文档。**此时，文档已硬删除。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p200">Go to the second-stage Recycle Bin (which is the site collection Recycle Bin) and delete the same document that you deleted from the first-stage Recycle Bin. **At this point, the document is hard-deleted.**</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p201">无法从处于保留状态（在 Office 365 中使用了某项保留或法定保留功能）的网站删除文档。如果 DSR 删除请求优先于法定保留，必须先从网站删除保留，才可永久删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p201">You can't delete a document that is located on a site that is on hold (with one of the retention or legal hold features in Office 365). In the case where a DSR delete request takes precedence over a legal hold, the hold would have to be removed from the site before a document could be permanently deleted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-600">有关详细过程，请参阅以下主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-600">See the following topics for detailed procedures.</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-601">从 SharePoint 文档库删除文件、文件夹或链接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-601">Delete a file, folder, or link from a SharePoint document library</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-file-folder-or-link-from-a-sharepoint-document-library-71f3c90a-0d24-4d80-8b66-f88234b79a52)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-602">删除 SharePoint 网站回收站中的项目或将其清空</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-602">Delete items or empty the Recycle Bin of a SharePoint site</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-or-empty-the-recycle-bin-of-a-sharepoint-site-2e713599-d13e-40d6-96dc-66f0a366f74e)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-603">从网站集回收站中删除项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-603">Delete items from the site collection recycle bin</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-from-the-site-collection-recycle-bin-dd5c00c2-aef6-4458-9d04-80b185077653)
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-604">[获取对前员工用户数据的访问权限并备份该数据](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)中的“获取对前员工 OneDrive for Business 文档的访问权限”部分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-604">"Get access to the former employee's OneDrive for Business documents" section in [Get access to and back up a former user's data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-605">删除 OneDrive for Business 中的文件或文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-605">Delete files or folders in OneDrive for Business</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/Delete-files-or-folders-in-OneDrive-21fe345a-e488-4fa7-932b-f053c1bebe8a)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-606">删除 SharePoint 中的列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-606">Delete a list in SharePoint</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-list-in-sharepoint-2a7bca5b-b8fd-4e5b-8f4b-2ac034f3070d)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-607">删除 SharePoint Online 中的列表项</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-607">Delete list items in SharePoint Online</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/delete-list-items-in-sharepoint-online-db722233-4a38-4889-a6cf-4b33fe5c60c0)

### <a name="deleting-a-sharepoint-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-608">删除 SharePoint 网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-608">Deleting a SharePoint site</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p202">你可能会确定响应 DSR 删除请求的最佳方法是删除整个 SharePoint 网站，从而删除位于该网站中的所有数据。可以通过在 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中运行 cmdlet 来执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p202">You may determine that the best way to respond to a DSR delete request is to delete an entire SharePoint site, which will delete all that data located in the site. You can do this by running cmdlets in SharePoint Online PowerShell.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-611">使用 [Remove-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-sposite) cmdlet 删除网站，并将其移动到 SharePoint Online 回收站（软删除）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-611">Use the [Remove-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-sposite) cmdlet to delete the site and move it the SharePoint Online Recycle Bin (soft-delete).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-612">使用 [Remove-SPODeletedSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spodeletedsite) cmdlet 永久删除网站（硬删除）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-612">Use the [Remove-SPODeletedSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spodeletedsite) cmdlet to permanently delete the site (hard-delete).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-613">无法删除实施了电子数据展示保留或分配到保留策略的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-613">You can't delete a site that is placed on an eDiscovery hold or is assigned to a retention policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-614">必须先从电子数据展示保留或保留策略删除网站，然后才能删除网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-614">Sites must be removed from an eDiscovery hold or retention policy before you can delete it.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-a-onedrive-for-business-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-615">删除 OneDrive for Business 网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-615">Deleting a OneDrive for Business site</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p204">同样，你可能会确定删除用户的 OneDrive for Business 网站以响应 DSR 删除请求。如果删除了用户的 Office 365 帐户，其 OneDrive for Business 网站保留 30 天（可恢复）。30 天后，该网站移动到 SharePoint Online 回收站（软删除），然后在 93 天后永久删除（硬删除）。要加快此过程，可使用 [Remove-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-sposite) cmdlet 将 OneDrive for Business 网站移动到回收站，然后使用 [Remove-SPODeletedSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spodeletedsite) cmdlet 将其永久删除。与 SharePoint Online 中的网站一样，如果用户的 OneDrive for Business 网站在删除用户帐户前分配到电子数据展示保留或保留策略，则无法将其删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p204">Similarly, you may determine to delete a user's OneDrive for Business site in response to a DSR deletion request. If you delete the user's Office 365 account, their OneDrive for Business site is retained (and restorable) for 30 days. After 30 days, it's moved to the SharePoint Online Recycle Bin (soft-deleted), and then after 93 days, it's permanently deleted (hard-deleted). To accelerate this process, you can use the [Remove-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-sposite) cmdlet to move the OneDrive for Business site to the Recycle Bin and then use the [Remove-SPODeletedSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spodeletedsite) cmdlet to permanently delete it. As with sites in SharePoint Online, you can't delete a user's OneDrive for Business site if it was assigned to an eDiscovery hold or a retention policy before the user's account was deleted.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online-experience-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-621">删除 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 体验设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-621">Deleting OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online Experience Settings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-622">除了存储在 OneDrive for Business 帐户和 SharePoint Online 站点中的用户创建的文件外，这些服务还存储用于实现各种体验的用户相关信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-622">In addition to user-created files stored in OneDrive for Business accounts and SharePoint Online sites, these services store information about the user that is used to enable various experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-623">本文档中以前记录了这些信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-623">These were previously documented in this document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-624">请参阅[使用内容搜索电子数据展示工具来响应 DSR](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs) 下的[选定应用程序的其他注意事项](#additional-considerations-for-selected-applications)部分，了解有关如何访问、查看和导出 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 应用程序数据的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-624">See the [Additional considerations for selected applications](#additional-considerations-for-selected-applications) section under [Using the Content Search eDiscovery tool to respond to DSRs](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs) for information about how to access, view, and export OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online application data.</span></span>

#### <a name="deleting-a-sharepoint-user-profile"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-625">删除 SharePoint 用户个人资料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-625">Deleting a SharePoint user profile</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p206">在 Azure Active Directory 中删除用户帐户 30 天后，将永久删除 SharePoint 用户个人资料。但也可通过硬删除用户帐户来删除 SharePoint 用户个人资料。有关详细信息，请参阅[本指南中的删除用户部分](#deleting-a-user)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p206">The SharePoint user profile will be permanently deleted 30 days after the user account is deleted in Azure Active Directory. However, you can hard-delete the user account, which will remove the SharePoint user profile. For more information, see the [Deleting a user section in this guide](#deleting-a-user).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p207">管理员可以通过使用 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中的 **Remove-SPOUserProfile** cmdlet 来加速用户个人资料的删除过程。请参阅 [Remove-SPOUserProfile](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spouserprofile)。这要求用户至少在 Azure Active Directory 中被软删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p207">An admin can expedite the deletion of the User Profile for a user by using the **Remove-SPOUserProfile** cmdlet in SharePoint Online PowerShell. See [Remove-SPOUserProfile](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spouserprofile). This requires the user to be at least soft-deleted in Azure Active Directory.</span></span>

#### <a name="deleting-user-information-lists-on-sharepoint-online-sites"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-632">删除 SharePoint Online 网站上的用户信息列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-632">Deleting User Information lists on SharePoint Online sites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p208">对于已离开组织的用户，此数据仍保留在他们与之进行交互的网站中，以实现 SharePoint 列字段的引用完整性。管理员可以通过使用 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中的 **Remove-SPOUserInfo** 命令删除给定站点上用户的所有用户信息属性。有关运行此 PowerShell cmdlet 的信息，请参阅 [Remove-SPOUserInfo](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spouserinfo)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p208">For users that have left the organization, this data remains in the sites they interacted with for referential integrity of SharePoint column fields. An admin can delete all User information properties for a user on a given site by using the **Remove-SPOUserInfo** command in SharePoint Online PowerShell. See [Remove-SPOUserInfo](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/remove-spouserinfo) for information about running this PowerShell cmdlet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-636">默认情况下，此命令会保留用户的显示名称，并删除属性，如电话号码、电子邮件地址、技能和专业知识或者从 SharePoint Online 用户个人资料复制的其他属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-636">By default, this command retains the display name of the user and deleted properties such as telephone number, email address, skills and expertise, or other properties that were copied from the SharePoint Online user profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-637">管理员可以使用 **RedactUser** 参数来指定用户信息列表中用户的备用显示名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-637">An admin can use the **RedactUser** parameter to specify an alternate display name for the user in the User Information list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-638">这会影响用户体验的多个部分，并在查看网站中的文件历史记录时，将导致信息丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-638">This affects several parts of the user experience and will result in information loss when looking at the history of files in the site.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p210">最后，修订功能将无法删除从文档引用用户的所有元数据或内容。本指南的[更改 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 中的内容](#making-changes-to-content-in-onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online)部分介绍了实现文件内容和元数据修订的方法。此方法包括下载、删除，然后上传文件的修订副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p210">Finally, the redaction capability will not remove all metadata or content referencing a user from documents. The way to achieve redaction of file content and metadata is described in the [Making changes to content in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online](#making-changes-to-content-in-onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online) section in this guide. This method consists of downloading, deleting, and then uploading a redacted copy of the file.</span></span>

#### <a name="deleting-onedrive-for-business-experience-settings"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-642">删除 OneDrive for Business 体验设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-642">Deleting OneDrive for Business experience settings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p211">删除所有 OneDrive for Business 体验设置和信息的建议方法是，向其他用户重新分配任何保留的文件后，删除相应用户的 OneDrive for Business 网站。管理员可以使用 [PowerShell 脚本](/powershell/scripting/overview)和 [SharePoint 客户端对象模型 (CSOM)](/sharepoint/dev/sp-add-ins/complete-basic-operations-using-sharepoint-client-library-code) 命令来删除这些列表。有关设置、存储方式和如何将其删除的详细信息，请参阅[删除 OneDrive for Business 体验设置](/sharepoint/delete-odfb-lists)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p211">The recommended way to delete all OneDrive for Business experience settings and information is to remove the user's OneDrive for Business site, after reassigning any retained files to other users. An admin can delete these lists using [PowerShell Script](/powershell/scripting/overview) and [SharePoint Client-Side Object Model (CSOM)](/sharepoint/dev/sp-add-ins/complete-basic-operations-using-sharepoint-client-library-code) commands. See [Deleting OneDrive for Business experience settings](/sharepoint/delete-odfb-lists) for more information about the settings, how they are stored, and how to delete them.</span></span>

#### <a name="onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online-search-queries"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-646">OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 搜索查询</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-646">OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online search queries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-647">用户在 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 搜索体验中创建的搜索查询在用户创建该查询 30 天后自动删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-647">A user's search queries created in the OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online search experience are automatically deleted 30 days after the user creates the query.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-items-in-exchange-online-mailboxes"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-648">删除 Exchange Online 邮箱中的项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-648">Deleting items in Exchange Online mailboxes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-649">可能需要删除 Exchange Online 邮箱中的项目来满足 DSR 删除请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-649">You may have to delete items in Exchange Online mailboxes to satisfy a DSR delete request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-650">IT 管理员可通过两种方法删除邮箱中的项目，具体取决于是要软删除还是硬删除目标项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-650">There are two ways that an IT admin can delete items in mailbox, depending on whether to soft-delete or hard-delete the target items.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-651">与 SharePoint Online 或 OneDrive for Business 网站上的文档相似，无法从 Office 365 永久删除处于保留状态的邮箱中的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-651">Like documents on SharePoint Online or OneDrive for Business sites, items in a mailbox that is on hold can't be permanently deleted from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-652">必须先删除保留，然后才能删除该项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-652">The hold must be removed before the item can be deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-653">同样，必须确定是保留邮箱还是 DSR 删除请求优先。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-653">Again, you'll have to determine whether the hold on the mailbox or the DSR delete request takes precedence.</span></span>

#### <a name="soft-delete-mailbox-items"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-654">软删除邮箱项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-654">Soft-delete mailbox items</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-655">可以使用内容搜索操作功能软删除内容搜索返回的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-655">You can use the Content Search Action functionality to soft-delete items that are returned by a Content Search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-656">如前所述，软删除的项目将移动到邮箱中的“可恢复的项目”文件夹中，而硬删除的项目将被永久删除且无法恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-656">As previously explained, soft-deleted items are moved to the Recoverable Items folder in the mailbox while hard-deleted items are permanently deleted and cannot be recovered.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-657">下文快速概述了此过程：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-657">Here's a quick overview of this process:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-658">创建并运行内容搜索，查找要从用户邮箱中删除的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-658">Create and run a Content Search to find the items that you want to delete from the user mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-659">可能需要重新运行搜索以缩小搜索结果的范围，以便搜索结果中只返回要删除的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-659">You may have to rerun the search to narrow that search results so that only the items that you want to delete are returned in the search results.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-660">在 Office 365 PowerShell 中使用 **New-ComplianceSearchAction** **-Purge** **PurgeType** **SoftDelete** 或 **New-ComplianceSearchAction** **-Purge** **PurgeType** **HardDelete** 命令，删除由在上一步中创建的内容搜索返回的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-660">Use the **New-ComplianceSearchAction** **-Purge** **PurgeType** **SoftDelete** or **New-ComplianceSearchAction** **-Purge** **PurgeType** **HardDelete** command in Office 365 PowerShell to delete items that are returned by the Content Search that was created in the previous step.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-661">有关详细说明，请参阅[在组织中搜索并删除电子邮件](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-for-and-delete-messages-in-your-organization)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-661">For detailed instructions, see [Search for and delete email messages in your organization](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-for-and-delete-messages-in-your-organization).</span></span>

#### <a name="hard-delete-items-in-a-mailbox-on-hold"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-662">硬删除处于保留状态的邮箱中的项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-662">Hard-delete items in a mailbox on hold</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p215">如前文所述，如果硬删除处于保留状态的邮箱中的项目，不会从邮箱中删除该项目。这些项目移动到“可恢复邮件”文件夹中的一个隐藏文件夹（**清除** 文件夹）并保留在其中，直到项目的保留持续时间到期或从邮箱删除了保留。如果发生上述任一事件，则这些项目在下一次处理邮箱时从 Office 365 中清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p215">As previously explained, if you hard-delete items in a mailbox on hold, items are not removed from the mailbox. They are moved to a hidden folder in the Recoverable Items folder (the **Purges** folder) and will remain there until the hold duration for the item expires or until the hold is removed from the mailbox. If either of those things happen, the items will be purged from Office 365 the next time that the mailbox is processed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p216">组织可能确定在保留持续时间到期时永久删除项目，以满足 DSR 删除请求的要求。但是，如果你确定必须立即从 Office 365 中清除邮箱项目，则必须从邮箱删除保留，然后从邮箱硬删除项目。有关详细说明，请参阅[删除基于云且处于保留状态的邮箱中可恢复邮件文件夹中的项目](/microsoft-365/compliance/delete-items-in-the-recoverable-items-folder-of-mailboxes-on-hold)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p216">Your organization might determine that items being permanently deleted when the hold duration expires meets the requirements for a DSR deletion request. However, if you determine that mailbox items must be immediately purged from Office 365, you would have to remove the hold from the mailbox and then hard-deleted the items from the mailbox. For detailed instructions, see [Delete items in the Recoverable Items folder of cloud-based mailboxes on hold](/microsoft-365/compliance/delete-items-in-the-recoverable-items-folder-of-mailboxes-on-hold).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-669">要按照上一主题中所述的过程硬删除邮箱项目以满足 DSR 删除请求，可能需要在邮箱仍处于保留状态时软删除这些项目，以便它们移动到“可恢复的项目”文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-669">To hard-delete mailbox items to satisfy a DSR deletion request by following the procedure in the previous topic, you may have to soft-delete those items while the mailbox is still on hold so that they are moved to the Recoverable Items folder.</span></span>

## <a name="deleting-a-user"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-670">删除用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-670">Deleting a user</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p217">除了删除个人数据以响应 DSR 删除请求外，还可通过删除用户帐户来实现数据主体的“被遗忘权”。以下是可能需要删除用户一些原因：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p217">In addition to deleting personal data in response to a DSR deletion request, a data subject's "right to be forgotten" may also be fulfilled by deleting their user account. Here are some reasons that you might want to delete a user:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-673">数据主体已离开（或正在离开）组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-673">The data subject has left (or is in the process of leaving) your organization.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p218">数据主体已请求删除已收集的与其相关的系统生成日志。系统生成日志的数据示例包括 Office 365 应用和服务使用情况数据、数据主体执行的搜索请求的相关信息、作为系统功能一部分的产品和服务所生成的数据以及用户或其他系统的交互。有关详细信息，请参阅本指南中的[第 3 部分：响应系统生成日志的 DSR](#part-3-responding-to-dsrs-for-system-generated-logs)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p218">The data subject has requested that you delete system-generated logs that have been collected about them. Examples of data in system-generated logs include Office 365 app and service usage data, information about search requests performed by the data subject, and data generated by product and services as a product of system functionality and interaction by users or other systems. For more information, see [Part 3: Responding to DSRs for system-generated Logs](#part-3-responding-to-dsrs-for-system-generated-logs) in this guide.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-677">永久防止数据主体访问或处理 Office 365 中的数据（与通过[响应 DSR 限制请求](#responding-to-dsr-restriction-requests)部分中所述的方法临时限制访问完全不同）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-677">Permanently prevent the data subject from accessing or processing data in Office 365 (as opposed to temporarily restriction access by the methods described in the section [Responding to DSR restriction requests](#responding-to-dsr-restriction-requests).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-678">删除用户帐户后：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-678">After you delete a user account:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-679">用户无法再登录 Office 365 或访问组织的任何 Microsoft 资源，例如其 OneDrive for Business 帐户、SharePoint Online 网站或其 Exchange Online 邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-679">The user can no longer sign-in to Office 365 or access any of your organization's Microsoft resources, such as their OneDrive for Business account, SharePoint Online sites, or their Exchange Online mailbox.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-680">将删除与该用户帐户关联的个人数据，例如电子邮件地址，别名、电话号码和通讯地址</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-680">Personal data, such as email address, alias, phone number, and mailing address, that's associated with the user account is deleted</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-681">某些 Office 365 应用将删除有关该用户的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-681">Some Office 365 apps remove information about the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-682">例如，在 Microsoft Flow 中，将从共享流的所有者列表中移除已删除的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-682">For example, in Microsoft Flow, the deleted user is removed from the list of owners for a shared flow.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-683">删除用户帐户 30 天后，将删除有关数据主体的系统生成日志（不包括可能会危及服务安全性和稳定性的数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-683">System-generated logs about the data subject, with the exception of data that may compromise the security or stability of the service, will be deleted 30 days after the user account is deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-684">有关详细信息，请参阅[删除系统生成日志](#deleting-system-generated-logs)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-684">For more information, see the section [Deleting system-generated logs](#deleting-system-generated-logs).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p221">删除用户帐户后，该用户无法再登录 Office 365，也无法登录其以前依赖的工作或学校帐户下的任何产品或服务。该用户还将无法直接在 Microsoft 作为数据控制者的实例中通过 Microsoft 发起任何 DSR 请求。有关详细信息，请参阅本指南第 4 部分[通过组织 ID 进行身份验证且由 Microsoft 作为数据控制者的产品和服务](#product-and-services-authenticated-with-an-org-id-for-which-microsoft-is-a-data-controller)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p221">After you delete a user account, that person will lose the ability to sign in to Office 365 and the ability to sign in to any products or services for which he or she formerly relied upon for a work or school account. That person would also be unable to initiate any DSR requests through Microsoft directly in instances where Microsoft is the data controller. For more information, see the [Product and services authenticated with an Org ID for which Microsoft is a data controller](#product-and-services-authenticated-with-an-org-id-for-which-microsoft-is-a-data-controller) section in Part 4 of this guide.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p222">如果你是目前正在使用 FastTrack 迁移的客户，那么删除用户帐户将不会删除由 Microsoft FastTrack 团队保留的数据副本（该副本仅保留用于完成迁移）。在迁移过程中，如果你希望 Microsoft FastTrack 团队同时删除数据副本，可以[提交请求](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=874544)。在正常业务过程中，Microsoft FastTrack 将在迁移完成后立即删除所有数据副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p222">In the event that you are a customer currently engaged in FastTrack migrations, deleting the user account will not delete the data copy held by the Microsoft FastTrack team, which is held for the sole purpose of completing the migration. If, during the migration, you would like the Microsoft FastTrack team to also delete the data copy, you can [submit a request](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=874544). In the ordinary course of business, Microsoft FastTrack will delete all data copies once the migration is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-691">与前文所述有关删除个人数据的软删除和硬删除数据相似，删除用户帐户时，也有软删除和硬删除状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-691">Like the soft-deletion and hard-deletion of data that was described in the previous section on deleting personal data, when you delete a user account, there is also a soft-deleted and hard-deleted state.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-692">最初删除用户帐户（通过在管理中心或 Azure 门户中删除用户）时，用户帐户被软删除，并在最多 30 天后移动到 Azure 中的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-692">When you initially delete a user account (by deleting the user in the admin center or in the Azure portal), the user account is soft-deleted, and moved the Recycle Bin in Azure for up to 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-693">此时，可以还原该用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-693">At this point, the user account can be restored.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p224">永久删除用户帐户后，用户帐户被硬删除，并从 Azure 中的回收站删除。此时，无法还原用户帐户，并且与用户帐户关联的任何数据都将从 Microsoft 云中永久删除。硬删除帐户还会删除有关数据主体的系统生成日志（不包括可能会危及服务安全性和稳定性的数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p224">If you permanently deleted the user account, the user account is hard-deleted and removed from the Recycle Bin in Azure. At this point, the user account can't be restored, and any data associated with the user account will be permanently removed from the Microsoft cloud. Hard-deleting an account deletes system-generated logs about the data subject, except for data that may compromise the security or stability of the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-697">下面是从组织删除用户的高级流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-697">Here's the high-level process for deleting a user from your organization.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-698">转到管理中心或 Azure 门户，并找到用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-698">Go to the admin center or the Azure portal and locate the user.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p225">删除用户。最初删除用户时，用户帐户发送到回收站。此时，用户被软删除。该帐户保持软删除状态 30 天，在此期间可还原该帐户。30 天后，该帐户自动硬删除。有关具体说明，请参阅[从 Azure AD 删除用户](/azure/active-directory/add-users-azure-active-directory)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p225">Delete the user. When you initially delete the user, the user's account is sent to the Recycle Bin. At this point, the user is soft-deleted. The account is retained in the soft-deleted for 30 days, which allows you to restore the account. After 30 days, the account is automatically hard-deleted. For specific instructions, see [Delete users from Azure AD](/azure/active-directory/add-users-azure-active-directory).</span></span><br><br> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-705">还可在管理中心软删除用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-705">You can also soft-delete a user account in the admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-706">请参阅[从组织中删除用户](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-706">See [Delete a user from your organization](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user).</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-707">如果不想等到 30 天后才硬删除用户帐户，可以手动进行硬删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-707">If you don't want to wait for 30-days for the user account to be hard-deleted, you can manually hard-delete it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-708">要在 Azure 门户中执行此操作，请转到最近删除的用户列表并永久删除用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-708">To do this in the Azure portal, go to the Recently deleted users list and permanently delete the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-709">此时，用户被硬删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-709">At this point, the user is hard-deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-710">有关说明，请参阅[如何永久删除最近删除的用户](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-restore)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-710">For instructions, see [How to permanently delete a recently deleted user](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-restore).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-711">无法在 Office 365 管理门户中硬删除用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-711">You can't hard-delete a user in the Office 365 admin portal.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p228">在由世纪互联运营的 Office 365（中国版）中，不能按照上文所述的方式永久删除用户。若要永久删除用户，可以在此 [URL](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage) 中通过 Office 365 管理门户来提交请求。转到“**商务**”，然后选择“**订阅**” -> “**隐私**” ->  “**GDPR**”并输入所需的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p228">In Office 365 operated by 21Vianet (China), you can't permanently delete a user as previously described. To permanently delete a user, you can submit a request via the Office 365 admin portal at this [URL](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage). Go to **Commerce** and then select **Subscription** -> **Privacy** ->  **GDPR** and enter the required information.</span></span>

### <a name="removing-exchange-online-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-715">删除 Exchange Online 数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-715">Removing Exchange Online data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-716">删除用户时，需要注意用户的 Exchange Online 邮箱会发生哪些变化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-716">One thing to understand when deleting a user is what happens to the user's Exchange Online mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-717">硬删除用户帐户后（在先前流程的步骤 3 中），已删除用户的邮箱未自动从 Office 365 中清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-717">After the user account is hard-deleted (in step 3 in the previous process) the deleted user's mailbox isn't automatically purged from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-718">硬删除用户帐户后，需要最多 60 天才可从 Office 365 中永久删除该用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-718">It takes up to 60 days after the user account is hard-deleted to permanently remove it from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-719">下面描述了删除用户帐户后的邮箱生命周期，以及该期间内邮箱数据的状态：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-719">Here's the mailbox lifecycle after the user account is deleted and a description of the state of the mailbox data during that time:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-720">**第 1 天 — 第 30 天** — 可通过还原软删除的用户帐户完全还原邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-720">**Day 1-Day 30** — The mailbox can be fully restored by restoring the soft-deleted user account.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-721">**第 31 天 — 第 60 天** — 在硬删除用户帐户 30 天后，组织中的管理员可恢复邮箱中的数据，并将其导入其他邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-721">**Day 31-Day 60** — For 30 days after the user account is hard-deleted, an admin in your organization can recover the data in the mailbox and import it into a different mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-722">这样，组织将能在必要时恢复邮箱数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-722">This provides organizations the ability to recover the mailbox data if necessary.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-723">**第 61 天 – 第 90 天** - 管理员不再能恢复邮箱中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-723">**Day 61-Day 90** - An admin can no longer recover the data in the mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-724">邮箱数据将被标记为永久删除，并且最多还要 30 天才会被从 Office 365 中清除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-724">The mailbox data will be marked for permanent removal, and it takes up to 30 more days for the mailbox data to be purged from Office 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-725">如果确定此邮箱生命周期无法满足组织响应 DSR 删除请求的要求，可在硬删除用户帐户 *后*[联系 Microsoft 支持部门](https://support.microsoft.com/)，请求 Microsoft 手动启动永久删除邮箱数据的流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-725">If you determine that this mailbox lifecycle doesn't meet your organization's requirements for responding to a DSR deletion request, you can [contact Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/) *after* you hard-delete the user account, and request Microsoft to manually initiate the process to permanently remove the mailbox data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-726">此永久删除邮箱数据的流程在邮箱生命周期的第 61 天自动开始，因此没有理由在生命周期的此时间点后联系 Microsoft。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-726">This process to permanently remove mailbox data starts automatically after day 61 in the lifecycle, so there would be no reason to contact Microsoft after this point in the lifecycle.</span></span>

## <a name="using-in-app-functionality-to-respond-to-dsrs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-727">使用应用内功能响应 DSR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-727">Using In-App functionality to respond to DSRs</span></span>
