<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-728">虽然大多数客户数据是使用上一节所述的应用程序进行创作和生成的，但 Office 365 也提供了许多其他应用程序，客户可以使用它们来生成和存储客户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-728">While most Customer Data is authored and produced using the applications described in the previous section, Office 365 also offers many other applications that customers can use to produce and store Customer Data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-729">但是，“内容搜索”当前尚不能找到在这些其他 Office 365 应用程序中创作的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-729">However, Content Search doesn't currently have the ability to find data authored in these other Office 365 applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-730">若要查找这些应用程序生成的数据，你或数据所有者必须使用产品内功能查找可能与 DSR 相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-730">To find data generated by these applications, you or the data owner must use in-product functionality or features to find data that may be relevant to a DSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-731">下表列出了这些 Office 365 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-731">The following list identifies these Office 365 applications.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-732">可在其中使用应用内功能查找客户数据的应用程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-732">Applications where in-app functionality can be used to find Customer Data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-733">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-733">Access</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-734">Business App  for Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-734">Business App for Office 365</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-735">教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-735">Education</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-736">Flow</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-736">Flow</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-737">Forms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-737">Forms</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-738">Kaizala</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-738">Kaizala</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-739">Microsoft Planner</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-739">Planner</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-740">Power Apps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-740">Power Apps</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-741">Power BI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-741">Power BI</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-742">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-742">Project</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-743">Publisher</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-743">Publisher</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-744">Stream</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-744">Stream</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-745">Yammer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-745">Yammer</span></span>

### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-746">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-746">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-747">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Access 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-747">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Access to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-748">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-748">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p234">有几种方法可以在 Access 数据库中搜索可能响应 DSR 请求的记录。对于 DSR 调查，可以搜索与数据主体相关的记录，或者搜索包含特定数据的记录。例如，可以搜索或访问与数据主体相对应的记录。也可以搜索包含特定数据的记录，比如关于数据主体的个人数据。有关更多信息，请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p234">There are several ways that you can search for records in an Access database that might be responsive to a DSR request. For a DSR investigation, you can search for records that related to the data subject or search for records that contain specific data. For example, you could either search or go to a record that corresponds to the data subject. Or you can search for records that contain specific data, such as personal data about the data subject. For more information, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-754">在 Access 数据库中查找记录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-754">Find records in an Access database</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/find-records-in-an-access-database-705220b7-0255-4ef9-9349-6bd7442d1b7e) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-755">创建简单的选择查询</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-755">Create a simple select query</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/create-a-simple-select-query-de8b1c8d-14e9-4b25-8e22-70888d54de59)

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-756">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-756">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p235">查找与 DSR 请求相关的记录或字段后，可以获取数据的屏幕截图，或者将其导出到 Excel 文件、Word 文件或文本文件中。还可以根据记录源或为查找数据而创建的选择查询创建和打印报表。请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p235">After you find the records or fields that are relevant to the DSR request, you can take a screenshot of the data or export it to an Excel file, Word file, or a text file. You can also create and print a report based on a record source, or a select query that you created to find the data. See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-760">Access 中的报表简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-760">Introduction to reports in Access</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/introduction-to-reports-in-access-e0869f59-7536-4d19-8e05-7158dcd3681c)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-761">将数据导出到 Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-761">Export data to Excel</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/export-data-to-excel-64e974e6-ae43-4301-a53e-20463655b1a9)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-762">将数据导出到 Word 文档</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-762">Export data to a Word document</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/export-access-data-to-a-word-document-6e954c8e-2243-4cb9-8544-607e5b7bfc12)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-763">将数据导出到文本文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-763">Export data to a text file</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/export-data-to-a-text-file-f72dfc38-a8a0-4c5b-8c2c-bf2950814140)

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-764">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-764">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-765">如前所述，可将数据从 Access 数据库导出为不同文件格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-765">As previously explained, you can export data from an Access database to different file formats.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-766">选择导出的文件格式可能由来自数据主体的特定 DSR 导出请求决定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-766">The export file format that you choose might be determined by the specific DSR export request from a data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-767">有关如何以不同的文件格式导出 Access 数据的主题列表，请参阅[导入和导出](https://support.microsoft.com/office/import-and-export-c060505b-d8ac-4499-8879-733e56c6106f)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-767">See [Import and export](https://support.microsoft.com/office/import-and-export-c060505b-d8ac-4499-8879-733e56c6106f) for a list of topics that describe how to export Access data in different file formats.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-768">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-768">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-769">可从 Access 数据库删除整个记录或仅删除一个字段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-769">You can delete an entire record or just a field from an Access database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-770">从 Access 数据库删除记录的最快方式是在数据表视图中打开表，选择要删除的字段中的记录（行）或仅数据，然后按“Delete”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-770">The quickest way to delete a record from an Access database is to open the table in Datasheet view, select the record (row) or just the data in a field that you want to delete, and then press Delete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-771">此外可以使用为查找数据而创建的选择查询，然后将其转换为删除查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-771">You can also use a select query that you created to find data and then convert it to a delete query.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-772">请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-772">See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-773">从数据库删除一个或多个记录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-773">Delete one or more records from a database</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/ways-to-add-edit-and-delete-records-5e90a80c-106d-4c55-996e-07d7200980ce)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-774">创建并运行删除查询</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-774">Create and run a delete query</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/create-and-run-a-delete-query-6da65fe1-0fc7-4a64-8ef0-c052cd4c3ec5)

### <a name="business-apps-for-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-775">Business Apps for Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-775">Business Apps for Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-776">该部分介绍如何使用以下每个 Business Apps for Office 365 中的应用内功能对 DSR 请求作出响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-776">This section explains how to use the in-app functionality in each of the following Business Apps for Office 365 to respond to DSR requests.</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-777">Bookings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-777">Bookings</span></span>](#bookings)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-778">企业一览表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-778">Listings</span></span>](#listings)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-779">Connections</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-779">Connections</span></span>](#connections)

#### <a name="bookings"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-780">Bookings</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-780">Bookings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-781">以下各部分介绍如何使用 Microsoft Bookings 中的应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-781">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Bookings to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-782">此方法适用于独立 Bookings 应用，也适用于通过业务中心访问的 Bookings。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-782">This applies to both the standalone Bookings app and to Bookings when accessed through the Business center.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p239">Microsoft Bookings 允许在其组织中具有 Bookings 许可证的管理员和用户或员工设置预订页面，以便客户可以安排和更改约会、接收确认电子邮件、更新、取消和提醒电子邮件。Business 所有者及其员工还可以代表其客户使用 Bookings 预订事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p239">Microsoft Bookings allows administrators and users or staff, with a Bookings license in their organization, to set up booking pages so customers can schedule and make changes to appointments, receive confirmation emails, updates, cancellation, and reminders email. Business owners and their staff can also book events on behalf of their customers with Bookings.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-785">客户、管理员或员工可以创建以下类型的数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-785">The following types of data are created by customers, administrators, or staff:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-786">**客户、合作伙伴和好友的联系信息** - 此数据包含姓名、电话号码、电子邮件、地址和备注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-786">**Contact information of customers, partners, and friends** - This data contains name, phone number, email address, address, and notes.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-787">可以使用 Bookings Web、iOS 和 Android 客户端手动创建任何人的联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-787">Contacts for anyone can be manually created by using the Bookings Web, iOS, and Android clients.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-788">任何人的联系人都可以从 C1 的移动设备导入到使用 Bookings iOS 和 Android 客户端的 Bookings。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-788">Contacts for anyone can be imported from a C1's mobile device into Bookings with the Bookings iOS and Android clients.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-789">联系人也可以通过已预订的任何人的预订工作流在创建预订时自动创建，而不考虑预订是由用户代表客户创建的，还是由客户使用所有者的预订页面创建的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-789">Contacts are also auto-created at the time of booking creation through the booking workflow for anyone booked, whether the booking is created by a user on a customer's behalf or if it's created by the customer using the owner's booking page.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-790">**预订事件** - 预订事件是业务所有者或其指定员工与客户之间的会议，这些会议是业务所有者或客户通过业务所有者的公开预订页面创建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-790">**Booking events** - These are meetings between the business owner or their designated staff and a customer, which are created either by the business owner or the customer through the business owner's public booking page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-791">此数据包括姓名、地址、电子邮件地址、电话号码以及业务所有者在预订时从客户处收集的任何其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-791">This data includes name, address, email address, phone number, and any other info the business owner collects from the customer at the time of booking.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-792">**电子邮件确认/取消/更新** - 这些是系统生成和发送的与特定预订事件关联的电子邮件消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-792">**Email confirmations/cancellations/updates** - These are email messages generated and sent by the system in association with specific booking events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-793">这些消息包含预定交付相关服务的员工的相关信息，并包含业务所有者或客户在预订时输入的客户的相关个人信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-793">They contain personal data about the staff who is scheduled to deliver the relevant service and they contain personal data about the customer that was entered by either the business owner or the customer at the time of booking.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-794">所有客户内容都存储在托管组织 Bookings 的 Exchange Online 邮箱中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-794">All customer content is stored in the Exchange Online mailbox that hosts the organization's Bookings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-795">只要业务所有者和客户在服务中处于活动状态，就会保留该内容，除非他们明确要求删除数据或者离开服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-795">This content is retained for as long as the business owner and customer are active in the service, unless they explicitly request that the data be deleted or if they leave the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-796">该内容可通过产品内 UI、cmdlet 或通过删除相关预订邮箱进行删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-796">This content can be deleted with in-product UI, with a cmdlet, or through deletion of the relevant booking mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-797">一旦启动删除操作，数据将在业务所有者设置的时间段内被删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-797">Once the deleted action is initiated, the data is deleted within the time period set by the business owner.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-798">如果客户决定不再使用这些服务，将在 90 天后删除其客户内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-798">If a customer decides to leave the service, their customer contents is deleted after 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-799">有关在用户帐户删除后删除邮箱内容的详细信息，请参阅[删除 Exchange Online 数据](#removing-exchange-online-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-799">For more information about when mailbox content is deleted after a user account in deleted, see [Removing Exchange Online data](#removing-exchange-online-data).</span></span>

#### <a name="end-user-identifiable-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-800">最终用户身份信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-800">End User Identifiable Information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p244">最终用户可识别信息 (EUII) 包含有关在 Bookings 中安排的员工的个人信息和联系信息。当业务所有者设置 Bookings 并在设置后进行更新，该信息会被添加到员工详细信息页中。其中包含员工姓名、姓名缩写、电子邮件地址和电话号码。这些数据存储在托管 Bookings 的 Exchange Online 邮箱中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p244">End user Identifiable Information (EUII) includes personal and contact information about the staff that gets scheduled in Bookings. It's added to the Staff details pages when the business owner sets up Bookings and makes updates after the setup. It contains staff member's name, initials, email address, and phone number. This data is stored in the Exchange Online mailbox that hosts Bookings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p245">只要职员在服务中处于活动状态，便会保留数据，除非显式删除业务所有者或使用应用内 UI 的管理员或通过删除相关预订邮箱。当管理员开始删除员工的详细信息，或者员工离开服务，将根据业务所有者或管理员设置的 Exchange Online 邮箱的内容保留策略删除其详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p245">This data is retained for as long as the staff member is active in the service unless it's explicitly deleted the business owner or an admin using the in-app UI or by deleting the relevant booking mailbox. When the admin initiates the deletion of staff's details, or if the staff member leaves the service, their details are deleted in accordance with the Exchange Online mailbox's content retention policies set by the business owner or admin.</span></span>

##### <a name="discoveraccess"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-807">发现/访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-807">Discover/Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-808">Bookings 收集并将存储以下类型数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-808">Bookings gather and store the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-809">**公司档案信息：** 有关使用 Bookings 的业务的客户内容是通过 Bookings 的业务信息表单收集的，并且如果客户将 Bookings 与业务中心一起使用，该内容还将与业务中心的公司档案同步。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-809">**Business profile information:** Customer content about the business using Bookings is collected through the Bookings' Business information form and is synchronized with the Business Center Business Profile if a customer is using Bookings along with the Business center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-810">与此数据关联的唯一 EUII 是 C1 的电子邮件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-810">The only EUII associated with this data is an email address of the C1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-811">新的预订通知和更新电子邮件将发送到此地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-811">This address is where new booking notifications and update emails are sent.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-812">**客户联系人：** 可以在 Bookings Web、iOS 和 Android 版客户端中手动创建联系人，也可以从移动设备导入联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-812">**Customer contacts:** Contacts can be manually created in the Bookings Web, iOS, and Android clients, or they can be imported from a mobile device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-813">在使用自助预订页面期间，也会自动创建联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-813">Contacts are also automatically created during the use of the self-service booking page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-814">它们包含 EUII，并且存储在 Bookings 邮箱中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-814">They contain EUII and are stored in the Bookings mailbox.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-815">**员工详细信息：** 客户内容包括有关员工的数据，这些员工有资格交付通过 Bookings Web、iOS 或 Android 版客户端创建的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-815">**Staff details:** Customer content includes data about the staff that are eligible to deliver the services created from either the Bookings Web, iOS, or Android clients.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-816">员工详细信息可包含姓名、电子邮件地址和电话号码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-816">Staff details can contain name, email address, and phone number.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-817">**预订事件：** 这些事件是客户会议以及企业使用 Web 客户端或 Android/iOS 应用创建的相关客户内容，或者是客户使用公共预订页面（或 Facebook 页面）创建的客户内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-817">**Booking events:** These are customer meetings and related customer content created by the business using a Web client or Android/iOS app, or created by the customer using a public booking page (or a Facebook page).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-818">这些事件可包括姓名、地址、电子邮件地址、电话号码和约会详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-818">These events can include name, address, email address, phone number, and appointment details.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-819">**会议请求、电子邮件确认/取消/更新以及电子邮件提醒：** 这些是系统发送的与预订关联的电子邮件消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-819">**Meeting requests, email confirmations/cancellations/updates, and email reminders:** These are email messages sent by the system in association with bookings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-820">它们包含员工数据以及在预订时输入的客户数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-820">They contain staff data and customer data that was entered at time of booking.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-821">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-821">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-822">要导出对应于业务所有者、员工和客户的数据，可以使用 [业务中心隐私门户](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-822">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-823">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-823">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-824">可以删除以下类型的 Bookings 数据以响应 DSR 删除请求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-824">You can delete the following types of Bookings data in response to a DSR deleting request:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-825">**业务配置文件信息和联系人：** 你可以在管理中心中删除 Bookings 邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-825">**Business profile information and contacts:** You can delete the Bookings mailbox in the admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-826">删除邮箱后，你可以在 30 天内将其还原。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-826">After you delete the mailbox, you can restore it with 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-827">30 天后，该帐户及相应的邮箱将被永久删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-827">After 30 days, the account and the corresponding mailbox are permanently deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-828">有关删除用户帐户的详细信息，请参阅[删除用户](#deleting-a-user)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-828">For details about deleting a user account, see the section [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-829">**员工详细信息：** 你可以从 Bookings 仪表板中删除员工。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-829">**Staff details:** You can delete staff from the Bookings dashboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-830">若要永久删除员工，你可以删除其 Office 365 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-830">To permanently detail staff, you can delete their Office 365 account.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-831">**预订事件：** 你可以从 Bookings 日历中删除预订事件，这将移除客户的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-831">**Bookings events:** You can delete bookings events from the Bookings calendar, which will remove the customer's information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-832">**会议请求、电子邮件确认/取消/更新和电子邮件提醒：** 你可以从 Bookings 日历中删除这些内容，这将移除客户的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-832">**Meeting requests, email confirmations/cancellations/updates, and email reminders:** You can delete these from the Bookings calendar, which will remove the customer's information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-833">要导出对应于业务所有者、员工和客户的数据，可以使用 [业务中心隐私门户](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-833">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p253">此外，可以删除业务所有者和员工数据，可删除相应的用户帐户。请参阅[删除用户](#deleting-a-user)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p253">Additionally, you can delete business owner and staff data, you can delete the corresponding user account. See the section  [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user).</span></span>

#### <a name="listings"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-836">企业一览表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-836">Listings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-837">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft 企业一览表中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-837">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Listings to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-838">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-838">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-839">企业一览表所有者可以将其业务连接到 Google、必应、Yelp 和 Facebook 以查看评级和评论的聚合视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-839">Listings owner can connect their business to Google, Bing, Yelp, and Facebook to see an aggregated view of ratings and reviews.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-840">企业一览表收集并存储以下类型数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-840">Listings collect and store the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-841">Google 评论和评级</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-841">Google reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-842">必应评论和评级</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-842">Bing reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-843">Yelp 评论和评级</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-843">Yelp reviews and ratings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-844">Facebook 评论和评级</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-844">Facebook reviews and ratings</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-845">访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-845">Access</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-846">企业一览表所有者可以登录到企业一览表仪表板以查看自己的评论和评级。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-846">Listings owner can sign in to the Listings dashboard to see their reviews and ratings.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-847">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-847">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-848">要导出对应于业务所有者、员工和客户的数据，可以使用 [业务中心隐私门户](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-848">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-849">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-849">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p255">如果企业一览表所有者要删除其企业一览表信息，他们可以断开与企业一览表页面上提供商的连接。断开连接后，将删除其企业一览表信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p255">If a Listings owner would like to delete their Listings information, they can disconnect from the provider on the Listings page. After they disconnect, their Listings information will be deleted.</span></span>

#### <a name="connections"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-852">Connections</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-852">Connections</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-853">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Connections 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-853">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Connections to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-854">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-854">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-855">Connections 收集并将存储以下类型数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-855">Connections collect and store the following types of data:</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-856">客户/联系人是由企业使用 Web 客户端或移动应用（iOS、Android）创建的，或者向业务联系人发送电子邮件市场营销活动时使用应用创建而成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-856">Customers/contacts are created by the business using the web client or mobile app (iOS, Android), or by using the app when a business contact is sent an email marketing campaign.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-857">客户数据可包括姓名、地址、电子邮件地址和税务 ID 号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-857">Customer data can include name, address, email address, and tax ID numbers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-858">联系人在所有业务中心应用中共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-858">Contacts are shared across all Business center apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-859">客户可以在 Connections 注册页面上进行注册并保存其个人信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-859">Customers can sign up on the Connections sign-up page and save their personal information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-860">电子邮件营销活动中的链接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-860">Links from email campaigns</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-861">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-861">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-862">Connections 所有者可以登录到 Connections 仪表板并查看他们发送的电子邮件营销活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-862">A Connections owner can sign in to the Connections dashboard and see the email campaigns they've sent.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-863">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-863">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-864">要导出对应于业务所有者、员工和客户的数据，可以使用 [业务中心隐私门户](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-864">To export data corresponding to the business owner, staff and customers, you can use the [Business center privacy portal](https://businessaccount.microsoft.com/).</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-865">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-865">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p257">Connections 所有者发送电子邮件营销活动后，他们不能删除活动。如果他们想要删除任何草稿营销活动，可以登录到 Connections 仪表板并删除草稿营销活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p257">After a Connections owner sends an email campaign, they can't delete the campaign. If there are any draft campaigns they want to delete, they can sign in to the Connections dashboard and delete the draft campaigns.</span></span>

### <a name="education"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-868">教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-868">Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-869">该部分介绍如何使用以下 Microsoft 教育版应用中的应用内功能对 DSR 请求作出响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-869">This section explains how to use the in-app functionality of the following Microsoft Education apps to respond to DSR requests.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-870">作业</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-870">Assignments</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-871">课堂笔记本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-871">Class Notebook</span></span>

#### <a name="assignments"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-872">作业</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-872">Assignments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-873">以下各节介绍如何在作业中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-873">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Assignments to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

##### <a name="discoveraccess"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-874">发现/访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-874">Discover/Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p258">作业将存储教师和学生生成的信息。此信息中的某些内容存储在 SharePoint 中，而某些内容则存储在非 SharePoint 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p258">Assignments stores information that is generated both by teachers and students. Some of this information is store in SharePoint and some is stored in a non-SharePoint location.</span></span>

##### <a name="finding-assignments-data-stored-in-sharepoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-877">查找存储在 SharePoint 中的作业数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-877">Finding Assignments data stored in SharePoint</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p259">与提交作业相关的学生文件存储在一个文档库中（名为 **学生工作**），而与教师创建的作业相关的文件（可由学生访问）则存储在不同的文档库中（名为 **课堂文件**）。两个文档库都在相应的课堂团队 SharePoint 网站中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p259">Students files associated with a Submission for Assignment are stored in a document library (named **Student Work**) and files associated with Assignments that are created by teachers and (accessible by students) are stored in a different document library (named **Class Files**). Both document libraries are in the corresponding Class Team SharePoint site.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-880">管理员可使用安全与合规中心的内容搜索工具搜索与作业提交相关的学生文件（在“学生作业”和“课堂作业”库中）以及与作业相关的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-880">An admin can use the Content Search tool in the Security & Compliance Center to search for student files (in the Student Work and Class Files libraries) that are related to submissions on assignments and files related to assignments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-881">例如，管理员可搜索组织中的所有 SharePoint 网站，并在搜索查询中使用学生姓名和课程/作业名称，以查找与 DSR 请求相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-881">For example, an admin could search all SharePoint sites in the organization and use the student's name and class or assignment name in the search query to find data relevant to a DSR request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-882">同样，管理员可在与作业相关的教师文件中搜索教师分配给学生的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-882">Similarly, an admin can search for teacher files related to assignments for files that a teacher distributed to students.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-883">例如，管理员可搜索组织中的所有 SharePoint 网站，并在搜索查询中使用教师姓名和班级或作业名称来查找与 DSR 请求相关的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-883">For example, an admin could search all SharePoint sites in the organization and use the teacher's name and class or assignment name in the search query to find data relevant to a DSR request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-884">有关详细信息，请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-884">For more information, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-885">作业管理员文档</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-885">Assignments Admin Documentation</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-admin-documentation)
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-886">[使用内容搜索电子数据展示工具响应 DSR](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs)（在本指南中）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-886">[Using the Content Search eDiscovery tool to respond to DSRs](#using-the-content-search-ediscovery-tool-to-respond-to-dsrs) (in this guide)</span></span>

##### <a name="finding-assignments-data-not-stored-in-sharepoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-887">查找未存储在 SharePoint 中的作业数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-887">Finding Assignments data not stored in SharePoint</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-888">以下类型的作业数据未存储在课堂团队 SharePoint 网站中，因此无法使用内容搜索发现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-888">The following types of Assignments data are not stored in the class team SharePoint site, and therefore aren't discoverable by using Content Search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-889">此数据包含以下信息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-889">This data this includes the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-890">学生成绩和教师反馈</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-890">Student grades and feedback from the teacher</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-891">每个学生为作业提交的文档列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-891">The list of documents submitted for an assignment by each student</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-892">作业详细信息，如作业的截止日期</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-892">Assignment details, like the date the assignment is due</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p263">若要查找数据，管理员或教师必须访问课堂团队网站中的“作业”以查找可能与 DSR 请求相关的数据。管理员可以将自己作为所有者添加到课堂并查看该课堂团队的所有作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p263">To find data, an admin or a teacher would have to go into the Assignment in the Class Team site to find data that may be relevant to a DSR request. An admin can add themselves as an owner to the class and view all the assignments for that class team.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-895">即使学生不再是课堂成员，其数据仍然可能会出现在课堂中，并标记为“不再选修”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-895">Even if a student is no longer part of a class, their data might still be present in the class and marked as "no longer enrolled".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-896">本例中，提交 DSR 请求的学生必须向管理员提供已经正式选修的课程列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-896">In this case, a student submitting a DSR request would have to provide the admin the list of classes that they were formally enrolled it.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-897">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-897">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-898">对于特定学生注册参加的所有课程，可使用 PowerShell 脚本获取该学生的课程列表，然后使用 PowerShell 脚本导出其作业数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-898">You can export Assignments data for a specific student for all classes in which the student is enrolled by using a PowerShell script to get a list of classes for the student and then using a PowerShell script to export the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-899">请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-899">See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-900">配置 Teams 的作业</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-900">Configure Assignments for Teams</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/configure-assignments-for-teams)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-901">获取特定学生的课程列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-901">Get a list of classes for a specific student</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-get)
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-902">[从作业中导出学生和教师数据](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-export)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-902">[Export student and teacher data from Assignments](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-export)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p266">如果已从团队课堂网站删除学生，管理员可以在运行导出脚本之前将学生添加回网站。或者管理员可以使用脚本的输入文件来标识学生以往选修的每个课程。作业导出脚本还可用于导出教师有权访问的所有作业的提交数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p266">If the student has been removed from the Team Class site, the admin can add the student back to the site before running the export script. Or the admin can use the input file for the script to identify every class that the student was ever enrolled in. You can also use the Assignment export script to export submissions data for all assignments that a teacher has access to.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-906">Delete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-906">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-907">对于特定学生注册参加的所有课程，可使用 PowerShell 脚本获取该学生的课程列表，然后使用 PowerShell 脚本删除其作业数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-907">You can delete Assignments data for a specific student for all classes in which the student is enrolled by using a PowerShell script to get a list of classes for the student and then using a PowerShell script to delete the data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-908">应在从课程中删除学生之前执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-908">You should do this before you remove the student from the class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-909">请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-909">See:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-910">配置 Teams 的作业</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-910">Configure Assignments for Teams</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/configure-assignments-for-teams)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-911">获取特定学生的课程列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-911">Get a list of classes for a specific student</span></span>](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-get)
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-912">[从作业中删除学生数据](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-delete)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-912">[Delete student data from Assignments](/microsoft-365/education/deploy/assignments-script-delete)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p268">如果已从团队课堂网站删除学生，管理员可以在运行导出脚本之前将学生添加回网站。或者管理员可以使用脚本的输入文件来标识学生以往选修的每个课程。不能使用作业删除脚本删除教师数据，因为所有作业在课堂团队网站之间共享。作为替代方法，管理员必须将自己添加到课堂团队网站，然后删除特定作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p268">If the student has been removed from the Team Class site, the admin can add the student back to the site before running the export script. Or the admin can use the input file for the script to identify every class that the student was ever enrolled in. You can't use the Assignments deletion script to delete teacher data because all Assignments are shared across the Class Team site. As an alternative, an admin would have to add themselves to the Class Team site and then delete a specific Assignment.</span></span>

#### <a name="class-notebook"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-917">课堂笔记本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-917">Class Notebook</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-918">本指南前面讨论了在课堂笔记本中搜索内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-918">Searching for content in Class Notebook is discussed previously in this guide.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-919">请参阅 [OneNote 课堂笔记本](#onenote-class-notebook)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-919">See the [OneNote Class Notebook](#onenote-class-notebook) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-920">内容搜索工具还可用于从课堂笔记本中导出数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-920">You can also use the Content Search tool to export data from a Class Notebook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-921">或者，管理员或数据主体也可从课堂笔记本中导出数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-921">Alternatively, an admin or the data subject can export data from a Class Notebook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-922">请参阅[保存课堂笔记本副本](https://support.office.com/article/44733e18-0ef1-4d4b-be51-fc2ac5bfe9ec)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-922">See [Save a copy of a Class Notebook](https://support.office.com/article/44733e18-0ef1-4d4b-be51-fc2ac5bfe9ec).</span></span>

### <a name="flow"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-923">Flow</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-923">Flow</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-924">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Flow 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-924">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Flow to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-925">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-925">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p270">用户可以使用 Flow 来执行与数据相关的任务，例如同步应用程序之间的数据、将文件从某个 Office 365 服务复制到另一个，以及收集某个 Office 365 应用中的数据，并存储在另一个 Office 365 应用中。例如，用户可设置 Flow，以将 Outlook 电子邮件附件保存到其 OneDrive for Business 帐户。在此示例中，可使用内容搜索工具搜索用户邮箱中包含附件的电子邮件，或搜索 OneDrive for Business 帐户中的文件。在此示例中，可在通过 Flow 工作流连接的 Office 365 服务中发现由 Flow 处理的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p270">People can use Flow to perform data-related tasks such as synchronizing files between applications, copying files from one Office 365 service to another, and collecting data from one Office 365 app and storing it in another. For example, a user could set up a Flow to save Outlook email attachments to their OneDrive for Business account. In this example, you could use the Content Search tool to search the user's mailbox for the email message that contained the attachment or search their OneDrive for Business account for the file. This is an example where data handled by Flow might be discoverable in the Office 365 services connected by a Flow workflow.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p271">此外，用户还可使用 Flow 从 Office 365 复制文件或将文件上传到外部服务（如 Dropbox）。在这些情况下，有关外部服务中数据的 DSR 请求必须提交到外部服务，由其处理此类情景中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p271">Additionally, people can use Flow to copy or upload files from Office 365 to an external service, such as Dropbox. In these cases, a DSR request concerning the data in an external service would have to be submitted to the external service, who is processing the data in this type of scenario.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-932">如果管理员收到 DSR 请求，他们可将自己添加为用户流的所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-932">If an admin receives a DSR request, they can add themselves as an owner of a user's flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-933">这使管理员能够执行导出流定义、运行历史记录和执行流权限重新分配等功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-933">This enables an admin to perform functions including exporting flow definitions, running histories, and performing flow permission reassignments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-934">请参阅[在管理中心管理流](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/managing-flow-resources-in-the-admin-center/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-934">See [Manage Flows in the Admin Center](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/managing-flow-resources-in-the-admin-center/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-935">要将自己添加为 Flow 的所有者，管理员需要具有以下权限的帐户：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-935">An admin's ability to add themselves as an owner of a Flow requires an account with the following permissions:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-936">Flow/PowerApps 计划 2 许可证（付费或试用版）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-936">Flow/PowerApps Plan 2 license (paid or trial)</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-937">全局管理员\ </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-937">Global administrator\ </span></span>](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles)

    <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-938">或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-938">or</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-939">Azure Active Directory 全局管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-939">Azure Active Directory global administrator</span></span>](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles-azure-portal)

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-940">具有这些特权的管理员可使用 Flow 管理中心访问组织中的所有流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-940">Having these privileges enables the admin to use the Flow admin center to access all Flows in the organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-941">将自己添加为某个流的所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-941">To add yourself as an owner of a flow.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-942">转到 <https://admin.flow.microsoft.com></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-942">Go to <https://admin.flow.microsoft.com></span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-943">使用 Office 365 帐户登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-943">Sign in with your Office 365 credentials.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-944">在“**环境**”页面上，选择要访问的流的环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-944">On the **Environments** page, select the environment for the flows that you want to access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-945">组织具有一个默认环境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-945">organizations have a default environment.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-946">在所选环境的页面上，选择“**资源**”，然后选择“**流**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-946">On the page for the environment that you selected, select **Resources**, and then select **Flows.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-947">环境中所有流的列表随即显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-947">A list of all flows in the environment is displayed.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-948">选择要将自己添加为其成员的流对应的“**查看详细信息**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-948">select **View details** for the flow that you want to add yourself as a member.</span></span>
6. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-949">在“**所有者**”下，选择“**管理共享**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-949">Under **Owners**, select **Manage sharing**.</span></span>
7. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-950">在“**共享**”飞出控件上，将自己添加为成员，然后保存更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-950">On the **Share** flyout, add yourself as a member and then save the change.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-951">使自己成为所有者后，转到“**流**”\>“**我的流**”\>“**团队流**”以访问流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-951">After you make yourself an owner, go to **Flow** \> **My flows** \> **Team flows** to access the flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-952">可在其中下载运行历史记录或导出流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-952">From there, you can download the run history or export the flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-953">请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-953">See:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-954">[Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)（下载流运行历史记录）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-954">[Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-955">[Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)（通过打包导出和导入各环境中的流）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-955">[Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-956">访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-956">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-957">用户可以访问流的定义和运行历史记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-957">A user can access the definitions and run histories of their flows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-958">**流定义：** 用户可以导出流的定义（导出为 Flow 包，格式化为压缩文件中的 JSON）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-958">**Flow definitions:** A user can export the definition of a flow (which is exported as a Flow package, formatted as JSON in a zipped file).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-959">请参阅[通过打包导出和导入各环境中的流](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-959">See [Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-960">**流运行历史记录：** 用户可以下载其每个流的运行历史记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-960">**Flow run histories:** A user can download the run history of each of their flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-961">流运行历史记录下载为 CSV 文件，可在 Excel 中打开以进行筛选和搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-961">A flow run history is downloaded as a CSV file, which can be opened in Excel to filter or search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-962">用户还可以下载多个流的运行历史记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-962">Users can also download the run history of multiple flows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-963">请参阅[下载流运行历史记录](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-963">See [Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-964">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-964">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-965">管理员可在 Flow 管理中心将自己添加为用户流的所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-965">An admin can add themselves as an owner of a user's flows in the Flow admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-966">如果用户离开组织并且其 Office 365 帐户已被删除，将会保留他们是唯一所有者的流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-966">If a user leaves your organization and their Office 365 account is deleted, the flows that they are the sole owner of will be retained.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-967">这有助于组织为流切换新的所有者，并避免可能用于共享业务进程的流的相关业务出现任何中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-967">This is to help your organization transition the flows to new owners and avoid any disruption to your business for flows that may be used for shared business processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-968">然后，管理员需要确定是删除归该用户所有的流，还是重新分配给新的所有者，并采取行动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-968">An admin then needs to determine whether to delete the flows that were owned by the user or reassign to new owners, and take that action.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-969">对于共享流，从组织中删除用户时，将从所有者列表中删除其姓名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-969">For shared flows, when a user is deleted from your organization, their name is removed from the list of owners.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-970">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-970">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p279">管理员可以导出用户流的定义和运行历史记录。为此，管理员必须在 Flow 管理中心将自己添加为用户流的所有者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p279">An admin can export the definition and run history of a user's flows. To do this, an admin must add themselves as an owner of the user's flow in the Flow admin center</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-973">**流定义** - 管理员将自己添加为流的所有者后，可转到“**流**”\>“**我的流**”\>“**团队流**”导出流定义（导出为 Flow 包，格式化为压缩文件中的 JSON）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-973">**Flow definitions:** After an admin adds themselves as an owner of a flow, they can go to **Flow** \> **My Flows** \> **Teams flows** to export the flow definition (which is exported as a Flow package, formatted as JSON in a zipped file).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-974">请参阅[通过打包导出和导入各环境中的流](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-974">See [Export and import your flows across environments with packaging](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/import-export-bap-packages/).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-975">**流运行历史记录：** 同样，管理员必须将自己添加为某个流的所有者才可导出其流运行历史记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-975">**Flow run histories:** Similarly, an admin must add themselves as an owner of a Flow to export its flow run history.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-976">流运行历史记录下载为 CSV 文件，可在 Excel 中打开以进行筛选和搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-976">The Flow run history is downloaded as a CSV file, which means you can use Excel to filter or search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-977">还可以下载多个流的运行历史记录（只要具有所有权）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-977">You can also download the run history of multiple Flows, as long as you have ownership.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-978">请参阅[下载流运行历史记录](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-978">See [Download flow run history](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/download-history-recurrence/).</span></span>

#### <a name="connections-and-custom-connectors-in-flow"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-979">Flow 中的连接和自定义连接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-979">Connections and custom connectors in Flow</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-980">连接需要用户提供凭据才可连接到 API、SaaS 应用程序和自定义开发系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-980">Connections require users to provide credentials to connect to APIs, SaaS applications, and custom developed systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-981">这些连接归建立该连接的用户所有，并且可在产品内[管理](/flow/add-manage-connections)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-981">These connections are owned by the user that established the connection and can be [managed](/flow/add-manage-connections) in-product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-982">重新分配流后，管理员可使用 PowerShell cmdlet 列出这些连接，并在删除用户数据时删除这些连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-982">After Flows have been reassigned, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list and delete these connections as part of deleting user data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-983">使用自定义连接器，组织可通过连接到未提供现成连接器的系统来扩展流的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-983">Custom connectors allow organizations to extend the capabilities of Flow by connecting to systems where an out-of-box connector is not available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-984">自定义连接器作者可与组中的其他人[共享](/flow/register-custom-api)其连接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-984">A custom connector author can [share](/flow/register-custom-api) their connector with others in an organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-985">收到 DSR 删除请求后，管理员应考虑重新分配这些连接器的所有权，以避免业务中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-985">After receiving a DSR deleting request, an admin should consider reassigning ownership of these connectors to avoid business disruption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-986">要加快此流程，管理员可使用 PowerShell cmdlet 来列出、重新分配或删除自定义连接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-986">To expedite this process, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list, reassign, or delete custom connectors.</span></span>

### <a name="forms"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-987">Forms</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-987">Forms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-988">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Forms 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-988">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Forms to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-989">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-989">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p284">Forms 用户可以转到 <https://forms.office.com> 并选择“**我的表单**”，查看其创建的表单。他们也可以选择“**与我共享**”，查看他人通过链接共享的表单。如果有许多表单需要翻查，用户可以使用产品内搜索栏按标题或作者搜索表单。要确定 Microsoft Forms 是否可能包含响应 DSR 的个人数据，可以让数据主体搜索其“**与我共享**”列表，确定哪些用户（表单所有者）向数据主体发送了表单。然后，你可以让表单所有者选择顶部导航栏中的“**共享**”，并向你发送指向特定表单的链接，以便你可以查看该表单，并进一步确定其是否是响应 DSR 的材料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p284">Forms users can go to <https://forms.office.com> and select **My forms** to see the Forms they've created. They can also select **Shared with me** to view Forms others have shared via a link. If there are many Forms to sort through, users can use the in-product search bar to search for Forms by title or author. To determine whether Microsoft Forms is a place where personal data responsive to your DSR is likely to reside, you can ask the Data Subject to search his or her **Shared with me** list to determine which users ("Forms owners") have sent Forms to the Data Subject. You can then ask the forms owners to select **Share** in the top navigation bar and send you a link to a specific form so you can view it and further determine whether it is material to your DSR.</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-995">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-995">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-996">找到相关表单后，可通过单击“**响应**”选项卡访问对表单的响应。深入了解如何 [检查测验结果](https://support.microsoft.com/office/check-and-share-your-quiz-results-c4a9b45c-d62f-4eb7-b5db-ad81892c7c07)或 [表单结果](https://support.office.com/article/02859424-341d-406f-b32a-9a0fbaf357af)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-996">After the relevant Forms are found, you can access the responses to the Form by clicking the **Responses** tab. Learn more about how to [check your quiz results](https://support.microsoft.com/office/check-and-share-your-quiz-results-c4a9b45c-d62f-4eb7-b5db-ad81892c7c07) or [form results](https://support.office.com/article/02859424-341d-406f-b32a-9a0fbaf357af).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-997">要在 Excel 中查看响应结果，请选择“**响应**”选项卡，然后选择“**在 Excel 中打开**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-997">To review response results in Excel, select the **Responses** tab, and then select **Open in Excel**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-998">如果要向数据主体发送表单副本，可以对应用程序中以 RTF 格式显示的相关问题和解答进行屏幕截图，或向数据主体发送结果的 Excel 副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-998">If you would like to send the Data Subject a copy of the Form, you can either take screenshots of the relevant questions and answers that are in shown in the application in rich text format or send the Data Subject an Excel copy of the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-999">如果在使用 Excel，并且只想与数据主体共享部分调查结果，可先删除某些行或列，或修订剩余部分，然后再共享结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-999">If you are using Excel and would like to share with the Data Subject only portions of the survey result, you can delete certain rows or columns or redact the remaining sections before sharing the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1000">或者，可以转到 **“共享”\>“获取链接以复制”**（在“共享为模板”下），为数据主体提供整个表单的副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1000">Alternatively, you can go to **Share \> Get a link to duplicate** (under Share as a template) to provide the Data Subject with a replicate of the entire Form.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1001">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1001">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1002">所有者可以永久删除任何调查、测验、问卷或快速调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1002">Any survey, quiz, questionnaire, or poll can be permanently deleted by its owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1003">如果要接受 DSR 的“忘记我”并完全删除表单，请在表单列表中找到“表单”，在表单预览窗口的右上角选择一连串小圆点（省略号），然后选择“**删除**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1003">If you would like to honor a DSR "forget me" and delete a form in its entirety, find the Form in the list of forms, select the series of dots (ellipsis) in the upper right corner of the form preview window, and then select **Delete**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1004">表单删除后，将无法检索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1004">Once a Form is deleted, it can't be retrieved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1005">有关信息，请参阅[删除表单](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-form-2207e468-ce1b-4c4a-a256-caf631d87af0)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1005">For information, see [Delete a Form](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-form-2207e468-ce1b-4c4a-a256-caf631d87af0).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1006">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1006">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1007">要导出表单问题并响应 Excel 文件，请打开表单，选择“**响应**”选项卡，然后选择“**在 Excel 中打开**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1007">To export form questions and responses to an Excel file, open the form, select the **Responses** tab, and then select **Open in Excel**.</span></span>

### <a name="kaizala"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1008">Kaizala</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1008">Kaizala</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1009">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Kaizala 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1009">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Kaizala to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1010">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1010">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p287">用户的组织数据，也就是在组织组中共享的数据，可由管理员通过 Kaizala 管理门户进行访问。组织数据会根据组织的保留策略保留一段时间。除了用户数据，Kaizala 服务器还存储以下类型的组织数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p287">A user's organizational data, which is data that is shared in organizational groups, can be accessed by an admin from the Kaizala management portal. Organizational data is retained for a duration of time determined by your organization's retention policies. In addition to user data, Kaizala servers also store the following types of organizational data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1014">组织组一部分的成员列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1014">List of members who are part of the organization's groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1015">组织组消息数据，它们是跨组织组共享的消息和响应</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1015">Organization group messages data, which are messages and responses shared across organizational groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1016">组织中的用户列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1016">A list of users in the organizations</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1017">为组织中所有用户捕获的产品和服务使用情况数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1017">Product and service usage data captured for all users in the organization.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1018">组织创建的 Kaizala 操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1018">Kaizala Actions created by the organization</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1019">Kaizala 连接器数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1019">Kaizala connectors data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p288">用户的消费者数据可由数据主体通过 Kaizala 移动应用进行访问以获取消费者数据。消费者数据包括以下类型的数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p288">A user's consumer data can be accessed by the data subject using the Kaizala mobile app for consumer data. Consumer data includes the following types of data:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1022">Kaizala 上的专用组数据（存储在 Kaizala 服务器长达 90 天）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1022">Data belonging to private groups on Kaizala (stored on Kaizala servers for 90 days)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1023">用户个人资料信息，以及用户联系人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1023">A user's profile information and the user's contacts</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1024">和用户同组的成员列表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1024">List of members who are part of the same groups as the user</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1025">在组间共享的组消息和响应</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1025">Group messages and responses shared across groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1026">用户的联系人列表（存储在 Kaizala 服务上）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1026">The user's contact list (stored on Kaizala service)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1027">由 Kaizala 用户所执行的事务（仅适用于印度的 Kaizala 用户）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1027">Transactions made by the user on Kaizala (applies to Kaizala users in India only)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1028">用户的产品和服务使用情况数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1028">Product and service usage data for the user</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1029">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1029">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1030">Kaizala 用户可以转到其移动设备，查看在设备上创建的 Kaizala 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1030">Kaizala users can go to their mobile device to see Kaizala content they've created on their device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1031">若要确定响应 DSR 的个人数据是否有可能驻留在 Kaizala 移动应用中，可以要求数据主体搜索其 Kaizala 应用以获取所需的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1031">To determine whether Kaizala mobile apps are a place where personal data responsive to a DSR is likely to reside, you can ask the data subject to search their Kaizala app for the requested information.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1032">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1032">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p290">当组织中的用户使用 Kaizala ，将生成消费者数据，如果用户参与组织组，还可能生成组织数据。管理员可以从 Kaizala 管理门户导出用户的组织数据。Kaizala 消费者用户可以将其私有数据从 Kaizala 移动应用中导出。在这两种情况下，请注意，当管理员或用户导出 Kaizala 数据时，还将导出产品和服务使用情况数据。有关详细信息，请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p290">When users in your organization use Kaizala, consumer data is generated, and organizational data may be generated if the user participates in an organization group. Admins can export a user's organizational data from the Kaizala management portal. Kaizala consumer users can export their private data from the Kaizala mobile app. In both cases, note that product and service usage data is also export when an admin or user exports Kaizala data. For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1038">导出或删除 Kaizala 中的用户组织数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1038">Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1039">导出或删除 Kaizala 移动应用中的数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1039">Export or delete your data in the Kaizala mobile app</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-your-data)

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1040">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1040">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p291">Kaizala 管理员可以在 Kaizala 管理门户中删除 Kaizala 用户的帐户。在删除用户帐户后，将从属于你组织的所有组中删除用户，同时从其设备中删除组织数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p291">A Kaizala admin can remove a Kaizala user's account in the Kaizala management portal. After a user account is deleted, the user is removed from all groups that belong to your organization and organizational data is deleted from their device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p292">若要从用户的移动设备中删除所有私有数据，Kaizala 用户可以删除其 Kaizala 帐户。在删除帐户后，包括聊天、照片和其他数据在内的所有相关 Kaizala 内容都将从设备中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p292">To remove all private data from the user's mobile device, the Kaizala user can delete their Kaizala account. After the account is deleted, all related Kaizala content including, chats, photos, and other data will be deleted from the device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1045">有关详细信息，请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1045">For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1046">导出或删除 Kaizala 中的用户组织数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1046">Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1047">导出或删除 Kaizala 移动应用中的数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1047">Export or delete your data in the Kaizala mobile app</span></span>](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-your-data)

### <a name="planner"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1048">规划器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1048">Planner</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1049">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Planner 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1049">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Planner to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1050">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1050">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1051">Planner 计划与 Microsoft 365 组关联，而 Microsoft 365 组的文件存储在组的关联 SharePoint Online 网站中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1051">Planner plans are associated with a Microsoft 365 Group, and the files for Microsoft 365 Groups are stored in an associated SharePoint Online site for the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1052">这意味可以使用内容搜索，通过搜索网站中的 Microsoft 365 组来查找 Planner 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1052">That means that you can use Content Search to find Planner files by searching the site for the Microsoft 365 Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1053">要执行此操作，需要有 Microsoft 365 组的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1053">To do this, you need to have the URL for the Microsoft 365 Group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1054">请参阅“Office 365 中的内容搜索”帮助主体中的[搜索 Microsoft Teams 和 Microsoft 365 组](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search)，了解有关获取 Microsoft 365 组相关信息的提示，了解如何在对应的 SharePoint Online 网站中搜索 Planner 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1054">See [Searching Microsoft Teams and Microsoft 365 Groups](/microsoft-365/compliance/content-search) in the "Content Search in Office 365" help topic for tips about getting information about Microsoft 365 Groups to help you search for Planner files in the corresponding SharePoint Online site.</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1055">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1055">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1056">如前所述，你可以搜索基础 SharePoint Online 网站和与计划关联的邮箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1056">As previously explained, you can search the underlying SharePoint Online site and mailbox that are associated with a plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1057">然后，你可以预览或下载相关搜索结果来访问数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1057">Then you can preview or download the related search results to access data.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1058">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1058">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p295">可通过为自己提供访问用户所属计划的权限或以用户身份登录进行更改，手动删除用户的个人信息。请参阅[删除 Microsoft Planner 中的用户数据](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-in-microsoft-planner-4349ded2-1891-4896-8e27-05fd40f3929f)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p295">You can manually delete a user's personally information by either giving yourself permissions to access the plans the user is part of or signing in as the user to make the changes. See [Delete user data in Microsoft Planner](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-in-microsoft-planner-4349ded2-1891-4896-8e27-05fd40f3929f).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1061">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1061">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p296">可使用 PowerShell 脚本从 Planner 导出用户数据。导出数据时，针对用户所属的每个计划导出单独的 JSON 文件。请参阅[从 Microsoft Planner 导出用户数据](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-microsoft-planner-91258c96-b353-4da1-b6d9-d78e4809cf08)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p296">You can use a PowerShell script to export a user's data from Planner. When you export the data, a separate JSON file is export for each plan that the user is a part of. See [Export user data from Microsoft Planner](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-microsoft-planner-91258c96-b353-4da1-b6d9-d78e4809cf08).</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1065">Power BI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1065">Power BI</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1066">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Power BI 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1066">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Power BI to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1067">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1067">Discover</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p297">可以在 Power BI 的不同工作区中搜索内容，包括仪表板、报表、工作簿和数据集。每种类型的工作区都包含一个搜索字段，可以使用它来搜索该工作区。请参阅[在 Power BI 服务中搜索、查找和排序内容](/power-bi/service-navigation-search-filter-sort)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p297">You can search for content in the different workspaces in Power BI, including dashboards, reports, workbooks, and datasets. Each type of workspace contains a search field that you can use to search that workspace. See [Searching, finding, and sorting content in Power BI service](/power-bi/service-navigation-search-filter-sort).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1071">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1071">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1072">可在 Power BI 中打印仪表板、报表以及报表中的视觉对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1072">You can print dashboards, reports, and visuals from reports in Power BI to produce a physical copy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1073">无法打印整个报表；一次只能打印一页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1073">You can't print entire reports; you can only print one page at a time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1074">为此，请转到报表，使用搜索字段查找特定数据，然后打印该页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1074">To do this, go to a report, use the search field to find specific data, and then print that page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1075">请参阅[从 Power BI 服务打印](/power-bi/service-print)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1075">See [Printing from Power BI service](/power-bi/service-print).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1076">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1076">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1077">要删除仪表板、报表和工作簿，请参阅[删除 Power BI 服务中的几乎任何内容](/power-bi/service-delete)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1077">To delete dashboards, reports, and workbooks, see [Delete almost anything in Power BI service](/power-bi/service-delete).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p299">删除仪表板、报表或工作簿不会删除基础数据集。由于 Power BI 依赖与基础源数据的实时连接来保持完整性和准确性，因此删除个人数据必须在基础源数据中进行。（例如，如果创建的 Power BI 报表连接到实时数据源 Dynamics 365 for Sales，则任何数据更正都必须针对 Dynamics 365 for Sales 中的数据进行。）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p299">Deleting a dashboard, report, or workbook doesn't delete the underlying dataset. Because Power BI relies on a live connection to the underlying source data to be complete and accurate, deleting personal data must be done there. (For example, if you created a Power BI report that is connected to Dynamics 365 for Sales as the live data source, you would have to make any corrections to the data in Dynamics 365 for Sales.)</span></span>
