<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1081">删除数据之后，可以使用 Power BI 中的[计划的数据刷新](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh)功能来更新存储在 Power BI 中的数据集，之后，已删除的数据不会再反映在任何之前利用了该数据的 Power BI 报表或仪表板中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1081">After the data is deleted, you can use the [scheduled data refresh](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh) capabilities in Power BI to update the dataset that is stored in Power BI, after which the deleted data will no longer be reflected in any Power BI reports or dashboards that used that data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1082">为帮助符合 GDPR 要求，应该制定相应的策略，确保按照适当的节奏刷新数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1082">To help comply with GDPR requirements, you should have policies in place to ensure that you are refreshing your data at an appropriate cadence.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1083">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1083">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1084">为了推进数据移植请求，可导出 Power BI 中的仪表板和报表：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1084">To facilitate a data portability request, you can export dashboards and reports in Power BI:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p301">可将仪表板和报表的基础数据导出到静态 Excel 文件。请参阅[从 Power BI 服务打印](/power-bi/service-print)中的视频。然后，可使用 Excel 编辑要包括在移植请求中的个人数据，并将其另存为常用的计算机可读格式，如 .csv 或 .xml。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p301">You can export the underlying data for dashboards and reports to a static Excel file. See the video in [Printing from Power BI service](/power-bi/service-print). Using Excel, you can then edit the personal data to be included in the portability request, and save it in a commonly used, machine-readable format such as .csv or .xml.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p302">如果 Power BI 服务中的报表最初是使用 Power BI Desktop 发布的，那么可在 Office 365 中将该报表导出（下载）到 .pbix 文件。然后，可将此文件导入 Power BI Desktop，并发布（导出）到另一组织的 Power BI 服务。请参阅[将 Power BI 服务中的报表导出到桌面](/power-bi/service-export-to-pbix)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p302">You can export (download) a report from the Power BI service in Office 365 to a .pbix file if it was originally published using Power BI Desktop. You can then import this file to Power BI Desktop and publish (export) it to the Power BI service of another organization. See [Export a report from Power BI service to Desktop](/power-bi/service-export-to-pbix).</span></span>

### <a name="powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1091">PowerApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1091">PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1092">以下各节介绍了如何在 Microsoft PowerApps 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1092">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Power Apps to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1093">这些步骤概述了管理员可如何为应用和依赖资源切换新的所有者，以减少业务中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1093">These steps outline how an admin can transition apps and their dependent resources to new owners to limit business disruption.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1094">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1094">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1095">PowerApps 是一项服务，可用于生成可在组织内共享和使用的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1095">PowerApps is a service for building apps that can be shared and used within your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1096">在生成或运行应用的过程中，用户最终将在 PowerApps 服务中存储多种类型的资源和数据，包括应用、环境、连接、自定义连接器以及权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1096">As a part of the process of building or running an app, a user ends up storing several types of resources and data in the PowerApps service, including apps, environments, connections, custom connectors, and permissions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1097">为了帮助推进与 PowerApps 相关的 DSR 请求，可利用在 [PowerApps 管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)和 [PowerApps 管理员 PowerShell cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804) 中公开的管理操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1097">To help facilitate a DSR request related to PowerApps, you can use the administration operations exposed in the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) and [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1098">访问这些工具需要具有以下权限的帐户：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1098">Access to these tools requires an account with the following permissions:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1099">PowerApps 计划 2 付费证或 PowerApps 计划 2 试用版许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1099">A paid PowerApps Plan 2 license or a PowerApps Plan 2 trial license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1100">可在[此处](https://web.powerapps.com/trial)注册 30 天的试用版许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1100">You can sign up for a 30-day trial license [here](https://web.powerapps.com/trial).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1101">[全局管理员](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles)或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1101">[Global administrator](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/assign-admin-roles) or</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1102">Azure Active Directory 全局管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1102">Azure Active Directory global administrator</span></span>](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles-azure-portal)

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1103">有关查找个人数据的详细信息，请参阅[发现 PowerApps 个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871880)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1103">For more information about finding personal data, see [Discover PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871880).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1104">PowerApps 服务还包括 Common Data Service For Apps，可让用户在 Common Data Service 数据库的标准和自定义实体中存储数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1104">The PowerApps service also includes the Common Data Service For Apps, which enables users to store data in standard and custom entities within a Common Data Service database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1105">可从 [PowerApps 生成器门户](https://web.powerapps.com)查看存储在这些实体中的数据，并使用[高级查找](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search)的产品内搜索功能搜索实体中的特定数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1105">You can view the data stored in these entities from the [PowerApps Maker portal](https://web.powerapps.com), and use the in-product search capabilities of [Advanced Find](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search) to search for specific data in the entity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1106">有关发现 Common Data Service 中的个人数据的详细信息，请参阅[发现 Common Data Service 个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871881)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1106">For more information around discovering personal data in the Common Data Service, see [Discover Common Data Service personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871881).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1107">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1107">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1108">管理员能够使用 [PowerApps 管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)或 [PowerApps 管理员 PowerShell cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804) 为自己分配访问和运行应用以及关联资源（包括流、连接和自定义连接器）的特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1108">Admins have the ability to assign themselves privileges to access and run the apps and associated resources (including flows, connections, and custom connectors) using the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) or [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p308">具有访问用户应用的权限后，可以使用 Web 浏览器打开该应用。打开应用后，可对数据进行屏幕截图。请参阅[在 Web 浏览器中使用 PowerApps](/powerapps/run-app-browser)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p308">After you have access to the user's app, you can use a web browser to open the app. After you open an app, you can take a screenshot of the data. See [Use PowerApps in a web browser](/powerapps/run-app-browser).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1112">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1112">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1113">由于 PowerApps 允许用户生成对组织日常运营至关重要的业务线应用，因此，当有用户离开了组织，并且其 Office 365 帐户被删除时，管理员需要确定是要删除归该用户所有的应用，还是仅重新分配给新的所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1113">Because PowerApps allow users to build line-of-business application that can be a critical part of your organization's day-to-day operations, when a user leaves your organization and their Office 365 account is deleted, the admin needs to determine whether to delete the apps owned by the user or reassign to new owners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1114">这有助于组织为应用切换新的所有者，并避免可能用于共享业务的应用流程的相关业务出现任何中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1114">This is to help your organization transition apps to new owners and avoid any disruption to your business for apps that may be used for shared business processes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1115">对于共享数据（如应用），管理员必须确定是要永久删除该用户的共享数据，还是要通过将数据重新分配给自己或组织中的其他人来保留这些数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1115">For shared data, like apps, admins must decide whether to permanently delete that user's shared data or keep them by reassigning the data to themselves or someone else within their organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1116">请参阅[删除 PowerApps 个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1116">See [Delete PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p311">对于用户存储在 Common Data Service For Apps 数据库的实体中的任何数据，管理员也需要使用产品内功能进行审阅和删除（如果需要）。请参阅[删除 Common Data Service 用户个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871886)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p311">Any data that was stored by a user in an entity in a Common Data Service For Apps database will also need to be reviewed and (if desired) deleted by an admin using the in-product capabilities. See [Delete Common Data Service user personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871886).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1119">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1119">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p312">管理员能够使用 [PowerApps 管理中心](https://admin.powerapps.com/)和 [PowerApps 管理员 PowerShell cmdlet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804) 导出 PowerApps 服务中存储的用户个人数据。请参阅[导出 PowerApps 个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p312">Admins have the ability to export personal data stored for a user within the PowerApps service using the [PowerApps Admin Center](https://admin.powerapps.com/) and [PowerApps Admin PowerShell cmdlets](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871804). See [Export PowerApps personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871883).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p313">此外，还可以使用[高级查找](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search)的产品内搜索功能搜索任何实体中的用户个人数据。有关导出 Common Data Service 中的个人数据的详细信息，请参阅[导出 Common Data Service 个人数据](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871889)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p313">You can also use the in-product search capabilities of [Advanced Find](/dynamics365/customer-engagement/basics/save-advanced-find-search) to search for a user's personal data in any entity. For details about exporting personal data in the Common Data Service, see [Export Common Data Service personal data](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=871889).</span></span>

#### <a name="connections-and-custom-connectors-in-powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1124">PowerApps 中的连接和自定义连接器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1124">Connections and custom connectors in PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1125">连接需要用户提供凭据才可连接到 API、SaaS 应用程序和自定义开发系统。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1125">Connections require users to provide credentials to connect to APIs, SaaS applications, and custom developed systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1126">这些连接归建立该连接的用户所有，并且可在产品内[管理](/powerapps/maker/canvas-apps/add-data-connection)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1126">These connections are owned by the user that established the connection and can be [managed](/powerapps/maker/canvas-apps/add-data-connection) in-product.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1127">重新分配 PowerApps 后，管理员可使用 PowerShell cmdlet 列些连出这接，并在删除用户数据时删除这些连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1127">After PowerApps have been reassigned, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list and delete these connections as part of deleting user data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1128">使用自定义连接器，组织可通过连接到未提供现成连接器的系统来扩展 PowerApps 的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1128">Custom connectors allow organizations to extend the capabilities of PowerApps by connecting to systems where an out-of-box connector is not available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1129">自定义连接器作者可与组中的其他人[共享](/connectors/custom-connectors/use-custom-connector-powerapps)其连接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1129">A custom connector author can [share](/connectors/custom-connectors/use-custom-connector-powerapps) their connector with others in an organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1130">收到 DSR 删除请求后，管理员应考虑重新分配这些连接器的所有权，以避免业务中断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1130">After receiving a DSR deleting request, an admin should consider reassigning ownership of these connectors to avoid business disruption.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1131">要加快此流程，管理员可使用 PowerShell cmdlet 来列出、重新分配或删除自定义连接器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1131">To expedite this process, an admin can use PowerShell cmdlets to list, reassign, or delete custom connectors.</span></span>

### <a name="project-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1132">Project Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1132">Project Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1133">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Project Online 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1133">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Project Online to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover-and-access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1134">发现和访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1134">Discover and access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1135">可使用内容搜索来搜索与某个项目关联的 SharePoint Online 网站（首次创建项目时，可选择创建关联的 SharePoint Online 网站）；内容搜索不会搜索 Project Online 中实际项目包含的数据，只会搜索关联的网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1135">You can use Content Search to search the SharePoint Online site that's associated with a Project (when a Project is first created, there's an option to create an associated SharePoint Online site); Content Search doesn't search the data in an actual project in Project Online, only the associated site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1136">尽管内容搜索将搜索有关项目的元数据（如主题中提及的人员），但是，这可能有助于查找（和访问）包含 DSR 相关数据的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1136">Though Content Search searches for metadata about projects such as people mentioned in the subject) However, this may help you find (and access) the Project that contains the data related to the DSR.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p317">组织中与项目关联的网站所属的网站集的 URL 为 `https://<your org>.sharepoint.com/sites/pwa`；例如，**<https://contoso.sharepoint.com/pwa>**。可以使用此特定网站集作为内容搜索位置，然后作为搜索查询中项目的名称。此外，IT 管理员可在 SharePoint 管理中心使用“网站集”页面来获取组织中的 PWA 网站集列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p317">The URL for the site collection in your organization where sites associated with Projects is `https://<your org>.sharepoint.com/sites/pwa`; for example, **<https://contoso.sharepoint.com/pwa>**. You can use this specific site collection as the location of your content search and then the name of the Project in the search query. Additionally, an IT admin can use the Site Collections page in the SharePoint admin center to get a list of PWA site collections in the organization.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1140">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1140">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p318">可从 Project Online 环境删除有关用户的信息。请参阅[从 Project Online 删除用户数据](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-from-project-online-252fa593-9c25-47ed-b861-643fe8bf1cb7)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p318">You can delete information about a user from your Project Online environment. See [Delete user data from Project Online](https://support.office.com/article/delete-user-data-from-project-online-252fa593-9c25-47ed-b861-643fe8bf1cb7).</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1143">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1143">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p319">可从 Project Online 环境导出特定用户的内容。此数据以 JSON 格式导出到多个文件。有关分步说明，请参阅[从 Project Online 导出用户数据](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-project-online-27f3838d-3dbe-4b98-80dc-df55f851154d)。有关所导出文件的详细信息，请参阅 [Project Online 导出 JSON 对象定义](https://support.office.com/article/project-online-export-json-object-definitions-ce5faeae-9af4-4696-b847-a1f4f20327c7)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p319">You can a specific user's content from your Project Online environment. This data is exported to multiple files in the JSON format. For step-by instructions see, [Export user data from Project Online](https://support.office.com/article/export-user-data-from-project-online-27f3838d-3dbe-4b98-80dc-df55f851154d). For detailed information about the files that are exported, see [Project Online export json object definitions](https://support.office.com/article/project-online-export-json-object-definitions-ce5faeae-9af4-4696-b847-a1f4f20327c7).</span></span>

### <a name="publisher"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1148">Publisher</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1148">Publisher</span></span>

  - [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1158">使用 Publisher 将出版物另存为或转换为 .pdf 或 .xps </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1158">Save As or convert a publication to .pdf or .xps using Publisher</span></span>](https://support.microsoft.com/office/save-as-or-convert-a-publication-to-pdf-or-xps-using-publisher-657332d0-d2c2-464a-9870-e9b3d22e6469)

### <a name="stream"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1167">Stream</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1167">Stream</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1168">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Stream 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1168">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Stream to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1169">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1169">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1170">若要发现可能与数据主体请求相关的生成或上传到 Stream 的内容，Stream 管理员可以运行用户报表，以确定 Stream 用户可能上传、创建或由用户发布的视频、视频说明、组、频道或评论。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1170">To discover content that is generated or uploaded to Stream that may be relevant to a data subject request, a Stream admin can run a user report to determine what videos, video descriptions, groups, channels, or comments a Stream user may have uploaded, created, or posted by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1171">有关如何生成报表的说明，请参阅[管理 Microsoft Stream 中的用户数据](/stream/managing-user-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1171">For instructions on how to generate a report, see [Managing user data in Microsoft Stream](/stream/managing-user-data).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1172">报表输出采用 HTML 格式，并且包含可用于导航到可能感兴趣的视频的超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1172">The report output is in HTML format and contains hyperlinks that can be used to navigate to videos of potential interest.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1173">如果想要查看已设置自定义权限的视频而你不是视频原始用户的成员，可在管理员模式下查看，请参阅 [Microsoft Stream 中的管理员功能](/stream/manage-content-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1173">If you would like to view a video that has custom permission set and you are not part of the original users for whom the video was intended, you can view in admin mode, See [Admin capabilities in Microsoft Stream](/stream/manage-content-permissions).</span></span>  

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1174">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1174">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p325">根据数据主体请求的性质，上文所述的报告副本可用于帮助满足数据主体请求。用户报告包括 Stream 用户的姓名和唯一 ID、用户上传的视频列表、用户有权访问的视频列表、用户创建的频道列表、用户所属的所有组列表，以及用户在视频上留下的所有评论列表。该报告进一步显示了用户是否查看了用户报告中列出的每个视频。如果想要为数据主体提供对视频的访问权限以满足 DSR 请求，可以共享该视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p325">Depending on the nature of the data subject request, a copy of the report described above can be used help satisfy a data subject request. The user report includes the Stream user's name and unique ID, a list of videos the user uploaded, a list of videos the user has access to, a list of channels the user created, a list of all the groups the user is a member of, and a list of all comments the user left on videos. The report further shows whether the user viewed each video listed in the user report. If you would like to provide the data subject with access to a video to satisfy a DSR request, you can share the video.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1179">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1179">Export</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1181">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1181">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p326">若要删除或编辑视频或任何其他 Stream 内容，Stream 管理员可以在管理员模式下选择视图来执行必要的功能。请参阅 [Microsoft Stream 中的管理员功能](/stream/manage-content-permissions)。如果某个用户离开了组织并且希望删除其名称使其不再在他们上传的视频旁边出现，可以删除其名称或将其替换为另一个名称。请参阅[管理 Microsoft Stream 中已删除的用户](/stream/managing-deleted-users)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p326">To delete or edit videos or any other Stream content, a Stream admin can select view in admin mode to perform the necessary function. See [Admin capabilities in Microsoft Stream](/stream/manage-content-permissions). If a user has left the organization and would like to have their name removed from appearing next to videos that they uploaded, you can remove their name or replace it with another. See [Managing deleted users in Microsoft Stream](/stream/managing-deleted-users).</span></span>

### <a name="whiteboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1202">Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1202">Whiteboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1203">以下各部分介绍如何在 Microsoft Whiteboard 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1203">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Whiteboard to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1204">Surface Hub 上的 Whiteboard 2016</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1204">Whiteboard 2016 on Surface Hub</span></span>](#whiteboard-2016-on-surface-hub)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1205">所有其他平台上的 Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1205">Whiteboard on all other platforms</span></span>](#whiteboard-for-pc-surface-hub-and-other-platforms)

#### <a name="whiteboard-2016-on-surface-hub"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1206">Surface Hub 上的 Whiteboard 2016</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1206">Whiteboard 2016 on Surface Hub</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1207">本部分介绍如何响应对使用 Surface Hub 上的内置 Whiteboard 2016 应用创建的数据的 DSR 请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1207">This section describes responding to DSR requests for data created using the built-in Whiteboard 2016 app on Surface Hub.</span></span>

##### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1208">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1208">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p330">Whiteboard 文件（.wbx 文件）存储在用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户中。可以询问数据主体或其他用户有关他们创建的白板是否可能包含响应 DSR 请求的个人数据。他们可以与你共享白板，你也可以获取其副本以提供给数据主体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p330">Whiteboard files (.wbx files) are stored in users' OneDrive for Business account. You can ask the data subject or other users if whiteboards they created may contain personal data responsive to a DSR request. They can share a whiteboard with you, or you can get a copy of it to give to the data subject.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1212">若要访问和转移白板：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1212">To access and transfer whiteboards:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p331">自行访问用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户。请参阅[获取对前用户数据的访问权限并备份该数据](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)中的“获取对前员工 OneDrive for Business 文档的访问权限”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p331">Give yourself access to the user's OneDrive for Business account. See the "Get access to the former employee's OneDrive for Business documents" section in [Get access to and back up a former user's data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data).</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1215">转到用户 OneDrive for Business 帐户中的“Whiteboard 应用数据”文件夹，并复制想要转移的白板的 .wbx 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1215">Go to the Whiteboard App Data folder in the user's OneDrive for Business account and copy the .wbx files of the whiteboards that you want to transfer.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1216">自行访问数据主体的 OneDrive for Business 帐户，然后转至“Whiteboard 应用数据”文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1216">Give yourself access to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account, and then go to Whiteboard App Data folder.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1217">粘贴上一步中复制的 .wbx 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1217">Paste the .wbx files that you copied in the previous step.</span></span>

##### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1218">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1218">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1219">如果在对 DSR 访问请求作出响应的白板中发现了个人数据，则可以以多种方式提供数据主体对白板的访问：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1219">If you find personal data in a whiteboard that's responsive to a DSR access request, you can provide the data subject access to a whiteboard in several ways:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1220">获取白板相关部分的屏幕截图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1220">Take screenshots of the relevant portions of a whiteboard.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p332">将 .wbx 文件副本上传到数据主体的 OneDrive for Business 帐户。有关访问和转移 .wbx 文件的步骤，请参阅上一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p332">Upload a copy of the .wbx file to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account. See the previous section for steps on accessing and transferring .wbx files.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1223">将白板副本导出为 .png 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1223">Export a copy of whiteboard as a .png file.</span></span>

##### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1224">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1224">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1225">如果已获得白板副本，可以将其导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1225">If you've obtained a copy of a whiteboard, you can export it.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1226">在 Surface Hub 上启动 Whiteboard。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1226">Launch Whiteboard on the Surface Hub.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p333">点击“共享”按钮，然后选择“导出副本”。可以将白板导出为 OneNote (.one) 文件或图像 (.png) 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p333">Tap the Share button and then select Export a copy. You can export a whiteboard to a OneNote (.one) file or to an image (.png) file.</span></span>

##### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1229">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1229">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1230">可以自行访问用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户，然后删除白板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1230">You can give yourself access to the user's OneDrive for Business account and then delete the whiteboards.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p334">自行访问数据主体的 OneDrive for Business 帐户。请参阅[获取对前用户数据的访问权限并备份该数据](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)中的“获取对前员工 OneDrive for Business 文档的访问权限”部分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p334">Give yourself access to the data subject's OneDrive for Business account. See the "Get access to the former employee's OneDrive for Business documents" section in [Get access to and back up a former user's data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data)</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1233">请转到“Whiteboard 应用数据”文件夹，然后删除此文件夹的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1233">Go to the Whiteboard App Data folder and then delete the contents of this folder.</span></span>

#### <a name="whiteboard-for-pc-surface-hub-and-other-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1234">适用于电脑、Surface Hub 和其他平台的 Whiteboard</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1234">Whiteboard for PC, Surface Hub, and other platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p335">如果管理员收到对新 Whiteboard 应用中的数据的 DSR 请求，他们可以使用 Whiteboard PowerShell 将自己（或其他用户）添加为用户白板的所有者。这样可以使管理员执行访问、导出和删除白板等操作。使用 **Set-WhiteboardOwner** cmdlet 将自己或其他用户添加为白板所有者，或使用 **Invoke-TransferAllWhiteboards** cmdlet 将特定用户所有白板的所有权转移给一个新所有者。有关使用这些 cmdlet 和安装 Whiteboard PowerShell 模块的信息，请参阅“Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet 参考”。在你或其他人获得某个白板的所有权后，请参阅 [Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet 参考](/powershell/module/whiteboard/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p335">If an admin receives a DSR request for data in the new Whiteboard app, they can use Whiteboard PowerShell to add themselves (or other users) as an owner of a user's whiteboards. This enables an admin to perform actions including accessing, exporting, and deleting whiteboards. Use either the **Set-WhiteboardOwner** cmdlet to add yourself or another user as the owner of a whiteboard or use the **Invoke-TransferAllWhiteboards** cmdlet to transfer the ownership of all whiteboards for a specific user to a new owner. For information about using these cmdlets and installing the Whiteboard PowerShell module, see Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet reference. After you or another person has ownership of a whiteboard, see [Microsoft Whiteboard cmdlet reference](/powershell/module/whiteboard/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1240">在你或其他人获得某个白板的所有权后，请参阅 [Whiteboard 支持文章](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=872780)，以获得有关访问、导出和删除白板的详细指导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1240">After you or another person has ownership of a whiteboard, see the [Whiteboard support article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=872780) for detailed guidance about accessing, exporting, and deleting whiteboards.</span></span>

### <a name="yammer"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1241">Yammer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1241">Yammer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1242">以下各节介绍如何在 Microsoft Yammer 中使用应用内功能查找、访问、导出和删除个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1242">The following sections explain how to use the in-app functionality in Microsoft Yammer to find, access, export, and delete personal data.</span></span>

#### <a name="discover"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1243">发现</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1243">Discover</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1244">从 Yammer 管理中心，Yammer 验证管理员（全局管理员或在 Yammer 中设置的验证管理员）可导出给定用户的相关数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1244">From the Yammer admin center, a Yammer verified admin (global admin or verified admin set up in Yammer) can export data pertaining to a given user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1245">导出的内容包括用户发布和修改的消息和文件，以及用户所创建主题和组的相关信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1245">The export includes the messages and files posted and modified by the user, and information about topics and groups created by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1246">导出用户特定的数据时，管理员还可在收件箱中收到包含用户帐户活动数据的邮件，可将这些数据提供给用户（如果这样选择）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1246">When a user-specific data export is run, the admin will also receive an inbox message with the user's account activity data that they can provide to the user if they so choose.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1247">有关详细说明，请参阅 [Yammer Enterprise：隐私](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1247">For detailed instructions, see [Yammer Enterprise: Privacy](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1248">用户特定的导出适用于单个网络，因此，如果用户位于外部 Yammer 网络中，管理员必须针对外部网络和主网络导出数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1248">User-specific exports are for a single network, so if the user is in an external Yammer network, the admin must export data for that external network, and for the home network.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1249">要访问未包含在数据导出中的数据，可对用户的个人资料、设置、组成员身份、添加为书签的消息、关注的用户以及关注的主题进行屏幕截图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1249">To access data not included in data export, screenshots can be taken for the user's profile, settings, group memberships, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1250">用户或管理员可以收集此信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1250">Users or admins can collect this information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1251">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Yammer Enterprise：隐私](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1251">For more information, see [Yammer Enterprise: Privacy](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

#### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1252">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1252">Access</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1253">可查看导出文件中的数据，包括邮件的完整文本和文件的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1253">You can view data in the exported files, including the full text of messages and the contents of files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1254">此外，还可选择导出文件中的链接，直接转到 Yammer 中发布的消息和文件、用户创建的主题和组、用户点赞的消息，@提及用户的消息、用户进行了投票的快速调查，以及用户添加的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1254">You can also select links in the exported files to go directly to the posted messages and files in Yammer, and to groups, and topics the user created, messages the user liked, messages where the user is @mentioned, polls the user has voted on, and links the user has added.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1255">每用户数据导出不包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1255">Per-user data export does not include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1256">用户的个人资料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1256">The user's profile:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p339">如果用户拥有 Yammer 标识，则该用户的个人资料由自己完全掌控。有关如何查看和修改个人资料的信息，请参阅[更改我的 Yammer 个人资料和设置](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p339">If the user has a Yammer identity, the user has full control of their profile. For information on how to view and modify the profile, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p340">如果用户拥有 Office 365 标识，则会自动从 Office 365 中拉取 Yammer 用户个人资料，获取 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 中的个人资料信息。Yammer 用户可在 Yammer 中临时更改其个人资料，但在 AAD 中进行的更改会覆盖这些更改，因此，必须在 AAD 中查看和更改目录数据。请参阅[从 Office 365 管理 Yammer 用户的整个生命周期](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle)和[在 Azure Active Directory 中添加或更改用户的个人资料信息](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p340">If the user has an Office 365 identity, the Yammer user profile is pulled automatically from Office 365, which gets the profile information from Azure Active Directory (AAD). Yammer users can temporarily change their profiles in Yammer, but these changes are overwritten when there is a change in AAD, so you must view and change directory data in AAD. See [Manage Yammer users across their lifecycle from Office 365](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle) and [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal).</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1262">用户的设置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1262">The user's settings:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1263">用户可以查看和更改自己的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1263">The user can view and change their own settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1264">有关如何查看和修改用户设置的信息，请参阅[更改我的 Yammer 个人资料和设置](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1264">For information on how to view and modify user settings, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1265">管理员可以查看此信息并拍摄屏幕截图，但不能对其进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1265">An admin can view this information and take screenshots, but can't change it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1266">转到 Yammer 设置\> **人员**，然后选择用户名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1266">Go to Yammer settings \> **People**, and then select the name of the user.</span></span><br/>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1267">用户的组成员身份、添加为书签的消息、关注的用户和关注的主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1267">The user's group membership, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics.</span></span>
    
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1268">用户可以查看此信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1268">The user can view this information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1269">有关如何操作的信息，请参阅[在 Yammer 中保持有序的技巧](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380)。  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1269">For information on how, see [Tips for staying organized in Yammer](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1270">管理员可以查看此信息并拍摄屏幕截图，但不能对其进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1270">An admin can view this information and take screenshots, but can't change it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1271">转到 Yammer 设置\> **人员**，然后选择用户名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1271">Go to Yammer settings \> **People**, and then select the name of the user.</span></span>

#### <a name="export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1272">导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1272">Export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p343">有关如何导出数据的说明，请参阅[在 Yammer Enterprise 中管理 GDPR 数据主体请求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。必须针对用户所属的每个 Yammer 网络运行每用户导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p343">For instructions for how to export data, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise). You must run a per-user export for each Yammer network the user is a member of.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1275">用户删除消息或文件时，Yammer 可设置数据保留设置（软删除或硬删除数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1275">Yammer has data retention settings that either soft-delete or hard-delete data when a user deletes a message or file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1276">如果设置为软删除，则用户删除的数据将包含在导出中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1276">If this is set to soft-delete, data a user has deleted will be included in the export.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1277">如果 Yammer 数据保留设置设为硬删除，则 Yammer 中不再存储已删除的信息，因此该信息不会包含在导出中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1277">If the Yammer data retention setting is set to hard-delete, the deleted information is no longer stored in Yammer, so will not be included in the export.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1278">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1278">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1279">Yammer 允许经过验证的管理员在收到 DSR 后通过 Yammer 管理中心执行符合 GDPR 的删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1279">Yammer allows verified admins to execute a GDPR-compliant delete via the Yammer admin center if they receive a DSR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1280">此选项被称为“擦除用户”，它将暂停用户 14 天，然后删除其所有个人数据（文件和邮件除外）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1280">This option is called Erase User, and it suspends the user for 14 days and then removes all their personal data, excluding files and messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1281">如果用户是来宾用户，则必须针对来宾成员的每个外部网络执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1281">If the user is a guest user, this must be done for each external network the guest is a member of.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p346">如果管理员想要在 14 天内删除用户的文件和消息，则必须执行用户级别导出以识别文件和消息，然后确定要通过产品内删除或 PowerShell 脚本删除的内容。14 天后，管理员无法再将用户与其文件或消息关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p346">If an admin wants to remove the files and messages of a user during the 14-day window, they will have to perform a user level export to identify the files and messages, and then decide which ones to delete either by in-product deletion or by using a PowerShell script. After the 14-day window, the admin can no longer associate the user with their files or messages.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p347">在使用“擦除用户”选项删除某个用户时，系统会向所有网络管理员和已验证管理员的 Yammer 收件箱发送通知。“擦除用户”选项会删除用户的 Yammer 个人资料，但不会删除他们的 Office 365 或 Azure Active Directory 个人资料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p347">When a user is deleted with the Erase User option, notification is sent to the Yammer Inbox of all network admins and verified admins. The Erase User option deletes the user's Yammer profile, but does not delete their Office 365 or Azure Active Directory profile.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1286">有关删除用户的详细步骤，请参阅[在 Yammer Enterprise 中管理 GDPR 数据主体请求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1286">For detailed steps to remove a user, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise).</span></span>

## <a name="responding-to-dsr-rectification-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1287">响应 DSR 纠正请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1287">Responding to DSR rectification requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1288">如果数据主体要求你纠正驻留在你的组织数据（存储在 Office 365 中）中的个人数据，你和你的组织需要确定是否可以接受该请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1288">If a data subject has asked you to rectify the personal data that resides in your organization's data stored in Office 365, you and your organization have to determine whether it's appropriate to honor the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1289">如果选择接受该请求，则纠正数据可能需要进行多种操作，如编辑、修订个人数据，或将个人数据从文档或其他类型的项目中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1289">If you choose to honor the request, then rectifying the data may include taking actions such as editing, redacting, or removing personal data from a document or other type or item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1290">完成此操作的最佳方法是请求数据/文档所有者使用相应的 Office 365 应用程序进行请求的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1290">The most expedient way to do this is to ask the data/document owner to use the appropriate Office 365 application to make the requested change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1291">也可以请求组织中的 IT 管理员户进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1291">An alternative is to have an IT admin in your organization make the change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1292">这可能需要 IT 管理员（或组织中具有相应特权的其他人员，如 SharePoint Online 网站集管理员）为自己或组织中处理 DSR 的其他人分配必要的权限，以便获取对文档或文档所在内容位置的访问权限，从而直接对文档进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1292">This will probably require the IT admin (or other people in your organization with the appropriate privileges, such as a SharePoint Online site collection administrator) to assign to themselves or someone else working on the DSR the necessary permissions to gain access to the document or the content location where the document is located to make the change directly to the document.</span></span>

### <a name="requesting-that-the-data-owner-to-make-the-approved-change"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1293">请求数据所有者进行已批准的更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1293">Requesting that the data owner to make the approved change</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p349">纠正个人数据最直接的方式是请求数据所有者进行更改。找到作为 DSR 主体的数据后，可提供以下信息，以便他们可以进行更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p349">The most direct way to rectify personal data is to ask the data owner to make the change. After you locate the data that is the subject of the DSR, you can provide the following information so that they can make the change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1296">需要更改的项目的位置和文件名（对于文档和其他文件）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1296">The location and file name (for documents and other files) of the item that needs to be changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1297">查找相关数据是发现过程中包含的内容，前文中介绍了此[发现过程](#using-content-search-to-find-personal-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1297">Locating the data in question is part of the discovery process [discovery process](#using-content-search-to-find-personal-data) that was previously explained.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1298">数据所有者应进行的已批准的更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1298">The approved change the data owner should make</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1299">你可能需要考虑实施确认流程，由你或涉及 DSR 调查的其他人验证已进行请求的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1299">You may want to consider implementing a confirmation process where you or another person involved in the DSR investigation verifies that the requested change has been made.</span></span>

### <a name="gaining-access-to-a-sharepoint-online-site-or-onedrive-for-business-account-to-make-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1300">获取对 SharePoint Online 网站或 OneDrive for Business 帐户的访问权限以便进行更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1300">Gaining access to a SharePoint Online site or OneDrive for Business account to make changes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p351">如果由数据所有者实施数据主体的纠正请求不可行，组织中的 IT 管理员或 SharePoint 管理员可以获取对内容位置的访问权限并进行必要的更改。或者，管理员可以为你或其他数据隐私部主管分配必要的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p351">If it's not feasible for the data owner to implement the data subject's request for rectification, an IT admin or SharePoint admin in your organization can get access to the content location and make the required changes. Or, an admin can assign you or another data privacy officer the necessary permissions.</span></span>

#### <a name="sharepoint-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1303">SharePoint Online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1303">SharePoint Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1304">要分配针对 SharePoint Online 网站的管理员或所有者权限以便你或其他人可以访问和编辑该文档，请参阅</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1304">To assign administrator or owner permissions to a SharePoint Online site so that you or someone else can access and edit that document, see</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1305">管理网站集的管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1305">Manage administrators for a site collection</span></span>](/sharepoint/manage-site-collection-administrators)

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1306">编辑和管理 SharePoint 列表和库的权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1306">Edit and manage permissions for a SharePoint list or library</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/Edit-and-manage-permissions-for-a-SharePoint-list-or-library-02d770f3-59eb-4910-a608-5f84cc297782)

#### <a name="onedrive-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1307">OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1307">OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1308">全局管理员可通过以下方式访问用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1308">A global admin can access a user's OneDrive for Business account by using the .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1309">使用全局管理员凭据登录 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1309">Sign in to Office 365 with your global admin credentials.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1310">转到“管理中心”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1310">Go to the admin center.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1311">转到“**活动用户**”并选择某个用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1311">Go to **Active users** and select the user.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1312">在细节窗格中展开“**OneDrive for Business 设置**”，然后选择“**访问文件**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1312">Expand **OneDrive for Business Settings** in the details pane, and then select **Access files**.</span></span>
5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1313">选择 URL，访问用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1313">select the URL to go to the user's OneDrive for Business account.</span></span>

### <a name="gaining-access-to-an-exchange-online-mailbox-to-make-changes-to-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1314">获取对 Exchange Online 邮箱的访问权限以对数据进行更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1314">Gaining access to an Exchange Online mailbox to make changes to data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p352">全局管理员可为自己分配必要的权限，以便打开和编辑（或删除）其他用户邮箱中的项目，就好像他们是邮箱所有者一样。全局管理员还可为另一用户分配这些权限。具体而言，全局管理员需要添加“**读取和管理**”权限，这是 Exchange Online 中的完全访问权限。有关详细信息，请参阅：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p352">A global admin can assign themselves the permissions necessary to open and edit (or delete) items in another user's mailbox, as if they were the mailbox owner. A global admin can also assign these permissions to another user. Specifically, the global admin needs to add the **Read and manage** permission, which is the Full Access permission in Exchange Online. For details, see:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1319">向 Office 365 中的其他用户授予邮箱权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1319">Give mailbox permissions to another user in Office 365</span></span>](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/give-mailbox-permissions-to-another-user)
- [<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1320">访问其他人的邮箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1320">Access another person's mailbox</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/Access-another-person-s-mailbox-A909AD30-E413-40B5-A487-0EA70B763081)

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1321">如果对用户邮箱实施了法定保留，或用户邮箱已分配到保留策略，则所有版本的邮箱都会保留，直到保留期限到期或从邮箱删除了保留。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1321">If the user mailbox is place on a legal hold or has been assigned to a retention policy, all versions of a mailbox are retained until the retention period expires or the hold is removed from the mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1322">这意味着如果更改了邮箱项目以响应 DSR 纠正请求，会在用户邮箱“可恢复邮件”文件夹中的一个隐藏文件夹中保留一份原始项目（进行更改前的项目）副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1322">That means if a mailbox item is changed in response to DSR rectification request, a copy of original item (before the change was made) is retained and stored in a hidden folder in the Recoverable Items folder in the user's mailbox.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-onedrive-for-business-and-sharepoint-online"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1323">更改 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 中的内容</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1323">Making changes to content in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p354">管理员或数据所有者可以对 SharePoint Online 文档、列表和页面进行更改。更改 SharePoint 内容时，请记住以下事项：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p354">Admins or data owners can make changes to SharePoint Online documents, lists, and pages. Keep the following things in mind when making changes to SharePoint content:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1326">更新文档将保存新版本的文档，其中包含修订内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1326">Updating a document saves a new version of the document, which will contain the revision.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1327">不会更新较早版本的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1327">Older versions of the document will not be updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1328">这意味着作为 DSR 纠正请求主体的数据可能一直保留在较早版本的主题中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1328">That means it's possible that the data that's the subject of a DSR rectification request may persist in older versions of the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1329">可删除较早版本的主题，然后将其从 Office 365 中永久删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1329">Older versions of a topic can be deleted and then permanently removed from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1330">请参阅本指南的[删除 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文档](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1330">See the [Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business) section in this guide.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1331">要完成 SharePoint 文件修订，并从文件中删除数据主体的所有痕迹（包括所有版本的文件和数据主体执行的所有记录的活动），需要执行以下步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1331">To completely redact a SharePoint file in a way that removes all traces of a data subject from the file, including all versions of the file and all recorded activity performed by the data subject, you have to perform the following steps:</span></span>

    1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1332">将文件副本下载到本地计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1332">Download a copy of the file to your local computer.</span></span>
    2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p356">通过删除文件，然后从第一阶段回收站和第二阶段回收站中删除该文件，从 SharePoint Online 中永久删除文件。请参阅本指南的[删除 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文档](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p356">Permanently delete the file from SharePoint Online, by deleting the file, and then deleting if from the first-stage and second-stage Recycle Bin. See the [Deleting documents in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](#deleting-documents-in-sharepoint-online-and-onedrive-for-business) section in this guide.</span></span>
    3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1335">在本地计算机上修订文档副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1335">Make the revisions to the copy of the document on your local computer.</span></span>
    4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1336">将修订后的文件上传到原始 SharePoint Online 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1336">Upload the revised file to the original SharePoint Online location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p357">可编辑 SharePoint 列表中的数据。请参阅[添加、编辑或删除列表项](https://support.microsoft.com/office/add-edit-or-delete-list-items-a4b31f53-f044-470e-9823-4526594bacde)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p357">Data in SharePoint lists can be edited. See [Add, edit, or delete list items](https://support.microsoft.com/office/add-edit-or-delete-list-items-a4b31f53-f044-470e-9823-4526594bacde).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1339">IT 管理员也可更正与文档关联某些个人属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1339">IT admins can also correct certain personal properties associated with a document:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p358">SharePoint 用户个人资料或 Office 365 中的用户信息通常与 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 文档关联，以对该人员进行描述。例如，文档或列表项的“创建者”和“修改者”人员列中的用户姓名。可通过多种方式纠正此用户信息，具体取决于数据源：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p358">User information from the SharePoint User Profile or Office 365 is often associated with OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online documents to represent that person. For example, a user's name in a Created By or Modified By People column for a document or list item. This user information can be rectified in several ways, depending on the source:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1343">在自己的本地 Active Directory 中纠正用户属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1343">Rectify user properties in their own on-premises Active Directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1344">对于从本地 AD 同步用户属性（如用户显示名称、名字等）的客户，应在本地 AD 中纠正这些属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1344">For customers syncing user properties such as user Display Name, First Name, etc. from an on-premises AD, those properties should be rectified there.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1345">正确映射的属性将流入 Office 365，然后流入 OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1345">Appropriately mapped properties flow into Office 365, and then OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1346">在管理中心纠正用户属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1346">Rectify user properties in the admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1347">OneDrive for Business 和 SharePoint Online 体验中可自动反映对帐户信息的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1347">Changes made to account information there will automatically be reflected in OneDrive for Business and SharePoint Online experiences.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1348">有关信息，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中添加或更改个人资料信息](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=864809)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1348">For info, see [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=864809).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1349">对于源于 Office 365 的属性，无法在 SharePoint 端进行任何更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1349">For properties sourced in Office 365, no changes can be made on the SharePoint side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1350">在 SharePoint 管理中心的 SharePoint 用户配置文件体验中纠正用户属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1350">Rectify user properties in the SharePoint user profile experience of the SharePoint admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1351">在 SharePoint 管理中心的“用户个人资料”选项卡中，管理员可以选择“**管理用户个人资料**”，并查找任何用户属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1351">In the user profiles tab of the SharePoint admin center, admins can select **Manage user profiles**, and look up any user's properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1352">然后，他们可以选择编辑用户的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1352">Then they can choose to Edit the user's properties.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p362">在自定义源中纠正用户属性。自定义 SharePoint 个人资料属性可能是通过 Microsoft Identity Manager (MIM) 或其他方法从自定义源同步的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p362">Rectify user properties in a custom source. Custom SharePoint profile properties may be syncing from a custom source via Microsoft Identity Manager (MIM) or another method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1355">并非所有体验都会受到影响，可能会保留较早的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1355">This won't affect all experiences, which may retain the older information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1356">例如，作为文档中文本的用户姓名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1356">For example, the user's name as text in the document.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-power-bi"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1357">更改 Power BI 中的内容</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1357">Making changes to content in Power BI</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p364">Power BI 依赖在其仪表板和报表中使用的基础源数据来保持完整性和准确性，因此必须在基础源数据中更正不正确或不完整的数据源。例如，如果创建的 Power BI 报表连接到实时数据源 Dynamics 365 for Sales，则任何数据更正都必须针对 Dynamics 365 for Sales 中的数据进行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p364">Power BI relies on the underlying source data used in its dashboards and reports to be complete and accurate, so correcting inaccurate or incomplete source data must be done there. For example, if you created a Power BI report that is connected to Dynamics 365 for Sales as the live data source, you would have to make any corrections to the data in Dynamics 365 for Sales.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p365">进行更改后，可以利用[计划的数据刷新](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh)功能来更新存储在 Power BI 中的数据集，以便在相关 Power BI 资产中反映修订后的数据。为帮助符合 GDPR 要求，应该制定相应的策略，确保按照适当的节奏刷新数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p365">After those changes are made, you can take advantage of the [scheduled data refresh](/power-bi/refresh-scheduled-refresh) capabilities to update the dataset that is stored in Power BI so that the revised data is reflected in the dependent Power BI assets. To help comply with GDPR requirements, you should have policies in place to ensure that you are refreshing your data at an appropriate cadence.</span></span>

### <a name="making-changes-to-content-in-yammer"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1362">更改 Yammer 中的内容</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1362">Making changes to content in Yammer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1363">对于邮件，用户可以编辑给定的邮件以纠正任何不准确之处。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1363">For messages, a user can edit a given message to rectify any inaccuracies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1364">用户可从 Yammer 验证管理员处请求其所有消息的列表，然后选择文件中的链接查看每条消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1364">They can request a list of all their messages from a Yammer verified admin, and then select a link in the file to review each message.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p367">对于文件，用户可编辑给定文件以纠正任何不准确的内容。用户可从 Yammer 验证管理员处请求其发布的所有文件，然后在 Yammer 中访问这些文件。可以通过按数字搜索文件来查看导出到“文件”文件夹中的文件。例如，对于导出中名为 12345678.ppx 的文件，使用 Yammer 中的搜索框搜索 1235678.ppx。或者，转到 <strong>https://www.yammer.com/\<network\_name\>/\#/files/\<file\_number\></strong>；例如 <strong>https://www.yammer.com/contosomkt.onmicrosoft.com/\#/files/12345678</strong>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p367">For files, a user can edit a given file to rectify any inaccuracies. They can request a list of all the files they posted from a Yammer verified admin, and then access the files in Yammer. Files that are exported into the Files folder can be viewed by searching for the file by number. For example, for a file named 12345678.ppx in the export, use the Search box in Yammer to search for 1235678.ppx. Or, go to <strong>https://www.yammer.com/\<network\_name\>/\#/files/\<file\_number\></strong>; for example, <strong>https://www.yammer.com/contosomkt.onmicrosoft.com/\#/files/12345678</strong>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1370">对于用户可通过其个人资料和设置访问的数据，用户可以进行任何必要的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1370">For data that the user can access through their profile and settings, the user can make any needed changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1371">用户的个人资料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1371">The user's profile:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p368">如果用户拥有 Yammer 标识，则该用户的个人资料由自己完全掌控。有关如何查看和修改个人资料的信息，请参阅[更改我的 Yammer 个人资料和设置](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p368">If the user has a Yammer identity, the user has full control of their profile. For information on how to view and modify the profile, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1374">如果用户拥有 Office 365 标识，则会自动从 Office 365 中拉取 Yammer 用户个人资料，获取 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 中的个人资料信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1374">If the user has an Office 365 identity, the Yammer user profile is pulled automatically from Office 365, which gets the profile information from Azure Active Directory (AAD).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1375">Yammer 用户可在 Yammer 中临时更改其个人资料，但在 AAD 中进行的更改会覆盖这些更改，因此，最好在 AAD 中查看和更改目录数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1375">Yammer users can temporarily change their profiles in Yammer, but these changes are overwritten when there is a change in AAD, so the best place to view and change directory data is AAD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1376">用户需要请求更新 AAD。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1376">The user needs to request that AAD be updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1377">请参阅[从 Office 365 管理 Yammer 用户的整个生命周期](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle)和[在 Azure Active Directory 中添加或更改用户的个人资料信息](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1377">See [Manage Yammer users across their lifecycle from Office 365](/yammer/manage-yammer-users/manage-users-across-their-lifecycle) and [Add or change profile information for a user in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-users-profile-azure-portal).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1378">用户的设置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1378">The user's settings:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p370">用户可更改自己的设置。有关如何查看和修改用户设置的信息，请参阅[更改我的 Yammer 个人资料和设置](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p370">The user can change their own settings. For information on how to view and modify user settings, see [Change my Yammer profile and settings](https://support.office.com/article/change-my-yammer-profile-and-settings-a3aeca0e-de34-4897-9b59-de6516542851).</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p371">用户的组成员身份、添加为书签的消息、关注的用户和关注的主题。用户可更改此信息；请参阅[有关在 Yammer 中保持井然有序的提示](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p371">The user's group membership, bookmarked messages, followed users, and followed topics. The user can change this information; see [Tips for staying organized in Yammer](https://support.office.com/article/tips-for-staying-organized-in-yammer-40ae9666-75c0-4254-a84c-d87a9542f380).</span></span>

## <a name="responding-to-dsr-restriction-requests"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1383">响应 DSR 限制请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1383">Responding to DSR restriction requests</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1384">可通过下面的方法限制 Office 365 中的数据处理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1384">Here are the ways to restrict the processing of data in Office 365:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1385">删除 Office 365 应用程序许可证，阻止用户通过应用程序访问数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1385">Remove an Office 365 application license to prevent users from accessing data via an application</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1386">阻止用户访问其 OneDrive for Business 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1386">Prevent users from accessing their OneDrive for Business account</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1387">关闭 Office 365 服务的数据处理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1387">Turn off an Office 365 service from processing the data</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1388">暂时从 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中删除数据，并将数据保留在本地</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1388">Temporarily remove the data from SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business and retain it on-premises</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1389">暂时限制对 SharePoint Online 网站的所有访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1389">Temporarily restrict all access to a SharePoint Online site</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1390">阻止用户登录 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1390">Prevent a user from signing in to Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1391">如果组织稍后确定限制不再适用，可通过反向执行用于实施限制的步骤来结束限制，如重新分配许可证、重新打开服务，或允许用户登录 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1391">If your organization determines later that a restriction no longer applies, you can end the restriction by reversing the steps you took to restrict it; such as reassigning licenses, turning a service back on, or allowing a user to sign in to Office 365.</span></span>

### <a name="removing-the-license-for-an-office-365-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1392">删除 Office 365 应用程序的许可证</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1392">Removing the license for an Office 365 application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1393">如上文所述，默认情况下，组织的 Microsoft 365 商业版订阅中包含的所有 Office 365 应用程序的许可证都分配给所有用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1393">As previously explained, licenses for all Office 365 applications that are included in your organization's Microsoft 365 for business subscription are assigned to all users by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1394">如果需要限制对作为 DSR 主体的数据的访问，IT 管理员可以使用 Office 365 管理门户暂时关闭应用程序的用户许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1394">If necessary to restrict,  access to data that's subject to a DSR, an IT admin can use the Office 365 admin portal temporarily turn off a user's license for an application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1395">如果用户之后尝试使用该应用程序，他们将收到未经授权的产品通知或一条显示他们不再有权访问的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1395">If a user then tries to use that application, they'll receive an unlicensed product notification or a message saying they no longer have access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1396">有关详细信息，请参阅[在 Office 365 商业版中删除用户许可证](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1396">For details, see [Remove licenses from users in Office 365 for business](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/delete-a-user).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1397">**注意：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1397">**Notes:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1398">要限制用户访问 Yammer，必须先[强制 Yammer 用户使用 Office 365 标识](/yammer/configure-your-yammer-network/enforce-office-365-identity)，然后删除用户的 Yammer 许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1398">To restrict a user from accessing Yammer, you must first [enforce Office 365 identify for a Yammer user](/yammer/configure-your-yammer-network/enforce-office-365-identity) and then remove the user's Yammer license.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1399">对于利用 Power BI Embedded 的方案，可以限制访问嵌入了内容的独立软件供应商 (ISV) 应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1399">For scenarios that take advantage of Power BI Embedded, you can restrict access to the independent software vendor (ISV) application that the content is embedded in.</span></span>

### <a name="preventing-users-from-accessing-their-onedrive-for-business-account"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1400">阻止用户访问其 OneDrive for Business 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1400">Preventing users from accessing their OneDrive for Business account</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1401">删除用户的 SharePoint Online 许可证不会阻止用户访问其 OneDrive for Business 帐户（如果该帐户已存在）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1401">Removing a user's SharePoint Online license won't prevent them from accessing their OneDrive for Business account if it exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1402">必须删除用户针对其 OneDrive for Business 帐户的权限才可实现该目的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1402">You have to remove the user's permissions to their OneDrive for Business account to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1403">为此，可以删除用户的 OneDrive for Business 帐户网站集所有者身份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1403">You can do this by removing the user as a site collection owner of their OneDrive for Business account.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1404">具体而言，必须在用户个人资料中将用户从网站集主管理员和网站集管理员组中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1404">Specifically, you have to remove the user from the Primary Site Collection Administrator and Site Collection Administrators groups in their user profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1405">请参阅的[在 SharePoint 管理中心管理用户个人资料](/sharepoint/manage-user-profiles)的“添加和删除 OneDrive for Business 帐户的管理员”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1405">See the "Add and remove admins on a OneDrive for Business account" section in [Manage user profiles in the SharePoint admin center](/sharepoint/manage-user-profiles).</span></span>

### <a name="turning-off-an-office-365-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1406">关闭 Office 365 服务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1406">Turning off an Office 365 Service</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1407">也可通过关闭 Office 365 服务来应对限制数据处理的 DSR 请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1407">Another way to address a DSR request to restrict the processing of data is to turn off an Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1408">这将影响整个组织中的所有用户，并阻止每位用户使用服务或访问服务中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1408">This impacts all users in your entire organization and prevents everyone from using the service or accessing data in the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p375">关闭服务的最佳方法是使用 Office 365 PowerShell 并删除组织中所有用户对应的用户许可证。这实际上将限制任何人访问该服务中的数据。有关详细说明，请参阅[使用 Office 365 PowerShell 禁止访问服务](/microsoft-365/enterprise/disable-access-to-services-with-microsoft-365-powershell)，并按照相关过程对用户禁用单个许可计划中的 Office 365 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p375">The most expedient way to turn off a service is to use Office 365 PowerShell and remove the corresponding user license from all users in the organization. This will in effect restrict anyone from access data in that service. For detailed instructions, see [Disable access to services with Office 365 PowerShell](/microsoft-365/enterprise/disable-access-to-services-with-microsoft-365-powershell) and follow the procedures to disable Office 365 services for users from a single licensing plan.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p376">对于 Yammer，除了从用户帐户删除 Yammer 许可证外，还必须禁止用户使用 Yammer 凭据登录 Yammer（强制用户在登录时使用 Office 365 凭据）。有关详细说明，请参阅[关闭 Microsoft 365 用户的 Yammer 访问权限](https://support.office.com/article/Turn-off-Yammer-access-for-Office-365-users-1f79bfad-f713-4143-aa5d-5584985ce53a)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p376">For Yammer, in additional to removing the Yammer license from user accounts, you also must disable users' ability to sign in to Yammer with Yammer credentials (by enforcing the use of their Office 365 credentials when signing in). For detailed instructions, see [Turn off Yammer access for Microsoft 365 users](https://support.office.com/article/Turn-off-Yammer-access-for-Office-365-users-1f79bfad-f713-4143-aa5d-5584985ce53a).</span></span>

### <a name="temporarily-removing-data-from-sharepoint-online-or-onedrive-for-business-sites"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1414">暂时从 SharePoint Online 或 OneDrive for Business 网站中删除数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1414">Temporarily removing data from SharePoint Online or OneDrive for Business sites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p377">限制个人数据处理的另一方法是暂时从 Office 365 中删除数据以响应 DSR。当组织确定限制不再适用时，可将数据重新导入 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p377">Another way to restrict the processing of personal data is to temporarily remove it from Office 365 in response to a DSR. When your organization determines that the restriction no longer applies, you can import the data back into Office 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1417">由于大多数 Office 文档都位于 SharePoint Online 或 OneDrive for Business 网站中，因此下文提供了从这些网站删除文档然后重新导入的高级流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1417">Because most Office documents are on a SharePoint Online or OneDrive for Business site, here's a high-level process for removing documents from sites and then re-importing them.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p378">获取作为限制请求主体的文档的副本。可能需要请求访问网站，或者请求全局管理员或网站集管理员提供文档副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p378">Get a copy of the document that is the subject of the restriction request. You may have to request either access to the site or ask a global admin or a site collection administrator to provide you with a copy of the document.</span></span>
