2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1420">在本地位置（如文件服务器或文件共享）或 Microsoft 云中除 Office 365 租户之外的位置存储文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1420">Store the document in an on-premises location (such as a file server or a file share) or another location other than your Office 365 tenant in the Microsoft cloud.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p379">从 Office 365 永久删除（清除）原始文档。此流程包含 3 个步骤：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p379">Permanently delete (purge) the original document from Office 365. This is a 3-step process:</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1423">删除文档的原始副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1423">Delete the original copy of the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1424">从网站删除文档时，该文档发送到网站回收站（也称为 *第一阶段回收站*）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1424">When you delete a document from a site, it's sent to the site Recycle Bin (also called the *first-stage Recycle Bin*).</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1425">转到网站回收站并删除文档副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1425">Go to the site Recycle Bin and delete that copy of the document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1426">从网站回收站删除文档时，该文档发送到网站集回收站（也称为 *第二阶段回收站*）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1426">When you delete a document from the site Recycle Bin, it's sent to the site collection Recycle Bin (also called the *second-stage Recycle Bin*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1427">请参阅[从 SharePoint 文档库中删除文件、文件夹或链接](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-file-folder-or-link-from-a-sharepoint-document-library-71f3c90a-0d24-4d80-8b66-f88234b79a52)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1427">See [Delete a file, folder, or link from a SharePoint document library](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-a-file-folder-or-link-from-a-sharepoint-document-library-71f3c90a-0d24-4d80-8b66-f88234b79a52).</span></span>

   1.  <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1428">转到网站集回收站并删除文档副本，此操作从 Office 365 中永久删除了该文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1428">Go to the site collection Recycle Bin and delete that copy of the document, which permanently removes it from Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1429">请参阅[从网站集回收站中删除项目](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-from-the-site-collection-recycle-bin-dd5c00c2-aef6-4458-9d04-80b185077653)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1429">See [Delete items from the site collection recycle bin](https://support.microsoft.com/office/delete-items-from-the-site-collection-recycle-bin-dd5c00c2-aef6-4458-9d04-80b185077653).</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1430">限制不再适用时，可在 Office 365 中将存储在本地的文档副本重新上传到网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1430">When the restriction no longer applies, the copy of the document that was stored on-premises can be re-uploaded to the site in Office 365.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p383">如果文档位于处于保留状态（在 Office 365 中使用了某项保留或法定保留功能）的网站中，则上述过程不起作用。如果 DSR 限制请求优先于法定保留，必须先从网站删除保留，才可永久删除文档。此外，还将永久删除已删除文档的文档历史记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p383">The preceding procedure won't work if the document is located on a site that is on hold (with one of the retention or legal hold features in Office 365). In the case where a restriction request for a DSR takes precedence over a legal hold, the hold would have to be removed from the site before a document could be permanently deleted. Additionally, the document history for deleted documents is permanently removed.</span></span>

### <a name="temporarily-restricting-access-to-sharepoint-online-sites"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1434">暂时限制对 SharePoint Online 网站的访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1434">Temporarily restricting access to SharePoint Online sites</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1435">SharePoint Online 管理员可通过锁定网站集（通过在 SharePoint Online PowerShell 中使用 **Set-SPOSite -LockState** 命令）暂时阻止所有用户访问 SharePoint Online 网站集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1435">A SharePoint Online administrator can temporarily prevent all users from accessing a SharePoint Online site collection by locking the site collection (by using the **Set-SPOSite -LockState** command in SharePoint Online PowerShell).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1436">这可阻止用户访问网站集或网站中包含的任何内容或数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1436">This prevents users for accessing the site collection and any content or data that's located in the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1437">如果稍后确定用户可访问网站，管理员可解锁网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1437">If you then determine that users should be able to access the site, the administrator can unlock the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1438">请参阅 [Set-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/set-sposite)，了解有关运行此 PowerShell cmdlet 的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1438">See [Set-SPOSite](/powershell/module/sharepoint-online/set-sposite) for information about running this PowerShell cmdlet.</span></span>

### <a name="preventing-a-user-from-signing-in-to-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1439">阻止用户登录 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1439">Preventing a user from signing in to Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p385">IT 管理员还可阻止用户登录 Office 365，从而阻止用户访问任何 Office 365 联机服务或处理存储在 Office 365 中的任何数据。请参阅[阻止以前的员工访问 Office 365 数据](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/remove-former-employee)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p385">An IT admin can also prevent a user from signing into Office 365, which would prevent the user from accessing any Office 365 online service or processing any data stored in Office 365. See [Block a former employee's access to Office 365 data](/microsoft-365/admin/add-users/remove-former-employee).</span></span>

## <a name="part-2-responding-to-dsrs-with-respect-to-insights-generated-by-office-365"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1442">第 2 部分：响应与 Office 365 生成的见解相关的 DSR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1442">Part 2: Responding to DSRs with Respect to Insights Generated by Office 365</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1443">Microsoft Office 365 服务套件包括多种联机服务，可为选择使用这些服务的用户和组织提供见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1443">The Microsoft suite of Office 365 services includes online services that provide insights to users and organizations that have opted to use them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1444">Delve 和 MyAnalytics 为单个用户提供见解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1444">Delve and MyAnalytics provide insights to individual users</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1445">Workplace Analytics 为组织提供见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1445">Workplace Analytics provides insights to organizations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1446">以下各节介绍了这些服务：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1446">These services are described in the following sections:</span></span>

### <a name="delve"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1447">Delve</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1447">Delve</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1448">在 Delve 中，用户可管理他们的 Office 365 个人资料，并发现可能与他们相关的人员和文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1448">In Delve, users can manage their Office 365 profile and discover people and documents that may be relevant to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1449">用户只能看到他们有权访问的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1449">Users can only see documents that they have access to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1450">有关一系列 Delve 相关实用文章，请参阅 [Office Delve](https://support.office.com/article/What-is-Office-Delve-1315665a-c6af-4409-a28d-49f8916878ca)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1450">For a series of helpful articles about Delve, see [Office Delve](https://support.office.com/article/What-is-Office-Delve-1315665a-c6af-4409-a28d-49f8916878ca).</span></span>

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1451">访问和导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1451">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p387">管理员无法访问或导出用户的 Delve 数据。这意味着用户需要自行访问和导出 Delve 数据。大部分数据类型都可直接从 Delve 中访问和导出，但某些数据类型仅可通过其他服务访问和导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p387">Admins can't access or export a users' Delve data. This means that users have to access and export Delve data themselves. Most of the data types can be accessed and exported directly from Delve, but some data types are only available through other services.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-available-in-the-delve-user-interface"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1455">Delve 用户界面中提供的数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1455">Data available in the Delve user interface</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1456">**个人资料数据：** 这是 Azure Active Directory 中组织的全局地址列表中的个人资料信息，以及用户选择添加的与自己相关的可选信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1456">**Profile data:** This is the profile information from your organization's Global Address List in Azure Active Directory, and optional information that users have chosen to add about themselves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1457">若要在 Delve 中访问或导出个人资料数据，用户可选择“**我**”\>“**更新个人资料**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1457">To access or export profile data in Delve, a user can select **Me** \> **Update profile**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1458">他们可以直接从页面中复制内容或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1458">They can either copy the content directly from the page or</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1459">**博客数据：** 这是用户发布的博客文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1459">**Blog data:** This is blog posts published by a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1460">若要访问或导出博客数据，用户可以选择“**我**”\>“**所有文章**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1460">To access or export blog data, a user can select **Me** \> **All posts**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1461">他们可以直接从页面中复制内容或获取屏幕截图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1461">They can either copy the content directly from the page or take a screenshot.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1462">**最近的人员数据：** 这些是 Delve 在给定时间推断为与用户最相关的组织中的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1462">**Recent people data:** These are the people in the organization that Delve has inferred are most relevant to the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1463">当用户在“选择某个人以查看他们正在处理的内容”窗格中选择“**我**”\>“**全部查看**”时，Delve 将显示在给定时间与用户最相关的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1463">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "select a person to see what they're working on" pane, Delve shows the most relevant people for a user at a given time.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-available-through-an-export-link-in-delve"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1464">通过 Delve 中的导出链接提供的数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1464">Data available through an export link in Delve</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1465">**人员列表数据：** 这些是用户已在 Delve 中查看的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1465">**People list data:** These are the people the user has viewed in Delve.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1466">“**人员**”列表显示在主页上的左侧窗格中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1466">The **People** list is shown in the left pane on the home page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1467">用户可以导出他们最近在 Delve 中查看的人员的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1467">Users can export the list of people they have most recently viewed in Delve.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1468">**收藏夹数据：** 这些是用户已标记为其收藏夹的版块和文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1468">**Favorites data:** These are boards and documents that the user has marked as their favorite.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1469">“**收藏夹**”页面显示用户已添加到其收藏夹的版块和文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1469">The **Favorites** page shows boards and documents that the user has added to their favorites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1470">用户可以将导出其当前收藏夹版块和文档的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1470">Users can export a list of their current favorite boards and documents.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1471">**功能设置数据：** 这些是用户使用 Delve 时生成的 Delve 配置或操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1471">**Feature settings data:** These are Delve configurations or actions that result from a user's use of Delve.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1472">用户可以导出这些设置的完整列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1472">Users can export a full list of these settings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1473">若要访问或导出以上数据，用户可以选择 Delve 右上角的齿轮图标，然后选择“**功能设置**” > “**导出数据**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1473">To access or export the above data, the user can select the gear icon in the upper-right corner in Delve, and then select **Feature settings** > **Export data**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1474">信息以 JSON 格式导出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1474">Information is exported in JSON format.</span></span>

##### <a name="data-thats-available-through-other-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1475">通过其他服务提供的数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1475">Data that's available through other services</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1476">**热门文档数据：** 这些是可能与用户相关的文档和电子邮件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1476">**Popular documents data:** These are documents and email attachments that may be relevant to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1477">Delve 会基于用户的活动以及他们在 Office 365 中协同工作的人员动态组织其文档和电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1477">Delve dynamically organizes these documents and email messages based on the user's activities and people they work with in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1478">当用户打开 Delve 或选择“**主页**”时，Delve 会显示在给定时间与用户最相关的文档或附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1478">When a user opens Delve or selects **Home**, Delve shows the most relevant documents or attachments for the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1479">若要访问或导出实际文档和附件，用户可以转到通过其提供了文档的 Office 365 服务（例如 Office.com、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business 或 Exchange Online）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1479">To access or export the actual documents and attachments, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available (such as Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1480">**最近的文档和电子邮件附件数据：** 这些是用户最近修改过的文档和电子邮件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1480">**Recent documents and email attachments data:** These are the most recent documents and email attachments that the user has modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1481">当用户在“返回最近的文档和电子邮件附件”窗格中选择“**我**”\>“**全部查看**” 时，Delve 会显示用户在给定时间修改的最新文档和电子邮件附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1481">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "Get back to your recent documents and email attachments" pane, Delve shows the latest documents and email attachments the user has modified at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1482">若要访问或导出实际文档和附件，用户可以转到通过其提供了文档或附件的 Office 365 服务；例如，Office.com、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business 或 Exchange Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1482">To access or export the actual documents and attachments, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available; for example, Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1483">**来自你周围的人员的文档数据：** 这些是 Delve 在给定时间推断为与用户最相关的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1483">**Documents from people around your data:** These are the documents that Delve has inferred are most relevant to the user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1484">当用户在“发现来自你周围的人员的文档”窗格中选择“**我**”\>“**全部查看**”时，Delve 会显示在给定时间与用户最相关的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1484">When a user selects **Me** \> **See all** in the "Discover documents from people around you" pane, Delve shows the most relevant documents for a user at a given time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1485">若要访问或导出实际文档，用户可以转到通过其提供了文档或附件的 Office 365 服务；例如，Office.com、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business 或 Exchange Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1485">To access or export the actual documents, the user can go to the Office 365 service through which the document or attachment was made available (for example, Office.com, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online).</span></span>

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1486">纠正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1486">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1487">用户可以修改 Delve 中的以下信息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1487">Users can modify the following information in Delve:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1488">**个人资料信息：** 用户可以选择“**我**”\>“**更新个人资料**”来更新其信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1488">**Profile information:** A user can select **Me** \> **Update profile** to update their information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1489">根据全局地址列表中组织的设置，用户可能无法修改其所有个人资料信息，例如其姓名或职称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1489">Depending on your organization's settings in the Global Address List, users may not be able to modify all their profile information, such as their name or job title.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1490">**功能设置：** 用户可以选择 Delve 中右上角的齿轮图标，然后选择“**功能设置**”\>来更改所需的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1490">**Feature settings:** A user can select the gear icon in the upper-right corner in Delve, and then select **Feature settings** \> to change the desired settings.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1491">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1491">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p399">要针对组织限制在 Delve 中进行处理，可关闭 Office Graph。在[此处](/sharepoint/delve-for-office-365-admins)了解详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p399">To restrict processing in Delve for your organization, you can turn off the Office Graph. Learn more [here](/sharepoint/delve-for-office-365-admins).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1494">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1494">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1495">用户可删除 Delve 中的以下信息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1495">Users can delete the following information in Delve:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1496">**个人资料信息：** 若要删除个人资料信息，用户可以选择“**我**”\>“**更新个人资料**”，并删除自由格式文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1496">**Profile information:** To delete profile information, a user can select **Me** \> **Update profile** and either delete free-form text.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1497">根据全局地址列表中组织的设置，用户可能无法删除其所有个人资料信息，例如其姓名或职称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1497">Depending on your organization's settings in the Global Address List, users may not be able to delete all their profile information, such as their name or job title.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1498">**文档和电子邮件附件：** 若要删除文档或附件，用户必须存储文档或附件的服务（例如 SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business 或 Exchange Online），并在该处删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1498">**Documents and email attachments:** To delete a document or attachment, users must go to the service where the document or attachment is stored (such as SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, or Exchange Online) and delete the document there.</span></span>

### <a name="myanalytics"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1499">MyAnalytics</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1499">MyAnalytics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1500">MyAnalytics 为用户提供统计信息，帮助他们了解如何安排工作时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1500">MyAnalytics provides statistics to users to help them understand how they spend their time at work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1501">要帮助用户更好地了解通过其个人仪表板呈现的数据以及数据的计算方式，请指导用户转到 [MyAnalytics 个人仪表板](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/use/dashboard-2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1501">To help your users better understand the data that is presented to them in their personal dashboard and how that data is calculated, direct your users to [MyAnalytics personal dashboard](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/use/dashboard-2).</span></span>

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1502">访问和导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1502">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1503">如果组织使用 MyAnalytics，Microsoft 将会生成面向所有用户的见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1503">If your organization uses MyAnalytics, then Microsoft generates insights for all users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1504">所有 MyAnalytics 见解均派生自用户邮箱中的电子邮件和会议标头。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1504">All MyAnalytics insights are derived from email and meeting headers in the user's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1505">用户可以转到 [MyAnalytics 仪表板](https://delve.office.com)，同时登录其 Office 365 帐户，查看生成的有关如何安排工作时间的见解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1505">Users can go to the [MyAnalytics dashboard](https://delve.office.com) while signed in to their Office 365 account to view the insights that are generated about how they spend their time at work.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1506">如果用户想要保存其信息的永久副本，还可对看到的内容进行屏幕截图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1506">They can take screenshots of MyAnalytics insights if they want to have permanent copies of their information.</span></span>

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1507">纠正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1507">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p403">MyAnalytics 生成的所有见解都派生自用户的邮件和日历项目。因此，只需纠正源电子邮件或日历项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p403">All insights generated by MyAnalytics are derived from the user's mail and calendar items. Therefore, there is nothing to rectify other than the source email or calendar items.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1510">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1510">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p404">要针对特定用户限制处理，可让这些用户选择退出 MyAnalytics。请参阅[配置 MyAnalytics 用户设置](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/setup/configure-myanalytics)了解相关方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p404">To restrict processing for a specific user, you can opt them out of MyAnalytics. To see how, see [Configure MyAnalytics user settings](/workplace-analytics/myanalytics/setup/configure-myanalytics).</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1513">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1513">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p405">从 Active Directory 中“硬删除”用户帐户时，将清除所有邮箱内容（包括 MyAnalytics 数据）。有关详细信息，请参阅本指南的[删除用户](#deleting-a-user)部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p405">All mailbox content, including MyAnalytics data, is purged when a user account is "hard-deleted" from Active Directory. For more information, see the [Deleting a user](#deleting-a-user) section in this guide.</span></span>

### <a name="workplace-analytics"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1516">工作区分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1516">Workplace Analytics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p406">使用 Workplace Analytics，组织可使用自己的业务数据扩充 Office 365 数据，以获取有关组织生产效率、协作模式和员工参与的见解。[本文](/workplace-analytics/index-orig)介绍了组织对 Workplace Analytics 所处理数据的掌控以及有权访问该数据的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p406">Workplace Analytics allows organizations to augment Office 365 data with their own business data to gain insights about organizational productivity, collaboration patterns, and employee engagement. [This article](/workplace-analytics/index-orig) explains the control that your organization has over the data that Workplace Analytics processes and who has access to that data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1519">在工作区分析中提供 DSR 方面的协助：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1519">To assist you with DSRs in Workplace Analytics:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p407">确定你的组织是否使用工作区分析。有关详细信息，请参阅[向用户分配许可证](/microsoft-365/admin/manage/assign-licenses-to-users)。如果组织没有使用工作区分析，则没有进一步操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p407">Determine whether your organization is using Workplace Analytics. For more information, see [Assign licenses to users](/microsoft-365/admin/manage/assign-licenses-to-users). If your organization is not using Workplace Analytics, there is no further action.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1523">如果组织在使用 Workplace Analytics，则查看组织中具有 Workplace Analytics 管理员角色的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1523">If your organization is using Workplace Analytics, then see who in your organization has been assigned to the role of Workplace Analytics administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1524">此外，还应确定数据主体的邮箱是否已获得 Workplace Analytics 许可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1524">You should also determine if the data subject's mailbox is licensed for Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1525">如有必要，请求 Workplace Analytics 管理员联系 Microsoft 支持部门处理以下 DSR 请求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1525">If necessary, have your Workplace Analytics administrator contact Microsoft Support in handling the following DSR requests:</span></span> 

#### <a name="access-and-export"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1526">访问和导出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1526">Access and export</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1527">由你创建的 Workplace Analytics 见解报表可能包含也可能不含组织中已获得 Workplace Analytics 许可的用户的个人数据，具体取决于组织用于补充 Office 365 数据的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1527">Workplace Analytics insight reports created by you may or may not contain personal data of users that your organization licensed for Workplace Analytics, depending on the information that your organization used to supplement the Office 365 data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1528">Workplace Analytics 管理员需要审阅这些报表，确定其是否包含用户的个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1528">Your Workplace Analytics administrator needs to review those reports to determine if they contain a user's personal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1529">如果报表包含用户的个人数据，则需要确定是否要向用户提供该报表的副本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1529">If a report does contain a user's personal data, then you need to decide if you want to provide a copy of that report to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1530">Workplace Analytics 允许你导出报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1530">Workplace Analytics allows you to export the report.</span></span> 

#### <a name="rectify"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1531">纠正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1531">Rectify</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1532">如上文所述，Workplace Analytics 结合使用 Office 365 数据以及你提供的组织数据（用于生成你感兴趣的报表）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1532">As explained above, Workplace Analytics uses Office 365 data with the organizational data that you provide to generate reports of interest to you.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1533">无法纠正 Office 365 数据，该数据基于用户的电子邮件和日历活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1533">The Office 365 data can't be rectified; it's based on a user's email and calendar activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1534">但是，可将你拥有的组织数据上传到 Workplace Analytics，生成可纠正的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1534">However, the organizational data that you have uploaded into Workplace Analytics to generate the report can be rectified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1535">要执行此操作，需要更正并上传源数据，并返回报表以生成新的 Workplace Analytics 报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1535">To do this, you need to correct the source data, upload it, and rerun the report to generate a new Workplace Analytics report.</span></span>

#### <a name="restrict"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1536">限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1536">Restrict</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1537">要限制特定用户的处理，可以删除其 工作区分析许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1537">To restrict processing for a specific user, you can remove their Workplace Analytics license.</span></span>

#### <a name="delete"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1538">删除</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1538">Delete</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p411">如果想要从工作区分析报告或一组报告中删除数据主体，可以删除该报告。你负责从用来生成报告的任何组织数据中删除用户，并重新上传数据。当从 Azure Active Directory 中“硬删除”用户帐户时，还将删除有关该用户的所有数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p411">If a data subject would like to be removed from a Workplace Analytics report or set of reports, you can delete the report. It is your responsibility to delete users from any organizational data that you used to generate the report, and reupload the data. All data about the user is removed when a user account is "hard-deleted" from Azure Active Directory.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1542">全局管理员可以采取以下步骤来删除数据主体的个人数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1542">To remove the personal data of a data subject, a global administrator can take the following steps:</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1543">删除数据主体的工作区分析许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1543">Remove the Workplace Analytics license from the data subject.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p412">删除数据主体的 Azure Active Directory (AAD) 项。（有关详细信息，请参阅[删除用户](/azure/active-directory/fundamentals/add-users-azure-active-directory#delete-a-user)。）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p412">Delete the Azure Active Directory (AAD) entry for the data subject. (For more information, see [Delete a user](/azure/active-directory/fundamentals/add-users-azure-active-directory#delete-a-user).)</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p413">联系支持人员，让支持人员提交数据主体权限 (DSR) 用户删除请求的票证。在此票证中使用用户主体名称 (UPN) 标识数据主体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p413">Contact support and have support open a ticket for a Data Subject Rights (DSR) user-delete request. In this ticket, identify the data subject by using their User Principal Name (UPN).</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1548">从公司的 HR 系统导出 HR 数据副本（请参阅[导出数据](/workplace-analytics/setup/prepare-organizational-data)），从该 HR 数据文件删除数据主体的信息，然后将编辑后的 HR 数据文件以 .csv 格式上传到工作区分析（请参阅[上传组织数据](/workplace-analytics/setup/upload-organizational-data)）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1548">Export a copy of the HR data from the company's HR system (see [Export data](/workplace-analytics/setup/prepare-organizational-data)), remove the data subject's information from that HR data file, and then upload the edited HR data file in .csv format into Workplace Analytics (see [Upload organizational data](/workplace-analytics/setup/upload-organizational-data)).</span></span>

## <a name="part-3-responding-to-dsrs-for-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1549">第 3 部分：响应对系统生成日志的 DSR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1549">Part 3: Responding to DSRs for system-generated Logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p414">Microsoft 还为你提供了访问、导出和删除根据 GDPR 中“个人数据”的广泛定义可能被视为个人数据的系统生成日志。根据 GDPR，系统生成日志的示例包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p414">Microsoft also provides you with the ability to access, export, and delete system-generated logs that may be deemed personal under the GDPR's broad definition of "personal data." Examples of system-generated logs that may be deemed personal under GDPR include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1552">产品和服务使用情况数据，例如用户活动日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1552">Product and service usage data such as user activity logs</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1553">用户搜索请求和查询数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1553">User search requests and query data</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1554">作为系统功能一部分的产品和服务所生成的数据以及用户或其他系统的交互</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1554">Data generated by product and services as a product of system functionality and interaction by users or other systems</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p415">不支持限制或纠正系统生成日志中的数据。系统生成日志中的数据构成 Microsoft 云内执行的实际操作和诊断数据，对此类数据的修改将会损坏操作的历史记录，增加诈骗及安全风险。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p415">The ability to restrict or rectify data in system-generated logs is not supported. Data in system-generated logs constitutes factual actions conducted within the Microsoft cloud and diagnostic data, and modifications to such data would compromise the historical record of actions and increase fraud and security risks.</span></span>

### <a name="accessing-and-exporting-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1557">访问和导出系统生成日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1557">Accessing and exporting system-generated logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1558">租户管理员是组织内唯一可以访问与特定用户的 Office 365 服务和应用使用情况相关联的系统生成日志的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1558">The tenant admin is the only person within your organization who can access system-generated logs associated with a particular user's use of Office 365 services and applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1559">为导出请求检索到的数据将以机器可读格式提供，并在允许用户知道数据与哪些服务关联的文件中提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1559">The data retrieved for an export request will be provided in a machine-readable format and will be provided in files that will allow the user to know which services the data is associated with.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1560">如上所述，检索到的数据不包括可能会危及服务安全性或稳定性的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1560">As noted above, the data retrieved will not include data that may compromise the security or stability of the service.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1561">访问和导出系统生成的日志：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1561">To access and export system-generated logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1562">登录到 Azure 门户，然后选择“**所有服务**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1562">Sign in to the Azure portal and select **All services**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1563">在筛选器中键入“策略”，然后选择“**策略**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1563">Type policy into the filter, and then select **Policy**.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1564">在“**策略**”边栏选项卡中，依次选择“**用户策略**”、“**管理用户请求**”和“**添加导出请求**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1564">In the **Policy** blade, select **User privacy**, select **Manage User Requests**, and then select **Add export request**.</span></span>
4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1565">完成“**导出数据请求**”：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1565">Complete the **Export data request**:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1566">**用户**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1566">**User**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1567">键入请求导出的 Azure Active Directory 用户的电子邮件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1567">Type the email address of the Azure Active Directory user that requested the export.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1568">**订阅**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1568">**Subscription**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1569">选择用于报告资源使用情况并计算服务费用的帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1569">Select the account you use to report resource usage and to bill for services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1570">这也是您的 Azure 存储帐户位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1570">This is also the location of your Azure storage account.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1571">**存储帐户**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1571">**Storage account**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1572">选择 Azure 存储的位置 (Blob)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1572">Select the location of your Azure Storage (Blob).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1573">有关详细信息，请参阅 “Microsoft Azure 存储简介 — Blob 存储”一文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1573">For more info, see the Introduction to Microsoft Azure Storage — Blob storage article.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1574">**容器**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1574">**Container**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1575">创建新的（或选择现有的）容器作为存放用户导出的隐私数据的存储位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1575">Create a new (or select an existing) container as the storage location for the user's exported privacy data.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1576">选择“创建”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1576">Select **Create**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1577">导出请求进入 **挂起** 状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1577">The export request goes into **Pending** status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1578">你可以在“**用户隐私**” > “**概述**”边栏选项卡上查看报告状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1578">You can view the report status on the **User privacy** > **Overview blade**.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1579">由于个人数据可能来自多个系统，因此导出过程可能需要一个月才能完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1579">Because personal data can come from multiple systems, it's possible that the export process might take up to one month to complete.</span></span>

### <a name="notify-about-exporting-or-deleting-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1580">通知导出或删除问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1580">Notify about exporting or deleting issues</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1581">如果在从 Azure 门户导出或删除数据时遇到问题，请转到 Azure 门户“**帮助 + 支持**”边栏选项卡，并在“**订阅管理**” > “**其他安全与合规请求**” > “**隐私边栏选项卡和 GDPR 请求**”下提交新票证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1581">If you run into issues while exporting or deleting data from the Azure portal, go to the Azure portal **Help + Support** blade and submit a new ticket under **Subscription Management** > **Other Security and Compliance Request** > **Privacy Blade and GDPR Requests**.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1582">从 Azure 门户导出数据时，将不会导出某些应用程序的系统生成的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1582">When you export data from the Azure portal, system-generated data for a few applications will not be exported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1583">若要导出这些应用程序的数据，请参阅[导出系统生成的日志数据所需的其他步骤](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-system-generated-log-data)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1583">To export data for these applications, see [Additional steps to export system-generated log data](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-system-generated-log-data).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1584">下面概述了如何访问和导出系统生成日志：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1584">The following summarizes accessing and exporting system-generated logs:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1585">**使用 Azure 门户执行的导出请求需要多长时间才能完成请求？**：这取决于若干因素。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1585">**How long does an export request using the Azure portal take to complete a request?**: This can depend on several factors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1586">通常，一到两天内可以完成，但最多可能需要 30 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1586">Usually it should complete in one or two days, but it can take up to 30 days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1587">**输出内容采用什么格式？**：输出内容是结构化的计算机可读文件（如 XML、CSV 或 JSON）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1587">**What format will the output be in?**: The output is structured machine-readable files such as XML, CSV, or JSON.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1588">**谁有权访问 Azure 门户以提交对系统所生成数据的访问请求？**：Office 365 全局管理员有权访问 Azure 门户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1588">**Who has access to Azure portal to submit access requests for system-generated data?**: Office 365 global administrators have access to the Azure portal.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1589">**导出结果将返回哪些数据？**：结果中包含 Microsoft 所存储的系统生成的日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1589">**What data do the export results return?**: The results contain system-generated logs that Microsoft stores.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1590">导出的数据将跨越各种 Microsoft 服务，包括 Office 365、Azure 和 Dynamics。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1590">Exported data spans across various Microsoft services including Office 365, Azure, and Dynamics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1591">结果不包括可能会危及服务安全性或稳定性的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1591">The results do not include data that may compromise the security or stability of the service.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1592">**如何向用户返回数据？**：数据将导出到你组织的 Azure 存储位置；由你组织的管理员来确定他们如何向用户显示/返回此数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1592">**How is data returned to the user?**: Data is exported to your organization's Azure storage location; it's up to admins in your organization to determine how they will show/return this data to users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1593">**系统生成的日志数据的样式是怎样的？**：下面是 JSON 格式的数据的示例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1593">**What will system-generated log data look like?**: Below is an example, the data are in JSON format:</span></span>

    ```JSON
    [{
    "DateTime": "2017-04-28T12:09:29-07:00",
    "AppName": "SharePoint",
    "Action": "OpenFile",
    "IP": "154.192.13.131",
    "DevicePlatform": "Windows 1.0.1607"
    }]
    ```

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1594">还可通过在安全与合规中心搜索 Office 365 审核日志来检索一些最常用的 Microsoft 服务（如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online、Skype for Business、Yammer 和 Office 365 组）的产品和服务使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1594">Product and service usage data for some of Microsoft’s most often-used services, such as Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, Skype for Business, Yammer, and Office 365 Groups can also be retrieved by searching the Office 365 audit log in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1595">有关详细信息，请参阅附录 A 中的[在 DSR 调查中使用 Office 365 审核日志搜索工具](#use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations)。你可能会对使用审核日志感兴趣，因为无法向组织中的其他人（例如合规部主管）分配搜索审核日志并访问此数据的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1595">For more information, see [Use the Office 365 audit log search tool in DSR investigations](#use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations) in Appendix A. Using the audit log may be of interest to you because it's possible to assign permissions to other people in your organization (such as your compliance officer) to search the audit log to access this data.</span></span>

### <a name="deleting-system-generated-logs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1596">删除系统生成日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1596">Deleting system-generated logs</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p426">要删除通过访问请求检索到的系统生成日志，必须从服务中移除用户并永久删除其 Azure Active Directory 帐户。有关永久删除用户的说明，请参阅本指南的[删除用户](#deleting-a-user)部分。请务必注意，永久删除用户帐户操作一旦启动便无法恢复。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p426">To delete system-generated logs retrieved through an access request, you must remove the user from the service and permanently delete their Azure Active Directory account. For instructions about permanently delete a user, see the [Deleting a user section](#deleting-a-user) in this guide. It's important to note that permanently deleting a user account is irreversible once initiated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1600">永久删除用户帐户将在 30 天内从几乎所有 Office 365 服务的系统生成日志中删除用户数据（不包括可能会危及服务安全性和稳定性的数据）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1600">Permanently deleting a user account removes the user's data from system-generated logs, except for data that may compromise the security or stability of the service, for nearly all Office 365 services within 30 days.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1601">此 30 天期限一个例外情况是在 Exchange Online 中永久删除用户帐户所用的时间超过 30 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1601">One exception to this 30-day period is that the permanent deletion of the user account in Exchange Online takes longer than 30 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1602">这是由于 Exchange Online 内容的关键性质，以防止数据意外丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1602">This is due to the critical nature of Exchange Online content and to prevent accidental data loss.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1603">Exchange Online 设计为有意地在永久删除用户帐户后将数据置于保留状态最多 60 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1603">Exchange Online has been engineered to intentionally place data in a holding state for up to 60 days after a user account has been permanently deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1604">要在 30 天的时间范围内永久删除用户 Exchange Online 数据，请在永久删除 Azure Active Directory 中的用户帐户后联系 [Microsoft 支持人员](https://support.microsoft.com/)，请求在计划删除流程之外手动删除用户的 Exchange Online 数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1604">To permanently delete a user's Exchange Online data in a 30-day time frame, permanently delete the user account in Azure Active Directory and then contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/) and request that the user's Exchange Online data be manually removed outside the scheduled delete process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1605">有关详细信息，请参阅本指南前文所述的[删除 Exchange Online 数据](#removing-exchange-online-data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1605">For more information, see [Removing Exchange Online data](#removing-exchange-online-data), which was previously explained in this guide</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p428">删除用户帐户将删除 Yammer 和 Kaizala 的系统生成日志。若要从这些应用程序中删除数据，请参阅以下文章之一：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p428">Deleting a user's account will not remove system-generated logs for Yammer and Kaizala. To remove the data from these applications, see one of the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1608">Yammer - [在 Yammer Enterprise 中管理 GDPR 数据主体请求](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1608">Yammer - [Manage GDPR data subject requests in Yammer Enterprise](/yammer/manage-security-and-compliance/gdpr-requests-in-yammer-enterprise)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1609">Kaizala - [导出或删除 Kaizala 中的用户组织数据](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1609">Kaizala - [Export or delete a user's organizational data in Kaizala](/office365/kaizala/export-or-delete-a-user-s-data)</span></span>

#### <a name="national-clouds"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1610">国家云</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1610">National clouds</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1611">全局 IT 管理员需要执行以下操作以导出以下国家云中的系统生成日志数据：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1611">A global IT admin needs to do the following to export system-generated log data in the following national clouds:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1612">**Office 365 德国版**：按照上面的步骤操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1612">**Office 365 Germany**: Follow the steps above.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1613">**Office 365 美国政府版**：[转到 Office 365 管理门户](https://portal.office365.us)，然后向 Microsoft 支持部门提交请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1613">**Office 365 US Government**: [Go to the Office 365 admin portal](https://portal.office365.us) and submit a request to Microsoft Support.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1614">**由世纪互联运营的 Office 365（中国版）**：[转到由世纪互联运营的 Office 365 的管理门户](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage)，然后转到“**商务**“ > “**订阅**” > “**隐私**” > “**GDPR**”并输入所需的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1614">**Office 365 operated by 21Vianet (China)**: [Go to the Office 365 operated by 21Vianet admin portal](https://portal.partner.microsoftonline.cn/AdminPortal/Home#/homepage) and then go to **Commerce** > **Subscription** > **Privacy** > **GDPR** and enter the required information.</span></span>

## <a name="part-4-additional-resources-to-assist-you-with-dsrs"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1615">第 4 部分：可提供 DSR 协助的其他资源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1615">Part 4: Additional resources to assist you with DSRs</span></span>

### <a name="dsr-guides-for-other-microsoft-enterprise-services"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1616">其他 Microsoft 企业服务的 DSR 指南</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1616">DSR guides for other Microsoft enterprise services</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1617">本指南专用于有关如何使用 Office 365 产品、服务和管理工具查找和处理个人数据以响应 DSR 的主题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1617">This guide is dedicated to the topic of how to find and act on personal data to respond to DSRs when using Office 365 products, services, and administrative tools.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1618">转到 [Microsoft 服务信任门户](https://servicetrust.microsoft.com/)，访问针对其他 Microsoft 企业服务的类似指南。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1618">Go to the [Microsoft Service Trust Portal](https://servicetrust.microsoft.com/) to access similar guides for other Microsoft enterprise services.</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1619">Microsoft 支持</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1619">Microsoft Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p430">“支持数据”是指你和你的用户与 Microsoft 合作，接受与 Office 365 或其他 Microsoft 产品和服务相关的产品支持（例如，意外产品行为疑难解答）时向 Microsoft 提供的数据。其中部分数据可能包含个人数据。有关详细信息，请参阅[符合 GDPR 的 Microsoft 支持部门和专业服务数据主体请求](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-dsr-prof-services)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p430">"Support Data" is the data you and your users provide to Microsoft if your organization or your users engage with Microsoft to receive product support related to Office 365 or other Microsoft products and services (for example, to troubleshoot unexpected product behavior). Some of this data may contain personal data. For more information, see [Microsoft Support and Professional Services Data Subject Requests for the GDPR](/microsoft-365/compliance/gdpr-dsr-prof-services).</span></span>

### <a name="product-and-services-authenticated-with-an-org-id-for-which-microsoft-is-a-data-controller"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1623">通过组织 ID 进行身份验证且由 Microsoft 作为数据控制者的产品和服务</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1623">Product and services authenticated with an Org ID for which Microsoft is a data controller</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1624">本指南的第 1 部分至第 3 部分介绍了由 Microsoft 充当组织的数据处理者，因而租户管理员可使用 DSR 功能的产品和服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1624">Parts 1–3 of this guide covers products and services for which Microsoft is a data processor to your organization, and thus DSR capability is made available to your tenant administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1625">在许多情况下，组织中的用户可能会使用其工作或学校帐户（也称为“Azure Active Directory ID”或“AAD”）登录由 Microsoft 充当数据控制者的 Microsoft 产品和服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1625">There are various circumstances where your organization's users may use their work or school account (also referred to as "Azure Active Directory ID" or "AAD") to sign in to Microsoft products and services for which Microsoft is a data controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1626">对于所有此类产品和服务，用户需要直接向 Microsoft 发出自己的数据主体请求，而 Microsoft 将直接针对该用户满足请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1626">For all such products and services, your users need to initiate their own data subject requests directly to Microsoft and Microsoft will fulfill the requests directly to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1627">涉及存储用户创作内容的产品和服务经过精心设计，使用户能够使用产品的固有功能访问、导出、纠正和删除其用户创作内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1627">By design, products and services involving storage of user-authored content enable users to access, export, rectify, and delete their user-authored content as part of the inherent functionality of the products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1628">相关情景包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1628">Scenarios where this may apply include the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1629">**可选的已连接联机服务：** Microsoft 365 企业应用版为用户提供了一些可选的已连接联机服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1629">**Optional connected online services:** Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise makes certain optional connected online services available to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1630">[此处](https://support.office.com/article/microsoft-s-other-connected-services-92c234f1-dc91-4dc1-925d-6c90fc3816d8)列出了服务和相关用户控件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1630">The list of services and related user controls are listed [here](https://support.office.com/article/microsoft-s-other-connected-services-92c234f1-dc91-4dc1-925d-6c90fc3816d8).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1631">是否允许最终用户使用这些服务取决于你自己。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1631">You can decide whether you would like to allow your end users to use these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1632">有关详细信息，请参阅[管理员如何管理 Microsoft 365 企业应用版中的控制者服务](/DeployOffice/manage-controller-services-office-365-proplus)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1632">For more information, see [How admins can manage controller services in Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise](/DeployOffice/manage-controller-services-office-365-proplus).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1633">如果这些可选服务处理个人数据，Microsoft 是这些服务的数据控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1633">If these optional services process personal data, Microsoft is a data controller for these services.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1634">**用户反馈：** 如果用户选择提供有关 Microsoft 产品和服务的反馈，且此类反馈包含个人数据，则由 Microsoft 作为该反馈的数据控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1634">**User feedback:** If your users elect to provide feedback on Microsoft products and services, Microsoft is a data controller for such feedback to the extent it contains personal data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1635">Microsoft 针对 Microsoft 收集的反馈（包括由 Microsoft 子处理商管理的反馈）实现任何数据主体请求，Microsoft 已指示用户不要在反馈收集过程中包括个人数据时例外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1635">Microsoft fulfills any data subject requests for feedback collected by Microsoft (including feedback managed by Microsoft subprocessors) except in cases where Microsoft has instructed users not to include personal data during the feedback collection process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1636">例外：如果 Microsoft 已指示用户不要在反馈收集过程中包括个人数据，Microsoft 将依赖该指示并假定未提供任何个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1636">Exceptions: If Microsoft has instructed users not to include personal data during the feedback collection process, Microsoft relies on that instruction and will assume that no personal data has been provided.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1637">已创建第三方反馈服务提供程序独立帐户的用户需要直接通过这些服务程序实现其 DSR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1637">Users who have created a separate account with third-party feedback service providers need to fulfill their DSR directly with those providers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1638">**经过工作或学校帐户身份验证的 Windows：** 如果组织已购买 Windows 许可证，而组织中的用户已使用其工作或学校帐户针对组织提供的 Windows 进行了身份验证，则由 Microsoft 作为数据控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1638">**Windows authenticated via work or school account:** If your organization has purchased Windows licenses, and your users authenticate to organization-provided Windows with their work or school account, Microsoft acts as a data controller.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1639">**用户获取的产品或服务：** 如果你允许以个人身份行事的用户获取使用 AAD 进行身份验证的 Microsoft 产品或服务（例如，Microsoft Store 中提供的 Office 加载项或应用程序），Microsoft 可能是数据控制者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1639">**User-acquired products or services:** If you allow your users, acting in their individual capacity, to acquire Microsoft products or services that use AAD for authentication (for example, Office add-ons or applications available in a Microsoft Store), Microsoft may be a data controller.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1640">对于任何此类 Microsoft 产品或服务，用户必须直接联系 Microsoft，才能发出 DSR。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1640">For any such Microsoft products or services, users need to contact Microsoft directly to initiate a DSR.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p435">通过 Azure Active Directory 删除已启用用户后，（旧）用户便无法再登录其工作或学校帐户以前依赖的任何产品或服务。此外，对于 Microsoft 是数据控制者的产品或服务，Microsoft 将无法再对相应用户进行与 DSR 请求相关的身份验证。若要让用户能够对此类服务发出 DSR，请务必指示用户在你删除用户的 AAD 帐户前发出请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p435">If you delete a user as enabled via Azure Active Directory, your (former) user will lose the ability to sign in to any products or services for which he or she formerly relied upon for a work or school account. Additionally, Microsoft will no longer be able to authenticate the user in connection with a DSR request for products or services for which Microsoft is a data controller. If you wish to enable a user to initiate DSRs against such services, it is important you instruct your user to do so before you delete the user's AAD account.</span></span>

### <a name="personal-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1644">个人帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1644">Personal accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1645">如果用户曾使用 Microsoft 帐户（即个人帐户）从 Microsoft 获取由 Microsoft 作为数据控制者的产品和服务并自行使用，则他们将可通过 [Microsoft 隐私仪表板](https://account.microsoft.com/account/privacy)发出 DSR 请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1645">If your users have used Microsoft accounts (that is, personal accounts) to acquire products and services from Microsoft for their own use and for which Microsoft is a data controller, they may initiate DSR requests by using the [Microsoft privacy dashboard](https://account.microsoft.com/account/privacy).</span></span>

### <a name="third-party-products"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1646">第三方产品</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1646">Third-party products</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1647">如果组织或以个人身份行事的用户已从第三方获取了产品或服务，并使用其 Microsoft 工作或学校帐户进行身份验证，则任何数据主体请求都应转到合适的第三方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1647">If your organization, or your users acting in their individual capacity, have acquired products or services from third parties and use their Microsoft work or school account for authentication, any data subject requests should be directed to the applicable third party.</span></span>

## <a name="appendix-a-preparing-for-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1648">附录 A：准备 DSR 调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1648">Appendix A: Preparing for DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1649">为了使用 Office 365 服务帮助组织准备执行 DSR 调查，请考虑以下建议：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1649">To help prepare your organization to undertake DSR investigations using Office 365 services, consider the following recommendations:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1650">在安全与合规中心使用 DSR 电子数据展示事例工具管理 DSR 调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1650">Use the DSR eDiscovery case tool in the Security & Compliance Center to manage DSR investigations</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1651">设置合规性边界，以限制内容搜索范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1651">Set up Compliance Boundaries to limit the scope of Content Searches</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1652">在 DSR 调查中使用审核日志搜索工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1652">Use the audit log search tool in DSR investigations</span></span>

### <a name="use-the-dsr-case-tool-to-manage-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1653">使用 DSR 事例工具管理 DSR 调查</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1653">Use the DSR case tool to manage DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p436">建议在安全与合规中心使用 DSR 事例工具管理 DSR 调查，使用 DSR 事例工具，可：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p436">We recommend that you use the DSR case tool in Security & Compliance Center to manage DSR investigations. By using the DSR case tool, you can:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1656">为每个 DSR 调查创建单独的事例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1656">Create a separate case for each DSR investigation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1657">使用内置搜索查询搜索与特定数据主体相关的所有内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1657">Use the built-in to search for all content related to a specific data subject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1658">创建新事例并开始搜索时，可搜索以下内容位置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1658">When you create a case and start the search, these content locations are searched:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1659">组织中的所有邮箱（包括与所有 Microsoft Teams 和 Microsoft 365 组相关联的邮箱）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1659">All mailboxes in your organization (including the mailboxes associated with all Microsoft Teams and Microsoft 365 Groups)</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1660">组织中的所有 SharePoint Online 网站和 OneDrive for Business 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1660">All SharePoint Online sites and OneDrive for Business accounts in your organization</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1661">组织中的所有 Microsoft Teams 网站和 Microsoft 365 组网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1661">All Microsoft Teams sites and Microsoft 365 group sites in your organization</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1662">Exchange Online 中的所有公用文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1662">All public folders in Exchange Online</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1663">修改默认搜索查询并重新运行搜索，以缩小搜索结果的范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1663">Revise the default search query and rerun the search to narrow the search results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1664">通过将人员添加为事例成员，控制有权访问事例的人员；只有成员才能访问事例，并在安全与合规中心的“DSR 事例”页面上查看其在事例列表中的事例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1664">Control who has access to the case by adding people as members of the case; only members can access the case and are only able to see their cases in the list of cases on the DSR cases page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1665">此外，可为同一事例的不同成员分配不同的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1665">Additionally, you can assign different permissions to different members of the same case.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1666">例如，可以只允许一些成员查看事例和内容搜索结果，而允许其他成员创建搜索和导出搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1666">For example, you could allow some members to only view the case and the results of a Content Search and allow other members to create searches and export search results.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1667">创建导出作业，导出响应 DSR 导出请求的搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1667">Create export jobs to export the search results in response to a DSR export request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1668">可以导出内容搜索返回的所有内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1668">You can export all content returned by the Content Search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1669">还会导出与数据主体相关的其他 Office 365 数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1669">Other Office 365 data related to a data subject is also exported.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1670">创建导出作业，导出响应 DSR 导出请求的搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1670">Create export jobs to export the search results in response to a DSR export request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1671">可以导出内容搜索返回的所有内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1671">You can export all content returned by the Content Search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1672">还可以导出 Office 漫游服务的系统生成日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1672">You can also export system-generated logs for Office Roaming service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1673">在 DSR 调查过程完成时删除案件集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1673">Delete cases when the DSR investigation process is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1674">这会删除所有内容搜索，并导出与案件集关联的作业。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1674">This removes all the content searches and export jobs associated with the case.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1675">若要开始使用 DSR 案件集，请参阅[在安全与合规中心内使用 DSR 案件集工具管理 GDPR 数据主体请求](/microsoft-365/compliance/manage-gdpr-data-subject-requests-with-the-dsr-case-tool)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1675">To get started with using DSR cases, see [Manage GDPR data subject requests with the DSR case tool in the Security & Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/manage-gdpr-data-subject-requests-with-the-dsr-case-tool).</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p442">电子数据展示管理员可查看和管理组织中的所有 DSR 案例。若要详细了解与电子数据展示相关的不同角色，请参阅[向潜在案例成员分配电子数据展示权限](/Office365/SecurityCompliance/assign-ediscovery-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p442">An eDiscovery Administrator can view and manage all DSR cases in your organization. For more information about the different roles related to eDiscovery, see [Assign eDiscovery permissions to potential case members](/Office365/SecurityCompliance/assign-ediscovery-permissions).</span></span>

### <a name="set-up-compliance-boundaries-to-limit-the-scope-of-content-searches"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1678">设置合规性边界，以限制内容搜索范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1678">Set up Compliance Boundaries to limit the scope of Content Searches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p443">合规性边界是通过使用安全与合规中心的搜索权限筛选功能实现的。合规性边界创建组织范围内的逻辑搜索边界，控制/限制 IT 管理员或合规部主管可以搜索的内容位置（例如 Exchange Online 邮箱和 SharePoint Online 网站）。合规性边界适用于需要服从地理边界的跨国组织、需要分散不同机构的政府组织和需要分为多个业务部门的企业组织。对于所有这些情景，都可在 DSR 调查中使用合规性边界来限制涉及调查的人员可搜索的邮箱和网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p443">Compliance Boundaries are implemented by using the search permissions filtering functionality in the Security & Compliance Center. Compliance Boundaries create logical search boundaries within an organization that control/limit which content locations (for example Exchange Online mailboxes and SharePoint Online sites) that an IT admin or compliance officer can search. Compliance Boundaries are useful for multi-national organizations that need to respect geographical boundaries, governmental organizations that need to separate different agencies, and business organizations that segregated into business unit or department. For all these scenarios, Compliance Boundaries can be used in DSR investigations to limit which mailboxes and sites can be searched by people involved in the investigation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1683">可结合使用合规性边界和电子数据展示事例，将可在调查中搜索的内容位置限制为机构或业务部门内的内容位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1683">You can use Compliance Boundaries together with eDiscovery cases to limit the content locations that can be searched in an investigation to those locations only within the agency or business unit.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1684">下面概括介绍了如何针对 DSR 调查实现合规性边界（结合使用电子数据展示事例）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1684">Here's a high-level overview of how to implement Compliance Boundaries (together with eDiscovery cases) for DSR investigations.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1685">确定组织中将指定为合规性边界的机构。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1685">Determine the agencies in your organization that will be designated as a compliance boundary.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p444">确定 Azure Active Directory 中将用于定义合规性边界的用户对象属性。例如，可能会选择国家/地区、国家/地区代码或部门属性，以便你在下一步中创建的管理员角色组的成员仅可搜索具有该特定属性值的用户的内容位置。可通过此方法限制特定机构中可搜索内容的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p444">Determine which user object attribute in Azure Active Directory will be used to define the compliance boundary. For example, you might choose the Country, CountryCode, or Department attribute, so that members of the admin role group that you create in the next step can only search the content locations of the users that have a specific value for that attribute. This is how you limit who can search for content in a specific agency.</span></span>

   > [!NOTE]
   > <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1689">目前，对于 OneDrive for Business，必须执行额外的步骤，并请求 Microsoft 支持部门将属性同步到 OneDrive for Business 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1689">Currently, you must perform an additional step for OneDrive for Business and file a Microsoft Support request to have the attribute synchronized to OneDrive for Business accounts.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p445">在安全与合规中心为每个合规性边界创建管理员角色组。建议通过复制内置电子数据展示管理者角色组，然后根据需要删除任何角色来创建这些角色组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p445">Create an admin role group in the Security & Compliance Center for each compliance boundary. We recommend that you create these role groups by copying the built-in eDiscovery Manager role group and then removing any roles as necessary.</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1692">以电子数据展示管理者的身份向每个特定角色组添加成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1692">Add members to each of the specific role groups as eDiscovery Mangers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1693">成员是负责调查和响应 DSR 人员，通常包括 IT 管理员、数据隐私部主管、合规性管理员和人力资源代表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1693">Members are the people responsible for investigating and responding to DSRs, and will typically consist of IT admins, data privacy officers, compliance managers, and human resource representatives.</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1694">为每个合规性边界创建搜索权限筛选器，以便对应管理员角色组中的成员可仅搜索机构/合规性边界内的用户的邮箱和网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1694">Create a search permissions filter for each compliance boundary so that the members of the corresponding admin role group can only search mailboxes and sites for users within that agency/compliance boundary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1695">使用搜索权限筛选器，对应角色组的成员可仅搜索对应于机构/合规性边界的具有用户对象属性值的内容位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1695">The search permissions filter allows members of the corresponding role group to search only the content locations with user object attribute value that corresponds to the agency/compliance boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1696">有关分步说明，请参阅[在 Office 365 中为电子数据展示调查设置合规性边界](/microsoft-365/compliance/set-up-compliance-boundaries)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1696">For step-by-step instructions, see [Set up compliance boundaries for eDiscovery investigations in Office 365](/microsoft-365/compliance/set-up-compliance-boundaries).</span></span>

### <a name="use-the-audit-log-search-tool-in-dsr-investigations"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1697">在 DSR 调查中使用审核日志搜索工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1697">Use the audit log search tool in DSR investigations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-p448">IT 管理员可使用安全与合规中心的审核日志搜索工具识别用户已创建、访问、更改或删除的文档、文件和其他 Office 365 资源。搜索此类活动有助于进行 DSR 调查。例如，在 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中，可在用户执行以下活动时记录审核事件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-p448">IT admins can use the audit log search tool in the Security & Compliance Center to identity documents, files, and other Office 365 resources that users have created, accessed, changed, or deleted. Searching for this kind activity can be useful in DSR investigations. For example, in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business, auditing events are logged when users perform these activities:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1701">访问文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1701">Accessed a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1702">修改文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1702">Modified a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1703">移动文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1703">Moved a file</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1704">上传或下载文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1704">Uploaded or downloaded a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1705">可以针对特定活动、活动类型、特定用户执行的活动和其他搜索条件搜索审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1705">You can search the audit log for specific activities, types of activities, activities performed by a specific user, and other search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1706">除了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 活动外，还可搜索 Flow、Power BI 和 Microsoft Teams 中的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1706">In addition to SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business activities, you can also search for activities in Flow, Power BI, and Microsoft Teams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1707">审核记录可保留 90 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1707">Auditing records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1708">因此，无法立即搜索超过 90 天前发生的用户活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1708">Therefore, you won't be able to search for user activities that occurred more than 90 days ago.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1709">有关审核活动的完整列表以及搜索审核日志的方法，请参阅[在安全与合规中心搜索审核日志](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1709">For a complete list of audited activities and how to search the audit log, see [Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center](/microsoft-365/compliance/search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance).</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1710">要避开上文讨论的 90 天的限制，并保留组织审核记录的运行历史记录，可以定期（例如每 30 天）导出所有活动，从而获得组织审核记录的连续记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1710">To work around the 90-day limitation discussed above and maintain a running history of your organization's auditing records, you could export all activities on a recurring schedule (for example, every 30 days) to have a continuous record of your organization's auditing records.</span></span>

## <a name="appendix-b-change-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1711">附录 B：更改日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1711">Appendix B: Change log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6f8a5-1712">下表列出了 Office 365 DSR 指南自 2018 年 5 月 25 日首次发布以来的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6f8a5-1712">The following table lists the changes to the Office 365 DSR guide since its initial publication on May 25, 2018.</span></span>
